SV_1.1ab–1.4ab	viśuddha jñāna dehāya tri vedī divya cakṣuṣe śreyaḥ prāpti nimittāya namaḥ soma ardha dhāriṇe abhivandya gurūn ādau śiṣya dhī padminī ravīn tad prasādāt kariṣye aham mīmāṃsā śloka vārttikam tad vidvāṃsaḥ anugṛhṇantu citta śrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ santaḥ praṇayi vākyāni gṛhṇanti hi anasūyavaḥ na ca atra ativa kartavyam doṣa dṛṣṭi param manaḥ 
SV_1.4cd–1.7cd	 doṣaḥ hi avidyamānaḥ api tad cittānām prakāśate kutas vā gṛhṇate doṣam sūrayaḥ madvidha uktiṣu na iṣyate yaḥ para sthaḥ api sa svayam gṛhyate katham nirdoṣa tva eka vākya tvam kva vā lokasya dṛśyate sa apavādāḥ yatas ke cit mokṣa svargau api prati āgama pravaṇaḥ ca aham na apavādyaḥ skhaliteṣu api apodyate na hi sat vartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣu api apodyate 
SV_1.8ab–1.11ab	 yathā kathan cit ārabdhā trayī mārga anusāriṇī vāc vṛttiḥ alpa sārā api śraddadhānasya śobhate mīmāṃsā śāstra tejobhiḥ viśeṣeṇa uj jvalīkṛte veda artha jñāna ratne me tṛṣṇā atīva vijṛmbhate prāyena eva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā tām āstika pathe kartum ayam yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ mayā atha atas dharma jijñāsā sūtram ādyam idam kṛtam 
SV_1.11cd–1.14cd	 dharma ākhyam viṣayam vaktum mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam sarvasya eva hi śāstrasya karmaṇaḥ vā api kasya cit yāvat prayojanam na uktam tāvat tat kena gṛhyate mīmāṃsā ākhyā tu vidyā iyam bahu vidyā antara āśritā na śuśrūṣayitum śkyā prāc anuktvā prayojanam vidyā antareṣu na api etat yadi abhīṣṭam prayojanam anartha prāpaṇam tāvat tebhyaḥ na āśaṅkyate kva cit 
SV_1.15ab–1.18ab	 mīmāṃsāyām tu iha ajñāte durjñāte vā avivekataḥ nyāya mārge mahān doṣaḥ iti yatna upacarya tā tasmāt prayojanam pūrvam uktam sūtra kṛtā svayam yat svena uktam vadeyuḥ tat bhāṣya kāra ādayaḥ katham siddhārtham jñāta sambandham śrotum śrotā pravartate śāstra ādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ sa prayojanaḥ śāstram prayojanam ca eva sambandhasya āśrayau ubhau 
SV_1.18cd–1.21cd	 tad ukti antargataḥ tasmāt bhinnaḥ na uktaḥ prayojanāt siddhiḥ śrotṛ pravṛttīnām sambandha kathanāt yatas tasmāt sarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvam ucyate yāvat prayojanena asya sambandhaḥ na abhidhīyate asambaddha pralāpi tvāt bhavet tāvat asaṃgatiḥ iha tu ākṣipya sambandham bhāṣyaḥ eva abhihdhāsyate dharma prasiddhi asiddhibhyām tasmāt na anyaḥ abhidhīyate 
SV_1.22ab–1.25ab	 na ca api atra atha śabdena śāstra sambandhaḥ ucyate sambandham kriyayoḥ hi eṣa brūte śāstrāt ca te pṛthak yaḥ api ayam śāstra sambandhaḥ varṇyate kaiḥ cit āditas kriyā ānantarya rūpaḥ vā guru parva kramaḥ api vā sat asat bhāvayoḥ tasya viśeṣaḥ na upalabhyate śrotu vidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstra gocare tasmāt vyākhyā aṅgam icchadbhiḥ sa hetuḥ sa prayojanaḥ 
SV_1.25cd–1.28cd	 śāstra avatāra sambandhaḥ vācyaḥ na anyaḥ tu niṣphalaḥ loke ityādi bhāṣyasya ṣaṭ arthān sampracakṣate bhāṣya kāra anusāreṇa prayuktasya āditas pṛthak sarva vyākhyām upālambham pratyākhyānam tathā pare parisaṃkhyāḥ tutī kecitha śabdasya dūṣaṇam sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtra vyākhyā dvidhā matā viśiṣṭā pratisūtram yā sarva arthā tu iyam ucyate 
SV_1.29ab–1.32ab	 pravṛttiḥ tu padeṣu eva nivṛttiḥ sūtra saṃśrayāḥ veda vākya aviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt tena eṣām iti sūtrāṇām pārārthye sati api grahaḥ eva śabdaḥ alpa vācya tvāt asya āvṛttau tu gauravam prasiddha tvāt avācyam ced na doṣaḥ puṅgirām ayam vyākhyā aṅgatva abhimānena yaḥ adhyāhāra ādi apekṣate 
SV_1.32cd–1.35cd	 sva saṃjñām vā api tasya idam śāstra rūpam nirūpyate vṛti antareṣu keṣān cit laukika artha vyatikramaḥ śabdānām dṛśyate teṣam upālambhaḥ ayam ucyate atha atas iti ayam loke na ānantarye prayujyate tasmāt tādarthyam etasya paribhāṣā ādibhiḥ bhavet prasiddha hāniḥ śabdānām aprasiddhe ca kalpanā na kāryā vṛtti kāreṇa sati siddhārtha sambhave 
SV_1.36ab–1.39ab	 sūtra arthe kliśyataḥ ca evam dūre veda artha nirṇayaḥ tatra yatnasya bhāra tvam vaktṛ śrotroḥ prasajyate na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanā artha paratvataḥ yat tasya parihāraḥ ayam pratyākhyānena ca ucyate prayāsaḥ veda vākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣu anena kim phalavat tva aphala tvābhyām ebhiḥ karaṇa sammataiḥ codanā arthaḥ upetavyaḥ na ubhayam yatna gauravāt 
SV_1.39cd–1.42cd	 padārthānām prasiddha tvāt vyākhyeyam na avaśiṣyate evaṃśabda ādikaḥ granthaḥ pakṣe ca asmin samarthyate pada= cheda dādi abhāvena pratyākhyāna matiḥ tu iyam brabīti eva hi sūtra artham atirikta ādi ca iṣyate nanu aśaktam idam sūtram samyak sūtritam iti api sūtre ca āgamaka tva ādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate na ca upāya anabhijñena śakya upeya avadhāraṇā 
SV_1.43ab–1.45cd	 na anyatas veda vidbhyaḥ ca sūtravṛtti kriyā iṣyate pratyākhyānasya hetuḥ ca padārthānām prasiddha tā yoktā sā veda vākyānam tulya artha tvāt nivārayet vākya arthe tatra sandehāt vyākhyānam ced pravartate sūtreṣu api samāna tvāt pratyākhyānam na yujyate na vyākhyātavyam iti evam pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati 
SV_1.46ab–1.49ab	 duṣṭa vyākhyā niṣedhena tad apetā na vāryate asya dṛṣṭa viruddha tvāt phalgu tvāt ca api parvayoḥ madhyame ca ati daurjanyāt parisaṃkhyā eva yujyate vaidikam jaiminīyam ca yatra vākyam virudhyate yathā śruta gṛhīte arthe tatra idam upadiśyate adhyāhāra ādibhiḥ sūtram vaidikam tu yathāśrutam na iyam virodhe anyonyasya vaidikānām bhavantu te 
SV_1.49cd–1.52cd	 yathā dharma avabodhasya pramāṇam vaidikam vacaḥ tad artha nirṇaye hetuḥ jaiminīyam tathā eva naḥ vākya sāmarthya tulya tvāt tathā padatad arthayoḥ adhyāhāra ādibhiḥ muktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate asambhavāt avaśyam yā virodhe anyatarasya tu anyāyi akalpanā sā api vikalpena prasajyate prāthamyena avaruddha tvāt upāya vaśataḥ atha vā 
SV_1.53ab–1.56ab	 yathā aśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyām bādheta codanām tena veda aviruddhasya sati sambhavaḥ iti ayam vidhīyate arthaḥ śeṣam tu yathāprāptam anūdyate śeṣa bhājām bhavet lopaḥ iti adhyāhāra kalpanā viprakarṣāt paśoḥ ca iti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate padena vyavadhānam tu loke saṃniyamāt iti sūtreṇa vyavadhānam tu pāna vyāpadi kalpitam 
SV_1.56cd–1.59cd	 paśu sāmānya vidhi ādau sūtram eva anyathā kṛtam agnayaḥ ca sva kāla tvāt deya dharma apayātanam vyākhyānam vākya bhedena guṇa kalpāḥ tu amī kṛtāḥ autpattikaḥ tu gavyasya tathā uṣṇikkakubhoḥ iti darśanāt ca viśeṣasya tathā abhyudayaḥ iti api sūtrakāra praśaṃsā vā lokaḥ ityādinā ucyate prasiddhaiḥ abhidhānāt dhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yatas 
SV_1.60ab–1.62cd	 bhavitavyam tu tena iti prāk asmāt eka vākyatā veda adhyayana vākyāt vā tena atha iti asya dūṣaṇam prasiddha artha padaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtraiḥ veda artha nirṇayaḥ na ca saḥ asti atha śabdasya vinā te pūrva karmaṇā prasiddha artham padam yuktam tat ca na asti iti dūṣaṇam prasiddhaḥ api atha śabda ādeḥ kiṃpadārthaḥ atra varṇyate 
SV_1.63ab–1.66ab	 pradarśana artham iti eke ke cit nānā artha vācinaḥ samudāyāt avacchidya bhava dāsena kalpitāt śaktitas avayavam ca eva varṇayanti aṣṭama ādi vat na ca atra codanā vyākhyā gauravam tatra coditam yat vā ākṣepaḥ yathā uktasya vṛtta abhāvāt asambhavāt yadi loka prasiddha artha grahaṇam kriyate pade sa na asti atra atha śabdasya iti adhyāhāra ādi kalpanam 
SV_1.66cd–1.69cd	 veda adhyayana vṛtta tvam snānasya utkarṣa kalpanā na avyākhyāte atha śabda arthe jñāyate tena varṇyate anarthake atha vā anya arthe prasiddhiḥ bādhyate dhruvam tasmāt śruta artha siddhi artham vṛttam kim api gamyate viśiṣṭa liṅga vijñānāt viśiṣṭe liṅgi nīkṣite sūtreṇa asambhavam matvā na etat iti abravīt paraḥ ānantarya upadeśena tad dṛṣṭa artha tayā api ca 
SV_1.70ab–1.73ab	 veda adhyayanam ākṣiptam kim asūtrita codanā yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā na eva upapadyate tat ā ānantaryam uktam hi dṛṣṭa artham avakalpate kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamāt yasya kasya cit kriyeta anantarā eva iti vyartham tad upadeśanam saṅkalpa ādibhiḥ api eṣā vinā satyam na sidhyati sādhāraṇyāt tu te api atra na upadeśyāḥ kathan canaḥ 
SV_1.73cd–1.76cd	 tasmāt dharma bubhutsāyām asādhāraṇa kāraṇam nirvṛttam sūtrakāreṣṭam tat ca na ākhyayanāt ṛte anyasya api iti anena eva veda pāṭhe prabādhite prāk api iti hi vaktavyam tatra api anyasya sambhavāt pūrveṇa eva hi labdha arthe tādṛśīm tu iti anena kim vakṣyamāṇam anālocya sambhavet paricodanā na tāvat sādhyate adya api codanā dharma sādhanam 
SV_1.77ab–1.80ab	 iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ dharma mātra abhidhānāt dhi buddha ādi vacanāni api paṭhitvā dharma jijñāsā iti anyasya api iti codanā yat vā bhavatu nāma īdṛś sūtram vedam adhītya tu jijñāsā anantaram kāryā iti atra api dvayam īpsitam na anadhītya na ca api anyat kṛtvā iti etat na labhyate vakṣyamāṇa vacaḥ bhaṅgyoḥ vākya bheda prasaṅgataḥ 
SV_1.80cd–1.83cd	 adhītya eva iti hi vidhau snāna ādeḥ api anantarā bhavet dharmasya jijñāsā na anantarya vidhiḥ tadā ānantarya vidhāne tu yāḥ veda adhyayane kṛte iti evam anuvāda tvāt prāk api eṣā prasajyate buddha vākya ādi pāṭhasya tādṛśīm tu iti apākriyā prāk api iti ca ca udyasya sāmarthyāt veda lābhataḥ na eva etayoḥ vacaḥ bhaṅgyoḥ ekaḥ api arthaḥ vidhīyate 
SV_1.84ab–1.87ab	 api ca iti ādikena uktam kin tu iti etat vidhīyate ānantaryam parastāt ca na api śiṃṣmaḥ iti iha tu ke cit adhyāharanti asya sūtrasya anya paratvataḥ na vāryate anadhīta tvam na ānantaryam vidhīyate sāmarthya asiddhi adṛṣṭa artha prasaṅgāt tena lakṣaṇā ānantarī avacā uvyaktiḥ āśritā eva atra lakṣyate śruta artham tu aparityajya lakṣaṇa arthaḥ vidhīyate 
SV_1.87cd–1.90cd	 pratītā dharma jiñāsā veda adhyāyāt anantarā tad kālasya avaruddha tvāt snāna abhāvam hi lakṣayet virodhaḥ yugapad prāpteḥ daurbalyam veda bādhanāt snānasya tena bādhaḥ syāt dharma jijñāsayā balāt dṛṣṭa artha tva ādi saṃyuktam vākyam lakṣaṇayā tu iti punaruktyā gata artha tvāt tyaktam kaiḥ cit tat ucyate yadi api asya bhavet vācyam ānantaryam asaṃśayam 
SV_1.91ab–1.94ab	 tathā api pūrva tā mātram lakṣayet avirodhataḥ grantha grahaṇa mātre ca kṛte snānam virudhyate adhītya iti adhigamya iti vyākhyāne tu avirodhitā yaḥ tu evam avirodhi tvam kurvan= āplavanam vadet adṣṭāya atha vā api anyaḥ saṃskāram tasya ca uttaram iha āsnān ādi niyamaḥ yaḥ kṛtaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ avidhi tvam anāśritya saḥ avasānam apekṣate 
SV_1.94cd–1.97cd	 tatas apekṣā vaśāt snānam asnāna ādi nivartanam virodha sāhacaryābhyām dṛṣṭa artha tvena lakṣayet tasmāt adhyayana snāna jijñāsā krama vācinām dṛṣṭa artha tvāya śabdānām evam vyākhyeyam āśritāḥ snātvā jijñāsamānaḥ api nanu vedam na bādhate tena avirodhi tā tasya iti evam vadate uttaram yathā eva adhyayanāt snānam smaryate samanantaram 
SV_1.98ab–1.101ab	 tathā tatas paraḥ api anyaḥ padārthaḥ anyaḥ paraḥ tatas tatas ca avaśya kartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit yogya tvāt āgate kāle prāthamyāt snāna bādhanam saḥ ayam pāṭha kramasya arthāt bādhaḥ iti avagamyate guṇa pradhānayoḥ vā api virodhāt guṇa bādhanam snāna upalakṣitā ca atra nivṛttiḥ guru veśmanaḥ virodhi tvena bādhyeta na tu madhu ādi bhakṣaṇam 
SV_1.101cd–1.104cd	 tasmāt guru kule tiṣṭhan madhu māṃsa ādi avarjayan jijñāseta aviruddha tvāt dharmam iti avagamyate guru geha nivṛtti aṃśaḥ yāvat ca na samāpyate tāvat sakala vāci tvāt na snānam paryavasyati guru gehāt anāvṛttaḥ snātakaḥ hi na kathyate tad paratva vidhānāt ca na tāvat dāra saṅgrahaḥ vyākhyāya kīrtitā ca atra snāyāt iti punar smṛtiḥ 
SV_1.105ab–1.108ab	 sma avartiṣṭa mā ityādi smṛteḥ yadi api anantaram viparīta artham iti asmāt tad vākyāt apanīyate athaśabdena yaḥ bādhaḥ purastāt upavarṇitaḥ tanmātrasya eva bādhaḥ atra dṛṣṭa artha tvāt pradarśitaḥ smṛti prāptam idānīm tu madhu māṃsa ādya varjanam pratiṣedhan adṛṣṭa artham sūtra kāraḥ na śobhate nivṛttya guru gehāt ca jijñāsā arthaḥ punar bhavet 
SV_1.108cd–1.111cd	 praveśaḥ saḥ api adṛṣṭa arthaḥ iti na eva iha sūtritaḥ nirgamaḥ hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭa arthaḥ guru veśmanaḥ smaryate tasya na arthaḥ syāt akṛtārthasya nirgame atha śabda prasiddhyā eva veda grahaṇa hetu tā ānantarya upadeśi tvāt atas śabdena kim punar yogya tvam atha śabdena yadi api pratipāditam tat eva hetuḥ atra iti na atas śabdāt vinā bhavet 
SV_1.112ab–1.115ab	 lakṣaṇam puruṣasya eva tadā tat dhi prasajyate jijñāsāyāḥ ca hetu tve phala artha tva ādi sambhavet atas śabda gṛhītam vā tatra adhyayanam āśritam hetau= akathyamāne hi maṅgala ādi api asau vadet snāna bādhasya vā hetuḥ atas iti ucyate punar yogyasya adhīta veda tvāt na avasthātum hi labhyate san vācyecśā antaram karma jñānam vyāpnoti tāvatā 
SV_1.115cd–1.118cd	 jñāna upasarjanā sā eva na tu vidhi ādi gamyate iṣeḥ tu karma bāhyaḥ syāt dharmaḥ sā vā atha vā dvayam samāna kartṛka tvam tu tumunā uktam liṅā vidhiḥ evam viṣaya nānā tvāt na kā cit punar ukta tā sūtrita icchā abhinirvṛttyai dvitīya icchā atra sūtritāḥ prakṛtyā vikṛtiḥ yasmāt caturthī antā samasyate tādarthye yūpa dāru ādau tena asmin asamāsa tā 
SV_1.119ab–1.122ab	 sa hi tasya iti anena uktaḥ dharmasya iti eṣa vigrahaḥ dharmāya iti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛttā iti kathyate prāpnoti atra caturthī eva viśeṣaḥ ced vivakṣitaḥ sāmānyasya vivakṣāyām tādṛśam kathyate katham sambandha mātre eva eṣā ṣaṣṭhī utpannā tathā api tu viśeṣa niṣṭhatā tasyāḥ bhāṣya kāreṇa varṇyate sādhana ābhāsa tā ca atra pūrva pakṣa artha gocarā 
SV_1.122cd–1.128cd	 anya sādhanam anyasya sādhana ābhāsaḥ ucyate kratu artham puruṣa arthasya tad artham ca kratoḥ iti śeṣa lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ ca kṛtsna śāstra vivakṣayā prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddha tvāt tu na iṣyate aprasiddhaḥ tu aśakya tvāt natarām iti atas abravīt jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayāt dharmaḥ śreyaskara tayā api ca asandigdhaḥ hi ajijñāsyaḥ yaḥ vā syāt niṣprayojanaḥ sva rūpa ādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate pūrvam pramāṇa rūpābhyām pādena ādyasya nirṇayaḥ sthite veda pramāṇa tve punar vākya artha nirṇaye matiḥ bahu vidām puṃsām saṃśayāt na upajāyate ke cit āhuḥ asau arthaḥ ke cit na asau ayam tu iti tad nirṇaya artham api etat param śāstram praṇīyate 
SV_2.1ab–2.3cd	 dharme sāmānyatas siddhe pramāṇam codanā ucyate svarūpa ādeḥ tatas siddhaḥ svarūpam ca iha sūtryate dvayam ekena sūtreṇa śruti arthābhyām nirūpyate svarūpe api hi tasya ukte pramāṇam kathyate arthataḥ kim ādi apekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayaḥ vidhau tena pravartakam vākyam śāstre asmin codanā ucyate 
SV_2.4ab–2.7ab	 codanā eva pramāṇam ca iti etat dharme avadhāritam sa ākāṅkṣam iti manvānaḥ yukti leśam dvaye aspṛśat sambhāvyate pramāṇa tvam śabdasya evaṃvidheṣu api indriya ādeḥ asāmarthyam vakṣyamāṇa madīdiśat atyanta asati api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi tena utsarge sthite tasya doṣa abhāvāt pramāṇa tā codanā iti abravīt ca atra śabda mātra vivakṣayā 
SV_2.7cd–2.10cd	 na hi bhūta ādi viṣayaḥ kaḥ cit asti vidhāyakaḥ indriya ādi vyudāsena śabdaḥ yāvat na sādhyate tāvat ca tad viśeṣasya kutas vā avasaraḥ bhavet nimitta mātram vocyeta pramāṇam ca iha lakṣaṇam pramāṇam tu api śabdaḥ vā tat jñānam vā nirūpyate padārthaḥ tad matiḥ vā syāt vākya artha adhigamaḥ api vā pūrveṣām tu pramāṇa tve phala tvam tasya gamyate 
SV_2.11ab–2.14ab	 jñāne lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ ayam yadi nāma prayujyate codanoktiḥ tadā kāryam tat kāryam ca api lakṣayet nimitta mātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhya vṛttayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt codanā lakṣaṇa tvayoḥ dravya kriyā guṇa ādīnām dharma tvam sthāpayiṣyate teṣām aindriyaka tve api na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā śreyaḥ sādhana tā hi eṣām nityam vedāt pratīyate 
SV_2.14cd–2.17cd	 tādrūpyeṇa ca dharma tvam tasmāt na indriya gocaraḥ pradarśana artham atra uktam indriyam sūtra kāra vat na anyat kiñ ca iti vā ācchedaḥ sāmānya arthaḥ prayujyate tat asāmarthya siddhyai ca punar indriya kīrtanam kiñ ca iti madhyam acchedaḥ hetu praśne prayujyate yadi api tu anumānasya api evamādau samartha tā vinā sambandha bodhena na tu tasya udbhavaḥ kva cit 
SV_2.18ab–2.20cd	 na sāmānya viśeṣābhyām dharma sambandha darśanam liṅgasya kasya cit siddham yena syāt anumāna tā nanu śabdaḥ api sambandha bodhān na ṛte pravarttate padam tat na ca tad vācyaḥ dharmaḥ vākya arthaḥ eva saḥ vākyasya avācaka tvam ca padārthānām ca hetu tā sambandhasya anapekṣāṇām vākya arthe sthāpayiṣyate 
SV_2.21ab–2.24ab	 nitya tva ādeḥ asiddha tvāt abhyupetya ucyate atha vā sutarām apramāṇa tvam vaktṛ prāmāṇya varjanāt pramāṇa antara dṛṣṭam hi śabdaḥ artham prāpayet sadā smṛti vat ca svayam tasya prāmāṇyam na upapadyate nūnam tatra anubhūtaḥ asau= iti āpta ukti nibandhanā buddhiḥ sākṣāt adṛṣṭe api yukta arthe puruṣa uktitaḥ na ātmīyāt anyadīyāt vā pratyakṣa ādeḥ vinā kva cit 
SV_2.24cd–2.27cd	 vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāt codanāsu api tena sati api vijñāne pratijña ādeḥ yathā eva hi svātantryāt na pramāṇa tvam tathā vede api dṛśyatām svarga yāga ādi sambandha viṣayā codanā mṛṣā pratyakṣa ādyagata artha tva ādīdṛś buddha ādi vākya vat yat vā āptena apraṇīta tvāt bāla unmatta ādi vākya vat vyoma ādi vat ca nitya tvāt prāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ 
SV_2.28ab–2.31ab	 yadi vā puruṣa adhīna prāmāṇyāḥ sarva codanāḥ svatas vā na pramāṇam syuḥ vākya tvāt puruṣokti vat prāmāṇyam vā nara apekṣam sarva śabdeṣu gamyatām śabdaiḥ sambandhyamāna tvāt apramāṇyam tathā eva hi na syāt vaktṛ guṇānām ced vacaḥ prāmāṇya hetu tā tad doṣaiḥ apramāṇa tvam kim iti asya bhaviṣyati evam sthite tu vedasya sati vā asati vā nare 
SV_2.31cd–2.34ab	 prāmāṇyam durlabham matvā nanu iti etat acūcudat tatra vipratiṣiddha tvam buddha vākye api yujyate tatas api pratyaya utpatteḥ tasmāt jāti uttaram tu idam sarva vijñāna viṣayam idam tāvat parīkṣyatām pramāṇa tva apramāṇa tve svatas kim paratas atha vā svatas asatām asādhya tvāt ke cit āhuḥ dvayam svatas 
SV_2.34cd–2.37cd	 apare kāraṇa utpanna guṇa doṣa avadhāraṇāt svatas tāvat dvayam na asti virodhāt paratas na ca niḥsvabhāva tvam evam hi jñāna rūpe prasajyate katham hi anya anapekṣasya viparīta ātma sambhavaḥ kimātmakam bhavet tat ca svabhāva dvaya varjitam vijñāna vyakti bhedena bhavet ced aviruddha tā tathā api anya anapekṣa tve kim kva iti na nirūpyate 
SV_2.38ab–2.41ab	 tasmāt svābhāvikam teṣām apramāṇa tvam iṣyatām prāmāṇyan ca para apekṣam atra nyāyaḥ abhidhīyate aprāmānyam avastu tvāt na syāt kāraṇa doṣataḥ vastu tvāt tu guṇaiḥ teṣām prāmāṇyam upajanyate prāmāṇyam hi yadā utsargāt tad abhāvaḥ atha kṛtrimaḥ tadā svapna ādi bodhe api prāmāṇyam kena vāryate mad pakṣe kāraṇa abhāvāt prāmānyam na upajāyate 
SV_2.41cd–2.44cd	 hetumat tva prasaṅgaḥ atas na bhaviṣyati avastunaḥ indriya ādi guṇāḥ ca asya kāraṇam tat asat dvidhā duṣṭa tvāt indriya ādīnām abhāve anyatamasya vā atas eva ca vaḥ bhrāntiḥ doṣaiḥ mithyā tva dhīḥ iti tad vyāpteḥ tu guṇa abhāvaḥ tad kṛtā hi apramāṇa tā tasmāt kāraṇa śuddha tvam jñāna prāmāṇya kāraṇam svabhāvataḥ apramāṇa tvam tad abhāvena lakṣyate 
SV_2.45ab–2.48ab	 anvaya vyatirekābhyām aprāmāṇyam na doṣataḥ na ajñāne dṛśyate hi etad kāraṇa abhāva hetuke tatas ca puruṣa abhāvāt sati vā śuddhi asambhavāt nirmūla tvāt pramāṇa tvam codanāyām na yujyate svatas sarva pramāṇānām prāmāṇyam iti gamyatām na hi svatas asatī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate ātma lābhe ca bhāvānām kāraṇa apekṣatā bhavet 
SV_2.48cd–2.51cd	 labdha ātmanām sva kāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayam eva tu jāte api yadi vijñāne tāvat na arthaḥ avadhāryate yāvat kāraṇa śuddha tvam na pramāṇa antarāt bhavet tatra jñāna antara utpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇa antarāt yāvat dhi na paricchinnā śuddhiḥ tāvat asat samā tasya api kāraṇe śuddhe tad jñāne syāt pramāṇatā tasya api evam iti icchaḥ ca na kva cit vyavatiṣṭhate 
SV_2.52ab–2.55ab	 yadā svatas pramāṇa tvam tadā anyat na eva gṛhyate nivarttat te hi mithyātvam doṣa ajñānāt ayatnatas tasmāt bodha ātmaka tvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇa tā arthānyathātva hetu uttha doṣa jñānāt apodyate aprāmāṇyam tridhā bhinnam mithyātva ajñāna saṃśayaiḥ vastu tvāt dvividhasya atra sambhavaḥ duṣṭa kāraṇāt avijñāne tu doṣāṇām vyāpāraḥ na eva kalpyate 
SV_2.55cd–2.58cd	 kāraṇa abhāvataḥ tu eva tat siddham naḥ tvad ukti vat doṣataḥ ca apramāṇa tve svatas prāmāṇya vādinām guṇa jñāna anavasthāvat na doṣeṣu prasajyate sākṣāt viparyaya jñānāt laghvi eva tu apramāṇa tā pūrva ābādhena na utpattiḥ uttarasya hi sidhyati duṣṭa kāraṇa bodhe tu siddhe api viṣaya antare arthāt tulya artha tām prāpya bādhaḥ go dohana ādi vat 
SV_2.59ab–2.62ab	 tatra doṣa antara jñānam bādha dhīḥ vā parā na ced tad udbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvāt ādyamāna tā svatas eva hi tatra api doṣa ajñānāt pramāṇa tā doṣa jñāne tu anutpanne na śaṅkyā niṣpramāṇa tā evam tri catur ajñāna janmanaḥ na adhikā matiḥ prārthyate tāvatā eva ekam svatas prāmāṇyam aśnute śabde doṣa udbhavaḥ tāvat vaktra dhīnaḥ iti sthitiḥ 
SV_2.62cd–2.65cd	 tad abhāvaḥ kva cit tāvat guṇavat vaktṛka tvataḥ tad guṇaiḥ apakṛṣṭānām śabde saṃkrānti asambhavāt yadā vaktuḥ abhāvena na syuḥ doṣāḥ nirāśrayāḥ pauruṣeye dvayam dṛṣṭam doṣa abhāvaḥ guṇāḥ tathā prāmāṇyam tatra guṇataḥ na eva syāt iti udāhṛtam tasmāt guṇebhyaḥ doṣāṇām abhāvaḥ tad abhāvataḥ aprāmāṇya dvaya asattvam tena utsargaḥ anapoditaḥ 
SV_2.66ab–2.69ab	 pratyaya utpatti hetutvāt prāmāṇyam na apanīyate doṣa abhāvaḥ guṇebhyaḥ ced nanu sā eva āsthitiḥ bhavet tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamāna tayā guṇāḥ doṣa abhāve tu vijñeye sattā mātra upakāriṇaḥ tatra apavāda nirmuktiḥ vaktra bhāvāt laghīyasī vede tena apramāṇa tvam na āśaṅkām api gacchati atas vaktra nadhīna tvāt prāmāṇye tad upāsanam 
SV_2.69cd–2.72cd	 na yuktam apramāṇa tve kalpye tad prārthanā bhavet tatas ca āpta apraṇīta tvam na doṣāya atra jāyate prayogāṇām tu sarveṣām vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇa antara mūla tā tad abhāve hi tat duṣyet itarat na kadā canaḥ tena itaraiḥ pramāṇaiḥ yā codanānām asaṅgatiḥ tayā eva syāt pramāṇa tvam anuvāda tvam anyathā 
SV_2.73ab–2.76ab	 anyasya api pramāṇa tve saṅgatiḥ na eva kāraṇam tulya arthānām vikalpya tvāt ekam tatra hi bodhakam yatra api syāt paricchedaḥ pramāṇaiḥ uttaraiḥ punar nūnam tatra api pūrveṇa saḥ arthaḥ na avadhṛtaḥ tathā saṅgatyā yadi ca iṣyeta pūrva pūrva pramāṇa tā pramāṇa antaram icchantaḥ na vyavasthām labhemahi kasya cit tu yadīṣyeta svatas eva pramāṇatā 
SV_2.76cd–2.79cd	 prathamasya tathā abhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ śrotra dhīḥ ca apramāṇam syāt itarābhiḥ asaṅgateḥ syāt ced tad janitena eva jñānena anyena saṅgatiḥ vede api śata kṛtvas syāt buddhiḥ uccāraṇa anugāḥ sādhana antara janyā tu buddhiḥ na asti dvayoḥ api yathā tu eka indriya adhīna jñāna antara nibandhanā saṅgatiḥ kāraṇam prāptā tathā vede api kalpyatām 
SV_2.80ab–2.83ab	 tasmāt dṛḍham yat utpannam na api saṃvādam ṛcchati jñāna antareṇa vijñānam tad pramāṇam pratīyatām na ca anumānataḥ sādhyā śabda ādīnām pramāṇatā sarvasya eva hi mā prāpat pramāṇa antara sādhya tā nanu pramāṇam iti evam pratyakṣa ādi na gṛhyate na ca ittham agṛhītena vyavahāraḥ avakalpate prāmāṇyam grahaṇāt pūrvam sva rūpeṇa eva saṃsthitam 
SV_2.83cd–2.86cd	 nirapekṣam sva kāryeṣu gṛhyate pratyaya antaraiḥ tena asya jñāyamāna tvam prāmāṇye na upayujyate viṣaya anubhāvaḥ hi atra pūrvasmāt eva labhyate apramāṇam punar sva artha grāhakam syāt svarūpataḥ nivṛttiḥ tasya mithyātve na agṛhīte paraiḥ bhavet na hi arthasya ātathā bhāvaḥ pūrveṇa arthaḥ tathā ātva vat tatra api arthāni atha abhāve dhīḥ yat vā duṣṭa kāraṇe 
SV_2.87ab–2.90ab	 tāvatā eva ca mithyātvam gṛhyate na anya hetukam utpatti avastham ca eva idam pramāṇam iti mīyate atas yatra api mithyātvam parebhyaḥ pratipādyate tatra api etat dvayam vācyam na tu sādharmya mātrakam codanā arthān yathā bhāvam kurvataḥ ca anumānataḥ tad jñānena eva yaḥ bādhaḥ sa katham vinivāryate tat mithyā tvāt abādhaḥ ced prāptam anyonya saṃśrayam 
SV_2.90cd–2.93cd	 na anumānāt atas anyat dhi bādhakam kiñ cit asti te na ca anyaiḥ agrahe arthasya syāt abhāvaḥ rasa ādi vat teṣām jihvā ādibhiḥ yasmāt niyamaḥ grahaṇe asti hi tat hiyā eva artha bodhaḥ ced tādṛś dharme bhaviṣyati mama asiddham idam kin tu vedāt jāte avabodhane vaktum na dveṣa mātreṇa yujyate satya vādinā dveṣāt asammata tvāt vā na ca syāt apramāṇa tā 
SV_2.94ab–2.97ab	 na ca ātma icchā abhyanujñābhyām prāmāṇyam avakalpate agni dāha ādi duḥkhasya na hi apratyakṣata iṣyate na ca abhilāpikam jñānam prāmāṇyena avadhāryate tasmāt āloka vat vede sarva sādhāraṇe sati na evam vipratipattavyam bauddha ādeḥ vakṣyate antaram puruṣa aśaktitaḥ tatra sa apavāda tva sambhavaḥ vedasya apauruṣeya tve siddhā tu evam pramāṇa tā 
SV_2.97cd–2.100cd	 kartṛ mat tve tu vedasya samyak mithyā tva vādibhiḥ kartā guṇāḥ ca doṣāḥ ca mahājana parigrahaḥ evamādi vinā yuktyā kalpyam mīmāṃsakaiḥ punar idānīm iva sarvatra dṛṣṭān na adhikam iṣyate evambhūtasya vedasya jñāna utpattim prakurvataḥ sva rūpa viparīta tva saṃśayau bhāṣya vāritau nivārayiṣyate ca api duṣṭa kāraṇa kalpanā 
SV_2.101ab–2.104ab	 puruṣa abhāvataḥ tena tad dvāreṇa api aśaṅkitau tathā satya tathā bhāvaḥ buddhi anutpattim āśritaḥ tatra vipratiṣiddha tvam bravīti iti evamādinā yathā adṛṣṭa artha vādi tvam tat ced pratyayitāt iti indriya iti tu mūlam ced asya asti iti evam abravīt draṣṭṛ tva satya vādi tve tat ced pratyayitāt iti dṛśyamāna artha vādi tve syāt anāpta ukti satya tā 
SV_2.104cd–2.107cd	 evam tu eka aṅga vaikalyāt pratyudāharaṇa sthitiḥ ekaika abhāva mātre syāt āpta tvā aindriyaka tvayoḥ apratyayita pakṣe syāt aindriyasya api asatya tā anindriya tva pakṣe vā sat pratyayita bhāṣitam vyāhata grantha tā evam syāt tasmāt pūrveṇa satya tā pareṇa mūla sadbhāvaḥ indriyeṇa tu darśitaḥ aprāmāṇya nivṛtti artham doṣa abhāva upavarṇanam 
SV_2.108ab–2.111ab	 guṇāt prāmāṇyam iti evam tat pūrvam su nirākṛtam pūrvatra pratiṣiddha tvāt na etat prāmāṇya kāraṇam samuccaya arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ pūrvasmin uttaratra ca vikalpena ubhayoḥ āha pratyudāharaṇe pṛthak śakye api asatye mithyātvam dṛṣṭam satye api aśaktike na anena vacanena iha sarvajña tva nirākriyā vacanāt ṛtaḥ iti evam apavādaḥ hi saṃśritaḥ 
SV_2.111cd–2.114cd	 yadi ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ syāt sarvajñaḥ kena vāryate ekena tu pramāṇena sarvajñaḥ yena kalpyate nūnam sa cakṣuṣā sarvān rasa ādīn pratipadyate yat jātīyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ tu yat jātīya artha darśanam bhavet idānīm lokasya tathā kāla antare api abhūt yatra api atiśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa sva artha an atilaṅghanāt dūra sūkṣma ādi dṛṣṭau syāt na rūpe śrotra vṛtti tā 
SV_2.115ab–2.118ab	 bhaviṣyati na dṛṣṭam ca pratyakṣasya manāk api sāmarthyam na anumāna ādeḥ liṅga ādi rahite kva cit sarvajña kalpanā anyaiḥ tu vede ca apauruṣeya tā tulya tā kalpitāḥ yena tena idam sampradhāryatām sarvajñaḥ dṛśyate tāvat na idānīm asmad ādibhiḥ nirākaraṇa vat śakyā na ca āsīt iti kalpanā na ca āgamena sarvajñaḥ tadīye anyonya saṃśrayāt 
SV_2.118cd–2.121cd	 nara antara praṇītasya prāmāṇyam gamyate katham na ca api evamparaḥ nityaḥ śakyaḥ labdhum iha āgamaḥ nityaḥ ced arthavāda tvam tad pare syāt anitya tā āgamasya ca nitya tve siddhe tad kalpanā vṛthā yatas tam pratipadyante dharmam eva tatas narāḥ yaḥ api indriya artha sambandha viṣaye satya vādi tām dṛṣṭvā tad vacana tvena śraddheye arthe api kalpayet 
SV_2.122ab–2.125ab	 tena api pāratantryeṇa bādhitā syāt pramāṇatā prāmāṇyam ced svayam tasya kāpekṣā anya indriya ādiṣu yathā eva atra indriya ādibhyaḥ paricchedāt pramāṇatā śraddheye api tathā eva syāt na svātantryeṇa labhyate yathā ca teṣām satya tvam sidhyati etena hetunā tathā anyān avabuddha artha prāmāṇya abhāva sādhanam aśraddheya artha satya tvam śraddheye ca api asatya tā 
SV_2.125cd–2.128cd	 pūrva jñāna anuvādi tvam dṛṣṭānta vat iha iṣyatām api ca alaukika artha tve sati puṃvākya hetukam mithyātvam bauddha vākyānām syāt anyonyam sa pakṣataḥ dharma adharma atirikta arthe prāmāṇyaṃa ca prasajyate sāṃkhya ādiṣu ca jīvatsu dṛṣṭāntaḥ durlabhaḥ asya ca alaukika artha vāci tvam nṛ vākya tve satī iti ca parasparam apekṣya eva bauddha ādeḥ syāt mṛṣārtha tā 
SV_2.129ab–2.132ab	 vadet evam ca yaḥ nāma vādī prathama saṅgataḥ tasya api hetuḥ syāt eṣa bhavantam pratyasaṃśayam buddha ādīnām asarvajñam iti satyam vacaḥ mama mad ukta tvāt yathā eva agniḥ uṣṇaḥ bhāsvaraḥ iti api pratyakṣam ca mad ukta tvam tvayā sādhyā tad ukta tā tena hetuḥ madīyaḥ syāt sandigdha asiddha tā tava pratyakṣa ādyavi saṃvādi prameya tva ādi yasya ca 
SV_2.132cd–2.135cd	 sadbhāva vāraṇe śaktam kaḥ nu tam kalpayiṣyati na ca api smṛti avicchedāt sarvajñaḥ parikalpyate vigānāt chinna mūla tvāt kaiḥ cit eva parigrahāt sarvajñaḥ asau iti hi eva tad kāle tu bubhutsubhiḥ tad jñāna jñeya vijñāna rahitaiḥ gamyate katham kalpanīyāḥ ca sarva jñāḥ bhaveyuḥ bahavaḥ tava yaḥ eva syāt asarva jñaḥ sa sarvajñam na budhyate 
SV_2.136ab–2.139ab	 sarvajñaḥ anavabuddhaḥ ca yena eva syāt na tam prati tad vākyānām pramāṇa tvam mūla ajñāne anya vākya vat rāga ādi rahite ca asmin nirvyāpāre vyavasthite deśanā anya praṇītā eva syāt ṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt sānnidhya mātrataḥ tasya puṃsaḥ cintāmaṇeḥ iva niḥsaranti yathākāmam kuḍya ādibhyaḥ api deśanāḥ evamādi ucyamānam tu śraddadhānasya śobhate 
SV_2.139cd–2.142cd	 kuḍya ādi niḥsṛta tvāt ca na āśvāsaḥ deśanāsu naḥ kin nu buddha praṇītāḥ syuḥ kimu kaiḥ cit durātmabhiḥ adṛśyaiḥ vipralambha artham piśāca ādibhiḥ īritāḥ evam yaiḥ kevalam jñānam indriya ādi anapekṣiṇaḥ sūkṣma atīta ādi viṣayam jīvasya parikalpitam na ṛte tad āgamāt sidhyet na ca tena āgamaḥ vinā dṛṣṭāntaḥ api na tasya anyaḥ nṛṣu kaḥ cit pravartate 
SV_2.143ab–2.146ab	 nitya āgama avabodhaḥ api pratyākhyeyaḥ anayā diśā na hi tatra api visrambhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anena kṛtaḥ atha vā sarvadā ca api puruṣāḥ prāyeṇa anṛta vādinaḥ yathā adya tve na visrambhaḥ tathā atīta artha kīrtane svapna ādi jñāna vat ca api pratyayaḥ asya āgama arthayoḥ bhavet iti sa śaṅkānām prāmāṇyam gamyate katham puruṣa atiśayaḥ ca iṣṭaḥ sā eva ca āgama nityatā 
SV_2.146cd–2.149cd	 kalpitam smaraṇam ca asya janma antara nibandhanam grāhya tve ca āgamasya evam dveṣaḥ artha grahaṇe vṛthā yaḥ hi anuccāritam śabdam gahṇa ati arthe asya kā kathā pumān tāvat svatantraḥ syāt artha grahaṇa vādinām āgama pratibhāne tu pāratantryam dvayoḥ api aneka puruṣa stha tvāt ekatra eva ca janmani grahaṇa smaraṇāt vede na svātantryam vihanyate 
SV_2.150ab–2.153ab	 anyathā karaṇe ca asya bahubhyaḥ syāt nivāraṇam ekasya pratibhānam tu kṛtakān na viśiṣyate atas ca sampradāye ca na ekaḥ puruṣaḥ iṣyate bahavaḥ paratantrāḥ syuḥ sarve hi adyatva vat narāḥ evam ca kalpayanti anye yāvat āgama siddhaye tāvat na kalpayati etat sama tvam jaimineḥ paraiḥ na hi dṛṣṭa adhikam kiñ cit prāmāṇye tena kalpyate 
SV_2.153cd–2.156cd	 aprāmāṇya nimitteṣu parasya adṛṣṭa kalpanā dṛṣṭa prāmāṇya bādhaḥ ca nāstikasya prasajyate utpanne sati vijñāne balāt bādha prakalpanā sādhite puruṣa abhāve nirdoṣa jñāna janmanaḥ pratyakṣāt nāstikaiḥ vācyaḥ viśeṣaḥ codana ādhiyaḥ upadeśaḥ anyathā na syāt atīndriya nidandhanaḥ tasya kartrā na ced dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ arthaḥ iti artha kalpanā 
SV_2.157ab–2.160ab	 yat vā anumānam eva idam upadeśi tvam ucyate dṛṣṭa artha pūrva tā vyāptam vyatirekaḥ asya nanu iti anyathā api upapanna tvam vyāmohāt iti kathyate liṅgasya vyabhicāraḥ vā bāla vākya nidarśanāt vedāt jñātvā upadiṣṭam ced iti evam siddha sādhanam vedāt api iti anena uktam manu ādeḥ ca etat iṣyate anyathā saṃvidānaḥ api vivakṣati anyathā yatas 
SV_2.160cd–2.163cd	 tasmāt ekāntataḥ na asti puṃvākyāt tat dhiyām gatiḥ bhrāntasya anya vivakṣāyām anyat vākyam ca dṛśyate yathā vivakṣam api etat tasmāt na eva pravartate vaktṛ dhīḥ āpta vākyeṣu gamyate anyatra viplutiḥ tena utsarga apavādābhyām vacasaḥ śaktiḥ ucyate padārtha racanā āyattaḥ vākya artha pratyaya udbhavaḥ vivakṣā pūrva vijñāna vaśāt ca racanā ākṛtiḥ 
SV_2.164ab–2.167ab	 vivakṣā antara yuktāḥ hi kurvāṇāḥ racanā antaram āvāpa udvāpa bhedena dṛśyante artheṣu mānavāḥ tena artha pratyaya utpāde śrotuḥ jāte api vākyataḥ jñātaḥ nūnam anena iti vaktuḥ jñāne matiḥ bhavet āpta ukti kāraṇam kañ cit anuyuṅkte naram yadā tadā ca nirdiśati āptam sa jānāti etat iti asau tad jñāna antarita tvāt ca śabdāḥ tāvat udāsate 
SV_2.167cd–2.170cd	 prāmāṇya sthāpanam tu syāt vaktṛ dhī hetu sambhavāt arthe pūrva pratīte api niścayaḥ hi tad āśrayaḥ tena artha jñāna gamya api prāmāṇye sā eva pūrva bhāj atas atra puṃnimitta tvāt upapannā mṛṣā artha tā na tu syāt tad svabhāva tvam vede vaktuḥ abhāvataḥ tad buddhi antarayoḥ na asti iti arthaḥ arthaiḥ ca pratīyate atas na jñāna pūrva tvam apekṣyam na ayathārtha tā 
SV_2.171ab–2.174ab	 apramāṇa tva siddhau vā dṛṣṭāntaḥ yaḥ udāhṛtaḥ buddha ādi vacanam tasya sādhyena asaṅga tā ucyate teṣām api hi yat kāryam pūrvatra pratipāditam tatra samyaktvam arthe tu vyāpāraḥ na eva vidyate sva vyāpāra atirikte arthe vedasya api mṛṣā artha tā pūrva pakṣa arthavat tvena prasaktā siddha sādhya tā ajñātvā evam abhiprāyam kṛtaka akṛtaka tvayoḥ 
SV_2.174cd–2.177cd	 satya mithyā tva hetu ukti mātra jñānāt paraḥ abravīt nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam na anya tvāt iti adūṣaṇam anya tvāt eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ na hi pakṣe sa pakṣatā tasmāt ayam abhiprāyaḥ bhāṣya kārasya varṇyate abhyupetya artha viṣayam vākya vyāpāram ucyate yadi syāt vyavadhāne api vākya artha apekṣayā anṛtam dṛṣṭāntaḥ nṛ vacaḥ atra api hetuḥ sādhāraṇaḥ bhavet 
SV_2.178ab–2.181ab	 satyeṣu api hi dṛṣṭā eva paurṣeyeṣu vākyatā atīndriye api kiñ cit dhi satyam dṛṣṭam yadṛcchayā na anya tvāt iti ca anena para uktāt anyatā ucyate anyaḥ hi eṣa tad ābhāsaḥ vipakṣam vā anyam abravīt yat vā anyasmāt visaṃvādān mithyātvam tatra na tu iha viṣayasya api ca anya tvāt sādhana āsaṅga tā eva sā na hi anyasya iti na ekasmin mṛṣā arthe anyam ṛṣā artha tā 
SV_2.181cd–2.184cd	 vivakṣāyāḥ mṛṣārtha tve na ca vākye mṛṣārtha tā śyāma tve puṃstva vat ca etat sādhāraṇye nidarśanam parokteḥ vā api duṣṭa tvāt vikalpa samam ucyate yat vā pramāṇam eva idam samyaktve anya tvam ucyate dhiruddha avi abhicāri tvam bādhaḥ vā api anumānataḥ codanā janitā buddhiḥ pramāṇam doṣa varjitaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ janyamāna tvāt liṅga āpta ukti akṣa buddhi vat 
SV_2.185ab–2.188ab	 tathā anāptā praṇīta ukti janya tvāt bādha varjanāt deśa kāla ādi bheda ādau ca āpta ukti pratyayaḥ yathā akartṛka tva siddhyā ca hetu tvam sādhayiṣyate evamādi avabudhya ayam na anya tvāt iti avocata pratyakṣaḥ tu iti dārḍhyam vā prāthamyam vā api lakṣayet svarūpataḥ pramāṇa tvam mithyātvam para rūpataḥ jñāna abhāvaḥ ca mithyātvam dvayasya asambhavāt yadi 
SV_2.188cd–2.191cd	 pratyakṣam tad pareṣām ca siddham asya anumānataḥ yathā ca tava mithyātvam sādhanam sādhayet idam tathā ca bādhaka adhīnam mithyātvam api sādhayet dharmaḥ iti upasaṃhārye yat śreyaskara bhāṣaṇam tad dharma pada vācya artha nirūpaṇa vivakṣayā śreyaḥ hi puruṣa prītiḥ sā dravya guṇa karmabhiḥ codanā lakṣaṇaiḥ sādhyā tasmāt teṣu eva dharmatā 
SV_2.192ab–2.195ab	 anyat sādhyam adṛṣṭvā eva yāga ādīn anuniṣṭhataḥ dhārmika tva samākhyānam tad yogāt iti gamyate paśu ādīni ca dharmasya phalāni iti vyavasthitam citrā go dohana ādīnām tāni uktāni phalāni ca tasmāt teṣu eva dharma tvam dhrmāṇi iti ca darśanāt liṅga saṃkhyā vinirmuktaḥ dharma śabdaḥ nidarśanam antaḥkaraṇa vṛttau vā vāsanāyām ca cetasaḥ 
SV_2.195cd–2.198cd	 pudgaleṣu ca puṇyeṣu nṛguṇe apūrva janmani prayogaḥ dharma śabdasya na dṛṣṭaḥ na ca sādhanam puruṣa arthasya te jñātum śakyante codana ādibhiḥ na ca vastu antaram śakyam apūrvam svarga yāgayoḥ jñātum sādhana bhūtam vā sādhyam vā na api atas anyathā śruta sādhana sādhya tva tyāgena aśruta kalpanā prasajyeta asya tādrūpye vyatireke tu arūpa tā 
SV_2.199ab–2.202ab	 tasmāt phale pravṛttasya yāga ādeḥ śakti mātrakam utpattau vā api paśu ādeḥ apūrvam na tatas pṛthak śaktayaḥ sarva bhāvānām bhāva śabdaiḥ viśeṣataḥ na upākhyāyante iti evam na apūrvam dharma śabda tā purastāt codanā śabdaḥ vidhau eva vyavasthitaḥ na ca tad lakṣaṇā hiṃsā pratyudāharaṇam katham codanā lakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ ca śyena ādiḥ hi gamyate 
SV_2.202cd–2.205cd	 niṣedha abhāvataḥ tasya katham brūyāt anartha tā yadi api syāt vidhi spṛṣṭe niṣedhaḥ na eva tādṛśaḥ vijñāyate hi anartha tvam ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa ādi vat codanā lakṣaṇam ca uktvā niṣiddha tvāt virudhyate śyena ādau upadiṣṭe ca hiṃsā hi iti na yujyate hiṃsā hi phalam eteṣām bhinnā tebhyaḥ svarūpataḥ sā hi prāṇa viyoga ātmā śyenaḥ tatra asi vat pṛthak 
SV_2.206ab–2.209ab	 upadeśa abhidhānam ca na avidheye avakalpate śyena ādeḥ avidhāne ca kasya anyasya vidheya tā sarvatra avasthitaḥ nyāyaḥ bhāvanā aṃśa dvaye vidhiḥ sa bādhyeta iha ye ca amī jyotiṣṭoma ādayaḥ matāḥ dharma tvena na te api syuḥ hiṃsā sādhanakāḥ hi te na ca avidhīyamānasya phala tad sādhana aṅgatā sādhana tvena vihitam na ca avihitam ucyate 
SV_2.209cd–2.212cd	 sādhya tvena vidhānam tu na eva iṣṭam loka vedayoḥ tena evam artha śabdasya prayojanam iha ucyate pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yā śabda śravaṇena dhīḥ sā codanā iti sāmānyam lakṣaṇam hṛdaye sthitam pravartaka gṛhītiḥ tu syāt udāharaṇa artha tā tātparye hi artha śabdasya na iyam vyākhyā upapadyate artha grahaṇa labhyam vā tad pravartaka bhāṣaṇam 
SV_2.213ab–2.216ab	 dharme pramāṇa bhūtāyāḥ tat vā lakṣaṇam uktavān evam sati vidhibhyaḥ syāt vidheya artha avadhāraṇam niṣedhebhyaḥ niṣedhyānām anartha tvena nirṇayaḥ tena artha grahaṇena uktāḥ vidheyasya iha dharmatā niṣedhyānām anartha tvam artha siddham na sūtritam tasmāt ubhayam iti atra vidheya pratiṣedhyayoḥ yāga ādi brahmahatyā di vargayoḥ syāt nidarśanam 
SV_2.216cd–2.219cd	 śyena ādīnām vidheya tvāt iṣṭasya api ca sādhanāt upacārāt anartha tvam phala dvāreṇa varṇyate pratiṣiddhā hi sā iti atra sphuṭam etat kariṣyate hiṃsā hi iti ca yat ca api brūte na abhicaret iti śyena ādīnām svarūpe tu na uttara grantha saṅgatiḥ vihita tvāt niṣedhasya pravṛttiḥ teṣu durlabhā yadā tu codanā śabdaḥ vidhau= eva vyavasthitaḥ 
SV_2.220ab–2.223ab	 tadā ubhaya ādikaḥ granthaḥ sadhya sādhana saṃśritaḥ sādhya sādhana sambandhe vidhinā pratipādite lakṣyamāṇa tvam ubhayoḥ dvividham ca phalam kratoḥ svarga ādi prāpyate tatra pratiṣedha anatikramāt atikrameṇa hiṃsā ādi śāstra antara nirīkṣayā phala aṃśe bhāvanāyāḥ ca pratyayaḥ na vidhāyakaḥ vakṣyate jaiminiḥ ca āha tasya lipsā artha lakṣaṇāḥ 
SV_2.223cd–2.226cd	 tena sāmānyatas prāptaḥ vidhinā na nivāritaḥ phala aṃśa upanipātinyāḥ hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ anartha prāpti hetu tvam bodhyate tatra yadi api śyena svarūpam na anarthaḥ tad phalasya tu anartha tā paraḥ tu ubhayam iti ādeḥ phalasya api vidheya tām bhāvanā antargata tvāt vā matvā anartha tvam ākṣipat na eva iti etāvatā ca asya vidheya tva nirākriyā 
SV_2.227ab–2.230ab	 kim vidheyam idānīm syāt āha śyena ādayaḥ tu iti praśna apākaraṇe ca atra tavyaḥ vidhi vivakṣayā prayuktaḥ na tu sādhye arthe dvaye api anupayogataḥ anarthasya api sādhya tvam avidheyasya hi iṣyate sādhya tva rahite ceṣṭā vidheye nityam artha tā śatuḥ ca lakṣaṇa artha tvam teṣām ca api upadeśanam bruvan sphuṭīkara uti iṣṭam upadeśaḥ hi na anyathā 
SV_2.230cd–2.233cd	 vidhi tvam ādi śabdāt syāt itikartavya tāsu api tasmāt phala aṃśe yā hiṃsā vaidikī sā niṣidhyate aṃśa dvaye tu yā nāma tad niṣedha abhidhāyinām aviśeṣeṇa yat śāstram śirovat iti ca uttaram niṣedhena anavaṣṭabdhe viṣaye na hi anartha tā pratyakṣa ādeḥ aśakya tvāt kalpyate niṣpramāṇikāḥ na hi hiṃsā ādi anuṣṭhāne tadānīm doṣa darśanam 
SV_2.234ab–2.237ab	 bāhye api vicikitsā tu śāstrāt eva upajāyate hiṃsyamānasya duḥkhi tvam dṛśyate yat na tāvatā kartuḥ duḥkha anumānam syāt tadānīm tad viparyayaḥ viṣaye asyāḥ phalam yādṛś pretya krtuḥ tathāvidham hiṃsā kriyā viśeṣa tvāt sūte śāstra ukta dāna vat yaḥ evam āha tasya api guru strī gamana ādibhiḥ surā pāna ādibhiḥ ca api vipakṣaiḥ vyabhicāritā 
SV_2.237cd–2.240cd	 viruddha tā ca yādṛś dhi dānaiḥ tādṛś phalam bhavet vidhi gamya phala avāptiḥ aduḥkha ātmaka tā tathā na ca yā sampradānasya prītiḥ tādṛś phalam śrutam dātuḥ tena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya hīnaḥ pratīyate sampradānam ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane vaiṣamyam sampradāne tu pakṣe tu etat viruddha tā prīyate sampradānam hi devatā iti matam tava 
SV_2.241ab–2.244ab	 dṛṣṭānte karma dānam ced tasya kīdṛś phalam bhavet japa homa ādi dṛṣṭāntāt para pīḍā ādi varjanāt codita tvasya hetu tvāt viruddha avyabhicāritā vihita pratiṣiddha tve muktvā anyat na ca kāraṇam dharma adharma avabodhasya tena ayukta anumāna gīḥ anugrahāt ca dharma tvam pīḍātaḥ ca api adharma tām vadataḥ japa sīdhvādi pāna ādau na ubhayam bhavet 
SV_2.244cd–2.247cd	 krośatā hṛdayena api guru dāra abhigāminām bhūyān dharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hi upakāritā anumāna pradhānasya pratiṣedha anapekṣiṇaḥ hṛdaya krośanam kasmāt dṛṣṭām pīḍām apaśyataḥ poḍātaḥ ca api adharma tvam tathā pīḍām adharmataḥ anyonya āśrayam āpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan evamādau aśāstra jñaḥ mla icchaḥ na udvijate kva cit 
SV_2.248ab–2.251ab	 tasya na adharma yogaḥ syāt pūrva uktā yadi kalpanā tasmāt anugraham pīḍām tad abhāvam apāsya ca dharma adharma arthibhiḥ nityam mṛgyau vidhi niṣedhakau kva cit asyāḥ niṣiddha tvāt śaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitāḥ pratyavāya nimitta tve vidhinā na apagacchati śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnām āvāpa udvāpana kriyāḥ vidyamānāḥ hi kathyante śaktayaḥ dravya karmaṇām 
SV_2.251cd–2.254cd	 tat eva ca idam karma iti śāstram eva anudhāvatā hiṃsā ādīnām adharma tvam kathyate na anumānataḥ evam ye nipuṇam prāhuḥ taiḥ api etat parīkṣyatām surā pāna ādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kim yāti narakam kṛtaiḥ vaiśya stomena vā kim syāt vipra rājanyayoḥ phalam pañcamyām iṣṭi karaṇāt madhyāhne ca agnihotrataḥ tasmāt yadi ādṛśam karma yat phala utpatti śaktikam 
SV_2.255ab–2.258ab	 śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasya eva tat phalam hiṃsā ca aṃśa dvayāt anyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedha jam pratyavāya artha tā jñānam vidhinā anyatra vāryate jñānam eva ca śaktīnām nāvāpa udvāpana kriyāḥ jñāyante śāstrataḥ tāḥ tu kriyā bheda vyavasthitāḥ vyavasthāḥ śakti bhedānām dṛṣṭa artheṣu api karmasu abhinna tve api dṛśyante bhujeḥ sva sthātuḥ eṣu api 
SV_2.258cd–2.261cd	 rūpa abhede api hiṃsā ādeḥ bhedaḥ aṅga an aṅga kāritaḥ tathā api eka phala tvam ced kriyā tvāt sarva saṅkaraḥ yajitvādya viśeṣāt ca citra ādi phala tulya tā bhedāt tatra vyavasthā ced iha api evam bhaviṣyati vidhīnām vā api sarveṣām sākṣāt vyavahitaḥ api vā puruṣa arthaḥ phalam tena na anarthaḥ atas pratīyate na ca eṣu śrūyate anarthaḥ niṣedhāt na ca kalpyate 
SV_2.262ab–2.265ab	 na ca prakaraṇa stha tvāt puruṣa arthaḥ phalam bhavet karma upakāraḥ kalpyaḥ tu dṛṣṭaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ atha vā punar kalpanā avasaraḥ tatra na anarthasya anapekṣaṇāt kratu arthaḥ ca api saṃskāraḥ paśoḥ nārāt upakriyā dṛṣṭā eva tu avadānānām niṣpattiḥ kratu apekṣitā abhicāre api upāya sthā hiṃsā na adharmaḥ ucyate tasmāt anaṅga bhūtāyām hiṃsāyām etat ucyate 
SV_2.265cd–2.268cd	 uddeśāt ca phalatvena śyena ādau na vidhīyate bhāvanā vidhiḥ api eva phala aṃśāt vinivartate atas svatas na dharma tvam śyena ādeḥ na api adharmatā phala anartha anubandhi tvāt tad dvāreṇa upacaryate nirākāṅkṣasya ca ekena śyenasya na phala dvayam tasmāt kriyā antarāt eva hiṃsātaḥ anarthaḥ ucyate phalataḥ api ca yat karma na anarthena anubadhyate 
SV_2.269ab–2.272ab	 kevala prīti hetu tvāt tad dharma tvena hi iṣyate nanu ceṣṭā abhyupāya tvāt śyena ādeḥ dharmatā bhavet phalam tāvat adharmaḥ asya śyena ādeḥ sampradhāryate yadi yena iṣṭa siddhiḥ syāt anuṣṭhāna anubandhinī tasya dharma tvam ucyeta tatas śyena ādi varjanam yadā tu codanā gamyaḥ kārya akārya anapekṣayā dharmaḥ prīti nimittam syāt tadā śyene api dharmatā 
SV_2.272cd–2.275cd	 yadi tu aprīti hetuḥ yaḥ sākṣāt vyavahitaḥ api vā saḥ adharmaḥ codanā arthaḥ syāt tadā śyene api adharma tā yaḥ tu hiṃsā tva sādharmyāt bāhya vat codanāsu api vadet anartha hetu tvam tasya api āgama bādhanam tam anādṛtya yaḥ brūyāt yāga ādeḥ api asau vadet svarga ādi sādhana aśaktim kriyā tvāt bhojana ādi vat gītā mantra artha vādaiḥ yā kalpyate anartha hetu tā 
SV_2.276ab–2.279ab	 pratyakṣa śruti bādhya tvāt sānya artha tvena nīyate śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭa tvāt sūtra vaidika vākyayoḥ aśakteḥ ca ubhayoḥ sāmyāt na sūtreṣu iti anuttaram prāc ukta parisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalam etat prakāśyate sūtreṣu hi anayā yuktyā gatiḥ eṣā api yujyate tasmāt āvartate sūtram tantram vā śakti bhedataḥ eka deśa anumānāt vā dve sūtre parikalpite 
SV_2.279cd–2.282cd	 itaretara sāmīpyāt etau eva parasparam kalpī ete vākya śeṣāya na anya avayava kalpanā viśiṣṭa artha anuvādi tvāt atha vā iti api bhāṣite vākya bhedaḥ saḥ eva iti saṃjñā tantra tvam uttaram artham vā pratyupādānāt saṃjñā lakṣaṇa śabdayoḥ tantram lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ vā vācyaḥ dharma artha śabdayoḥ dharme sāmānyatas siddhe pramāṇam kathyate yadā 
SV_2.283ab–2.287ab	 vṛttam eva tadārtha tvam kim artham punar ucyate codanā lakṣaṇa tvasya dharmam prati vidheya tā labhyate artha anuvādena saṃśayaḥ hi anyathā bhavet tathā ca ye api anarthasya sādhana tvena kalpitāḥ niṣedhaiḥ te api dharmāḥ syuḥ codanā lakṣaṇa tvataḥ tasmāt artha aparityāgāt eka artha grahaṇam yathā labhyate vacana vyaktyā sā syāt artha anuvādataḥ viśeṣaṇāt vinā ca etad artha sāmarthya kāritam kathyate bhāṣya kāreṇa phalam hiṃsā ādi varjanam 
SV_3.1ab–4.4ab	 pratijñā vyatirekeṇa bhāṣya kāreṇa yadi api vakṣyamāṇā sva pakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvam nidarśitāḥ pratijñā mātram iti etat jaimineḥ matam ucyate vṛtti kāraḥ adhikam vā api bhūtādi dvāram abravīt varṇyate sūtra bhedena yena pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam tena sūtrasya sambandhaḥ vācyaḥ pūrva pratijñayā lakṣaṇasya abhidhānam tu kena aṃśena upayujyate kimartham ca anumāna ādeḥ lakṣaṇam na atra kathyate na tāvat apramāṇa tvam teṣām na api akṣa buddhiṣu śakyate antargatiḥ vaktum na ca lakṣaṇa tulya tā na ca api siddhiḥ eṣām syāt arthāt pratyakṣa lakṣaṇāt 
SV_4.4cd–4.7cd	 na hi tad pūrvakam sarvam pramāṇam iti niścitam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa uktiḥ ca na anumāna ādi lakṣaṇāt vinā na sidhyati iti evam artha ākṣepaḥ na yujyate tat etat pūrvaka tve dhīḥ na ca tad lakṣaṇāt bhavet tad ukteḥ vā anumāna ādi kim na syāt tad apūrvakam na ca lakṣaṇa bhedasya svarūpe yat tayoḥ api pratyakṣa lakṣaṇāt eṣām kathan cit avadhāraṇāḥ 
SV_4.8ab–4.10cd	 prasiddha tvāt avācya tvam pratyakṣe api prasajyate tena anya parisaṃkhya artham sūtram mūḍhena vā ucyate na tu ekam lakṣayet eṣu buddhi pūrvam kathan canaḥ sambhavati eka vākya tve vākya bhedaḥ ca na iṣyate na ca api etena sūtreṇa pratyakṣam lakṣyate sphuṭam tad ābhāse api tulya tvāt svapna jñāna eka varjanāt 
SV_4.11ab–4.14ab	 tat hīndriya artha sambandha vyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet kena cit samprayoge tu bhrānti ādi syāt niyogataḥ grāhyeṇa anyena vā iti etat kṛtam na eva viśeṣaṇam samprayogasya yena syāt viśeṣaḥ vakṣyamāṇa vat asāmarthya ca matvā asya vṛtti kāreṇa lakṣaṇe tad samprayogaḥ iti evam pāṭhā antara mṛdāhṛtam tena anyena api saṃyoge cakṣuḥ ādeḥ yat utthitam 
SV_4.14cd–4.17cd	 viṣaya antara vijñānam tat pratyakṣam prasajyate sat samprayoga nirdeśaḥ vyarthaḥ ced etat eva hi pratipādyam parasya api lakṣaṇa asiddhiḥ eva ca svapna ādīnām nivṛttiḥ vā phalam tasya bhaviṣyati tasmāt vidhi anuvādi tvam na anukte lakṣaṇe bhavet tena na eṣā vacā uvyaktiḥ yat sati indriya saṅgame vijñānam jāyate tasya pratyakṣa tvam pratīyatām 
SV_4.18ab–4.21ab	 pratyakṣam yat jane siddham tasya evandharmaka tvataḥ vidyamāna upalambha tvam tena dharme nimitta tā evaṃlakṣaṇa tvam ca na sva rūpa vivakṣayā evaṃliṅgakam iti etat bhāṣya kāreṇa varṇyate yatas asti tatra dharmaḥ ayam vidyamāna upalambhanam tasmāt tena prasiddhena gamyatām animitta tā pratyakṣa tva madaḥ hetuḥ śeṣam hetu prasiddhaye 
SV_4.21cd–4.24cd	 asmāt ādau prasiddha tvāt yogi artham abhidhīyate prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣa aprāmāṇya darśanāt tad aprāmāṇya siddhiḥ ca sambandha ādeḥ anīkṣaṇāt śakyam anya apramāṇa tvam iti sūtraiḥ na paṭhyate na ca paryanuyogaḥ atra lakṣaṇa anupayogataḥ na ca nyūna atireka ādi prasaṅgaḥ lakṣaṇam prati sarvathā loka siddha tvāt dharmaḥ ayam tāvat iṣyate 
SV_4.25ab–4.28ab	 tatas ca mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi na pratyakṣam prasajyate animitta prasaṅgaḥ tu tasya api na nivāryate atīta anāgate api arthe sūkṣme vyavahite api ca pratyakṣam yoginām iṣṭam kaiḥ cit mukta ātmanām api vidyamāna upalambha tvam asiddham tatra tān prati bhaviṣyat tu asya vā hetoḥ tad grāhyaiḥ vyabhicāritā mā bhūtām iti tena āha loka siddham sat iti ayam 
SV_4.28cd–4.31cd	 na loka vyatiriktam hi pratyakṣam yoginām api pratyakṣa tvena tasya api vidyamāna upalambhanam sat samprayoga ja tvam vā api asmad pratyakṣa vat bhavet teṣām avartamāne arthe vā nāma utpadyate matiḥ pratyakṣam sā tatas tu eva na abhilāṣa smṛta ādi vat loke ca api aprasiddha tvāt pratyakṣa tva pramāṇataḥ pratibhāvat dvaya asattvam sat iti etena kathyate 
SV_4.32ab–4.34cd	 laukikī pratibhā yadvat pratyakṣa ādi anapekṣiṇī na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syāt yoginām api avidyamāna saṃyogāt syāt ced pratyakṣa dhīḥ kva cit bhaviṣyati api dharme syāt śakta iti āha sat iti ayam pratyakṣaḥ prāc anuṣtānāt na dharmaḥ anuṣṭhitaḥ api vā phala sādhana rūpeṇa tadānīm yena na asti asau 
SV_4.35ab–4.38ab	 asmad pratyakṣa vat ca api vidyamāna upalambhanam pratyakṣam dhyāyinām dharme pratyakṣa tvāt ca na iṣyate avidyamāna saṃyogāt pratyakṣa tu a nirākṛtiḥ yoginām kena labhyeta na iṣṭam sat grahaṇam yadi saptamyā api tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ kalpanā punar pareṣām vāraṇīya iti yatnaḥ jaimininā kṛtaḥ samyak arthe ca saṃśabdaḥ duṣprayoga nivāraṇaḥ 
SV_4.38cd–4.41cd	 prayogaḥ indriyāṇām ca vyāpāraḥ artheṣu kathyate duṣṭa tvāt śuktikā yogaḥ vāryate rajata īkṣaṇāt evam sati anuvāda tvam lakṣaṇasya api sambhavet tatas ca aprāpya kāri tvāt yat bauddhaiḥ śrotra cakṣuṣoḥ lakṣaṇa avyāpti siddhi artham saṃyogaḥ na iti kīrtyate prāpya grahaṇa pakṣe hi sāntara agrahaṇam kila adhiṣṭāna adhikaḥ ca arthaḥ na gṛhyeta tvac ādi vat 
SV_4.42ab–4.45ab	 vyāpāra mātra vāci tvāt aviruddham tat atra naḥ yadi vā artha ārjava sthānam samprayogaḥ atra varṇyate yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kārya lakṣitaḥ sāṃkhya ādīn vā vinirjitya prāpti pakṣaḥ atra dūṣyatām tayoḥ ca prāpya kāri tvam indriya tvāt tvac ādi vat ke cit tayoḥ śarīrāt ca bahis vṛttim pracakṣate cikitsā ādi prayogaḥ ca yaḥ adhiṣṭhāne prayujyate 
SV_4.45cd–4.48cd	 saḥ api tasya eva saṃskāraḥ ādheyasya upakārakaḥ tad deśaḥ ca api saṃskāraḥ sarva vyāpti arthaḥ ucyate cakṣuḥ ādi upakāraḥ ca pāda ādau api dṛśyate tasmāt na ekāntataḥ śakyam saṃskārāt tatra vartanam bahis vṛttiḥ tayoḥ ceṣṭā pṛthu agrā santatā api ca adhiṣṭhāna adhikam tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam pṛthutvam vṛtti bhāge syāt dūre api grahaṇam tathā 
SV_4.49ab–4.52ab	 dīpa prabhā yathā tasmin vinaśyati vinaśyati tathā bahis gatā api eṣā mūla= chedāt vinaśyati adhiṣṭhāna pidhāne tu sati api ucchinna yatnayā tayā arthaḥ anupanīta tvāt ātmanā na anubhūyate vicchinnaḥ iti buddhiḥ syāt adhiṣṭhānam apekṣya ca śabde tu ādhikya vicchedau bhrāntyā eva uktau asambhavāt puruṣa indriya śabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau 
SV_4.52cd–4.55cd	 puruṣaḥ laukikaḥ vā syāt yaḥ vā asmin sādhayiṣyate vikriyāḥ jñāna rūpā asya na nitya tve virotsyate buddhi janma iti ca api āha jāyamāna pramāṇa tām vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇām hi dṛṣṭaḥ janma atirekataḥ pramāṇe api tathā mā bhūt iti janma vivakṣyate na hi tat kṣaṇam api āste jāyate vā aprama ātmakam yena artha grahaṇe paścāt vyāpriyeta indriya ādi vat 
SV_4.56ab–4.59ab	 tena janma eva viṣaye buddheḥ vyāpāraḥ iṣyate tat eva ca pramā rūpam tadvatī karaṇam ca dhīḥ janma ca avyatirekeṇa bhāṣya kāreṇa varṇitam tat ca bhūta bhaviṣyat tvāt kṛtam buddheḥ viśeṣaṇam yadā api aulūkya siddhāntāt samavāyasya janma tā buddhiḥ tatra indriya adhīnā tena pratyakṣam aśnute pramāṇa phala bhāvaḥ ca yayā iṣṭam parikalpyatām 
SV_4.59cd–4.62cd	 sarvathā api animitta tvam vidyamāna upalambhanāt yat vā indriyam pramāṇam syāt tasya vā arthena saṅgatiḥ manasaḥ vā indriyaiḥ yogaḥ ātmanā sarve eva vā tadā jñānam phalam tatra vyāpārāt ca pramāṇa tā vyāpāraḥ na yadā teṣām tadā na utpadyate phalam na ca sarva ātmanā akṣeṇa sambandhaḥ arthasya vidyate yena sarva artha bodhaḥ syāt tad pramāṇa abhidhāyinām 
SV_4.63ab–4.66ab	 prāpti mātram hi sambandhaḥ na indriyasya abhyupeyate mā bhūt kāraṇa mātreṇa tvacā rūpa avadhāraṇam yathā pramāṇa niṣpattau yogya tvāt indriya arthayoḥ niyatā saṅgatiḥ hetuḥ phale api evam bhaviṣyati yogasya dvi āśraya tve api bhavati anyatara āśrayaḥ vyapadeśaḥ atha vā api akṣam tatra asādhāraṇam bhavet saṃyoge tu ātma manasoḥ syāt ced viṣaya bhinna tā 
SV_4.66cd–4.69cd	 pramāṇa phalayoḥ na asau arthe hi vyāpṛtam dvayam atha api āśraya iṣṭaḥ te na yogāt viṣaya antaram ātma stha tvena vijñānam na bhinna viṣayam tatas prakṛṣṭa sādhana tvāt ca pratyāsatteḥ saḥ eva naḥ karaṇam tena na anyatra kārake syāt pramāṇatā pramāṇe sarva saṃyoge doṣaḥ na ekaḥ api vidyate pramāṇam tu indriyam yasya tasya ekaḥ viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ 
SV_4.70ab–4.73ab	 pramāṇa phalate buddhyoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ yadā tadā api pūrva uktā bhinna artha tva nirākriyā viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocana mātrakam prasūte niścayam paścāt tasya prāmāṇya kalpanā niścayaḥ tu phalam tatra na asau ālocite tadā tadā na eva pramāṇa tvam syāt artha anavadhāraṇāt hāna ādi buddhi phala tā pramāṇam ced viśeṣya dhīḥ 
SV_4.73cd–4.76cd	 upakāra ādi saṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaḥ ced iyam phalam viṣaya eka tvam icchan tu yaḥ pramāṇam phalam vadet sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhedaḥ laukikaḥ tena bādhitaḥ chedane khadira prāpte palāśe na cchidā yathā tathā eva paraśoḥ loke cchidayā saha na ekatā bhavate bheda hānena rucitā viṣaya eka tā tad tyāgena parebhyaḥ tu bhedaḥ rucim upāgataḥ 
SV_4.77ab–4.80ab	 karaṇa tva upacāraḥ tu phale ced kalpyate tvayā kathan cit viṣaya eka tvam paraiḥ vā kim na kalpyate pariccheda phala tvena vṛttasya anantarasya naḥ pramāṇa tvam bhavet jñāne pramāṇe tu param phalam sva saṃvitti phala tvam tu tad niṣedhāt na yujyate pramāṇe viṣaya ākāre bhinna artha tvāt na yujyate su a ākāraḥ ca sva saṃvittim muktvā na anyaḥ pratīyate 
SV_4.80cd–4.83cd	 prāmāṇyam yasya kalpyeta sva saṃvitti phalam prati su a ākārasya paricchedaḥ na ca ākāra antarāt vinā tasya api evam tathā ca syāt na ākāra antaḥ kadā canaḥ na ca asan cetitaḥ sattām su a ākāraḥ pratipadyate grāhye ca viṣaya ākāre grāhakaḥ anyaḥ na labhyate manasaḥ tu indriya tvena pratyakṣāḥ dhīḥ sukha ādiṣu manasā samprayuktaḥ hi tāni ātmā pratipadyate 
SV_4.84ab–4.87ab	 sambaddham vartamānam ca grahyate cakṣuḥ ādinā sāmānyam vā viśeṣaḥ vā grāhyam na atas atra kalpyate lakṣaṇam yat ca yaiḥ uktam pratyakṣe laukike sati vidyamāna upalambhii tvāt sarvasya eva animitta tā nirvikalpaka pakṣe tu sutarām animitta tā sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ na avikalpya hi gṛhyate katham pratyakṣa pūrva tvam anumāna ādi naḥ bhavet 
SV_4.87cd–4.90cd	 yadā smṛtya samartha tvāt nirvikalpa indriyasya dhīḥ na ca avikalpya liṅgasya liṅgi sambandhayoḥ tathā gṛhītiḥ upamāne api sādṛśya grahaṇāt smṛteḥ arthāpattiḥ punar prāyas na anya dṛṣṭe arthaḥ iṣyate pravartate ca yam dṛṣṭvā saḥ api arthaḥ sa vikalpakaḥ yatra ca anumitam liṅgam sūrya gati ādi liṅgi ca tatra pratyakṣa pūrva tvam katham adhyavasīyate 
SV_4.91ab–4.94ab	 pratyakṣa avagate ca arthe kutas teṣām pramāṇatā taiḥ yadā sa pratīyeta tadā na akṣasya gocaraḥ atha kasya cit arthasya jñānāt tat pūrva tā bhavet tadā arthasya bhaviṣyat tvam na syāt ajñāna kāraṇam vartamāne hi kasmin cit vijñāte arthe akṣa buddhibhiḥ liṅgāt avidyamānaḥ api dharmaḥ gamyeta taiḥ tadā pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca varṇān vede api gṛhyate 
SV_4.94cd–4.97cd	 prameyam iti saḥ api syāt tad pūrva tvāt akāraṇam ke cit tat pūrvaka tvam tu hetuḥ na eva iti manvate tad pūrvaka tvāt yat tāvat prāmāṇyam tad asambhavaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca liṅga ādi anyatamam dhruvam pravṛttiḥ anumāna ādeḥ na ca dharme asti tādṛśam anumāna anumāna ādeḥ na ca api asti iha sambhavaḥ sambandha liṅgi liṅgānām pūrva siddheḥ asambhavāt 
SV_4.98ab–4.101ab	 sattā ca na anumānena kasya cit pratipadyate dharmeṇa anyat viśeṣyam ced pakṣaḥ asiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ tasmāt adṛṣṭa pūrva tvāt kena cit vastunā saha dharmasya na anumeya tvam asādhāraṇa vastu vat adṛṣṭa sadṛśa tvāt ca svyam ca anupalambhanāt dharmasya na upameya tvam asādhāraṇa vat bhavet nanu arthāpattiḥ evam syāt jagat vaicitrya darśanāt 
SV_4.101cd–4.104cd	 sukhi duḥkha ādi bhedaḥ hi na adṛṣṭāt kāraṇāt ṛte dṛṣṭasya vyabhicāri tvāt tad abhāve api sambhavāt sevā avyayana tulya tve dṛṣṭā ca phala bhinna tā syāt evam yadi śakyeta svābhāvika nivāraṇāḥ karma śakteḥ ca vaicitrye hetuḥ anyaḥ bhavet yadi yathā ca phala vaicitrye karmaṇām śakta tā svatas tathā ca citra tā loke svabhāvāt upapatsyate 
SV_4.105ab–4.108ab	 adharme dharma rūpe vā hi avibhakte phalam prati kim api asti iti vijñānam narāṇām kva upayujyate kim nu yāgāt itas dukham hiṃsā ādeḥ kim sukha udbhavaḥ svarga putra ādi bhedaḥ ca kīdṛśāt karma bhedataḥ iti yāvat avijñānam tāvat na eva pravartate pravṛtti aṅgam ca yat jñānam tasya mūlam pratīkṣyate tasmāt siddhe api sāmānye viśeṣaḥ na āgamāt ṛte 
SV_4.108cd–4.111cd	 viśeṣasya tu jijñāsā sūtrakāreṇa sūtritāḥ gamyamāne viśeṣe ca tad antar bhāva kāritaḥ sāmānya pratyayaḥ api syāt śāstrāt eva iti akāraṇam yathā artha āpattiḥ evam ca na anumāna upamā iṣyate śāstram ced tad apekṣeta tasya eva syāt pramāṇatā pratyakṣa agrahaṇam yat tu liṅga ādeḥ avikalpanāt tat na iṣṭa tvāt vikalpasya api artha rūpa upakāriṇaḥ 
SV_4.112ab–4.115ab	 asti hi ālocanā jñānam prathamam nirvikapakam bāla mūka ādi vijñāna sadṛśam śuddha vastu jam na viśeṣaḥ na sāmānyam tadānīm anubhūyate tayoḥ ādhāra bhūtā tu vyaktiḥ eva avasīyate mahā sāmānyam anyaiḥ tu dravyam sat iti ca ucyate sāmānya viṣaya tvam ca pratyakṣasya evam āśritam viśeṣāḥ tu pratīyante sa vikalpaka buddhibhiḥ 
SV_4.115cd–4.118cd	 te ca ke cit pratidravyam ke cit bahuṣu saṃśritāḥ tān akalpayat utpannam vyāvṛtta anugata ātmanā gavyaśve ca upajātam tu pratyakṣam na viśiṣyate tat ayuktam pratidravyam bhinna rūpa upalambhanāt na hi ākhyātum aśakya tvāt bhedaḥ na asti iti gamyate nirvikalpaka bodhe api dvi ātmakasya api vastunaḥ grahaṇam lakṣaṇa ākhyeyam jñātrā śuddham tu gṛhyate 
SV_4.119ab–4.122ab	 na ca asādhāraṇa tvena para vyāvṛttya kalpanāt viśeṣa anugama ākpteḥ sāmānyam iti na api tat tatas param punar vastu dharmaiḥ jāti ādibhiḥ yayā buddhyā avasīyate sā api pratyakṣa tvena sammatāḥ karaṇam ca indriyam buddheḥ na tatra jñānam āhitam tatas smṛtya samartha tvāt vikalpaḥ atas na vāryate ātmani eva sthitam jñānam sa hi boddhā atra gamyate 
SV_4.122cd–4.125cd	 smaraṇe ca asya sāmarthyam sandhāna ādau ca vidyate tena indriya artha sambandhe vicyamāne smaran api vikalpayan svadharmeṇa vastu pratyakṣavān naraḥ tat ca etat indriya adhīnam iti taiḥ vyapadiśyate tad asambandha jātam tu na eva pratyakṣam iṣyate punar punar vikalpe api satī jātiḥ pratīyate tad sambandha anusāreṇa sarvam pratyakṣam iṣyate 
SV_4.126ab–4.129ab	 na hi praviṣṭa mātrāṇām uṣṇāt garbhagṛha ādiṣu arthāḥ na pratibhānti iti gṛhyante na indriyaiḥ punar yathā tu ābhāsa mātreṇa pūrvam jñātvā svarūpataḥ paścāt tatra avabudhyante tathā jāti ādi dharmataḥ yadi tu ālocya saṃmīlya netre kaḥ cit vikalpayet na syāt pratyakṣatā tasya sambandhān anusārataḥ asambaddha vikalpe api tulyam ātma ādi kāraṇam 
SV_4.129cd–4.132cd	 tena asādhāraṇa tvam syāt atra akṣasya eva kalpane nirvikalpaka bodhe api na akṣam kevala kāraṇam tad pāramparya jāte vā rūḍhiḥ syāt paṅkaja ādi vat animittā eva vā rūḍhiḥ sutarām sa vikalpakam pratyakṣam sammatam loke na tathā nirvikalpakam vṛddha prayoga gamyāḥ ca śabda arthāḥ sarve eva naḥ tena yatra prayuktaḥ ayam na tasmāt apanīyate 
SV_4.133ab–4.136ab	 siddha anugama mātram hi kartum yuktam parīkṣakaiḥ na sarva loka siddhasya lakṣaṇena nivartanam kalpanāyāḥ sva saṃvittau indriya adhīna tā katham manaḥ tatra indriyam ced syāt go tva ādau api tad samam sva saṃvittau tat iṣṭam ced lokaḥ na hi evam icchati tasmāt rūḍha tvam eṣṭavyam pāribhāṣika tā api vā manasaḥ tu indriya tvena sudha duḥkha ādi buddhiṣu 
SV_4.136cd–4.139cd	 yathā pratyakṣata evam naḥ tad adhīnā bhaviṣyati tad adhīna tva sāmye api kalpanā apoḍha śabdanāt pratyakṣam kiñ cit eva iṣṭam yathā tatra tathā eva naḥ liṅga ādi abhāvataḥ ca api na anumāna ādi dhīḥ iyam bādhaka pratyaya asattvāt na aprāmāṇyam ca yujyate na ca parvam adṛṣṭa tvāt smṛti tvam upapadyate tasmāt pratyakṣam eva idam vyavahāraḥ tathā eva ca 
SV_4.140ab–4.143ab	 jāti ādi artha antaram yasmāt atad rūpe api vastuni bhavati adhyasya dhīḥ tasmāt mṛgatṛṣṇā ādibhiḥ samāḥ na etat aśva ādi buddhīnām adhyāra upādya sambhavāt sthitam na eva hi jāti ādeḥ paratvam vyaktitaḥ hi naḥ yadi hi ekāntataḥ bhinnam viśeṣyāt syāt viśeṣaṇam sva anurūpām sadā buddhim viśeṣye janayet katham sphaṭika ādau tu lākṣā ādi svarūpā yā matiḥ bhavet 
SV_4.143cd–4.146cd	 avyutpannasya sā mithyā vyutpannānām hi bheda dhīḥ na tu jāti ādi nirmuktam vastu dṛṣṭam kadā cana tad vimokena vā tāni lākṣā ādi sphaṭika ādi vat tatra api ced na dṛśyeta bhedaḥ kaiḥ cit kadā canaḥ rakta ādi buddhi samyaktvam vinivāryeta kena vā na ca api ayuta siddhānām sambandhi tvena kalpanā na aniṣpannasya sambandhaḥ niṣpattau yuta siddha tā 
SV_4.147ab–4.150ab	 tathā ca sati sambandhe hetuḥ kaḥ cit na vidyate tasmāt ca api na sambandhaḥ padārthānām pratīyate samavāya viyogāt ca viśleṣaḥ syāt parasparam tad kptau= avyavasthā syāt tasya tasya anya saṅgateḥ atha tasya ātma rūpa tvāt na anya sambandha kalpanā abhedāt samavāyaḥ astu svarūpam dharma dharmiṇoḥ na hi sa vyatiriktaḥ san sambandham pratipadyate 
SV_4.150cd–4.153cd	 tasmin tābhyām abhinne tu na nānātvam tayoḥ bhavet nanu dharma atirekeṇa dharmiṇaḥ anupalambhanāt tad saṅgha mātraḥ eva ayam gavādiḥ syāt vana ādi vat āvirbhāva tirobhāva dharmakeṣu anuyāyi yat tad harmi yatra vā jñānam prāc dharma grahaṇāt bhavet atas jāti ādi rūpeṇa dharmi yat gṛhyate naiḥ pārarūpyam na tasya asti iti aprāmāṇyam na yujyate 
SV_4.154ab–4.156cd	 yasya api vyatirekaḥ syāt dharmebhyaḥ dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭaḥ nityam tasya api tādrūpyāt na mithyātvam prasajyate yaḥ hi asat rūpa saṃvedyaḥ saṃvedyetān yathā punar sa mithyā na tu tena eva yaḥ nityam avagamyate na ca aneka indriya grāhyam bhinna tām pratipadyate mā bhūt bhinna śarīra stha grāhya tvāt bhinna rūpa tā 
SV_4.157ab–4.160ab	 jātya bhedāt abhedaḥ ced indriya tvena tad samam tulya buddheḥ atas bhinnā na satta indriya bhedataḥ buddhi bhedāt ca na ekatvam rūpa ādīnām prasajyate eka aneka tvam iṣṭam vā sattā rūpa ādi rūpataḥ kva cit ca saṅkarāt na akṣam ekam iti avasīyate dārḍhya daurbalya bhedena vyavasthā api yatas kva cit yathā hi manasaḥ sārdham rūpa ādau cakṣuḥ ādinā 
SV_4.160cd–4.163cd	 pravṛttiḥ sukha duḥkha ādau kevalasya eva dṛśyate na kva cit saṅkara abhāvāt sarvatra eva nivartate kva cit ca saṅkaram dṛṣṭvā saṅkaraḥ anyatra kalpyate śrotra ādeḥ upaghāte api śabda ādi smṛti darśanāt vartamānasya ca ajñānāt vyavasthā sampratīyate ekam yadi bhavet akṣam sarvaiḥ gṛhyeta vā na vā kalpyate śakti bhedaḥ ced śaktiḥ eva indriyam bhavet 
SV_4.164ab–4.167ab	 śṛṇuyāt badhiraḥ śabdam saṅkare cakṣuḥ ādinā manasaḥ vā svatantra tve vartamāna artha buddhiṣu na smaret badhiraḥ śabdam śrotram ced smṛti kāraṇam smṛti vat vā bhavet asya vartamāna artha dhīḥ api smṛtiḥ ca na bhavet paścāt gṛhṇīyāt tat na ced manaḥ śrotra grahaṇa velāyām na ca asarvā smṛtiḥ bhavet bodha ātmaka tayā puṃsaḥ sarvatra grahaṇam bhavet 
SV_4.167cd–4.170cd	 yugapad viṣaye api asya karaṇa apekṣitāḥ na ced tasmāt jñāna anusāreṇa vyavasthā saṅkarau kva cit grāhya grāhaka śaktibhyaḥ kārya dvāreṇa kalpitau cakṣū rūpa ādi bhedaḥ tu pañcadhā eva vyavasthitaḥ tena nīla ādi bhede api na indriya ānantya kalpanā tasmāt pañcabhiḥ api akṣaiḥ bodhaḥ sattā guṇa tvayoḥ dravya mūrtau punar dvābhyām rūpa ādau ekaśas sthitaḥ 
SV_4.171ab–4.174ab	 nanu jāti ādi rūpe api śabda abheda upacārataḥ pravartamānā mithya syāt buddhiḥ rūpeṣu buddhi vat na śabda abheda rūpeṇa buddhiḥ artheṣu jāyate prāk śabdāt yādṛśī buddhiḥ śabdāt api hi tādṛśī nanu go tva ādi rūpeṇa gavā ākāra ādi buddhayaḥ na prāk śabda artha sambandha jñānāt santi kadā canaḥ jāti ādeḥ tad svarūpam ced aśabda jñaḥ api lakṣayet 
SV_4.174cd–4.177cd	 anvaya vyatirekābhyām śabda rūpa tva niścayaḥ yathā rūpa ādayaḥ bhinnāḥ prāk śabdāt sva ātmanā eva tu gamyante tadvat eva etat saṃjñi tvam kevalam param na ca avikalpitaḥ śabdāt iti vācyaḥ na gṛhyate tena agṛhīta śabdaḥ api go tva ādīn pratipadyate śruti saṃsparśa bodhe api go tva ādīn pratipadyate vivekāt artha śabdānām cakṣuḥ śrotra dhiyā kṛtāt 
SV_4.178ab–4.181ab	 ananta dharmake dharmiṇī eka dharma avadhāraṇe śabdaḥ abhyupāya mātram syāt na ātma adhyāra upakāraṇam na ca upeye abhyupāyasya rūpa adhyāsaḥ prasajyate na hi dīpa indriya ādīnām rūpa adhyāropaḥ iṣyate nityam yadi ca go tva ādi śabda rūpeṇa gṛhyate rūpa antaram na dṛṣṭam ced bheda adhyāsau kutas nu imau yadi abhedaḥ na mithyātvam bhedaḥ ced syāt svarūpataḥ 
SV_4.181cd–4.184cd	 na adhyāra upaprasaṅgaḥ syāt bhrāntyā tu adhyāsa kalpanā śabdena eva ca nirdeśaḥ gṛhīte arthe avakalpate gauḥ iti eva ca nirdeśaḥ vācya tad buddhi vādinām nirdeśa tulya tāyām ca śrotrāḥ vaktṛ svarūpa tā śabda jñāna prameyeṣu vijñānasya avasīyate bhrānti hetu samāna tve api upāya tvāt mati śrutī manyate arthe samadhyaste na artha adhyāsam tayoḥ punar 
SV_4.185ab–4.188ab	 go tve sāsnādi mat rūpa aṅga ādi rūpa abhidhāyake nirākāra ubhaya jñāne saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ yadi ca abheda rūpeṇa śabdena arthaḥ pratīyate eka rūpa tvam akṣa ādau devana ādeḥ prasajyate syāt anakṣa nivṛtyā ced na prāk śabdāt pratīyate gavā ādiṣu api tulyam ced neka rūpasya darśanāt traye bibhītaka ādīnām na eka dharma anvayaḥ asti hi 
SV_4.188cd–4.191cd	 śabdaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ teṣām jāti śabdāt vilakṣaṇaḥ paraspara vibhinnam tu jñāyate atra ākṛti trayam tad adhyāse na yujyeta tad rūpasya avibhāgataḥ bhinnāḥ syuḥ akṣa śabdāḥ ced na arthe saṃśaya darśanāt na sāmānyāt ṛte sa syāt rūpa abhedaḥ ca gamyate bhavati ādau ca bhinne api nāma ākhyāta tva saṃjñayā rūpa eka tvena ca adhyāse tulya artha tvam prasajyate 
SV_4.192ab–4.195ab	 śabda niṣpatti abhedāt ca tiṅanta arthasya sādhya tā katham katham ca mūrta arthaḥ vācake mūrti varjite gavā aśva śukla śabda ādeḥ vācya rūpa anapekṣaṇe vācaka tva vyavasthānam katham jāti guṇa ādiṣu vṛkṣa plakṣa ādi śabdānām tulye bhede ghaṭa ādibhiḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvam katham artha anapekṣayā sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca na syat vācaka buddhi vat 
SV_4.195cd–4.198cd	 ekatra ca upasaṃhāraḥ na buddhyoḥ nirvikalpake vastu mātre sa ced evam sarveṣām ekavācya tā bhavet gavā ādi śabdānām sarvaiḥ vastu hi gamyate na ca asādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalam iti iṣyate na hi śabda pravṛttiḥ syāt anyatra anyatra ca iṣyate na ca nīlotpalam nāma vastu ekam kiñ cit iṣyate śabda arthayoḥ yatas bhedaḥ gamyate avayava anugaḥ 
SV_4.199ab–4.202ab	 śabda dvayasya ca adhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣu api dṛśyate eka adhikaraṇāḥ tena syuḥ te nīlotpala ādi vat na ca anavagate pūrvam padam arthe prayujyate tatra sambandha velāyām kīdṛśaḥ arthaḥ pratīyate tadānīm na artha rūpe hi śabda rūpasya sambhavaḥ na ca asādhāraṇa aṃśena sambandha anugamaḥ kva cit tatra pūrva anapekṣa tve yadi ātma adhyāsa śakta tā 
SV_4.202cd–4.205cd	 śabdasya prathame api syāt śravaṇe adhyasta rūpa tā mama vācya anabhijña tvāt na bhavet smaraṇam tatas bhavataḥ tu artha rūpasya vācakeṣu api darśanāt yathā tu ajñāta śabdānām vācye tad dhīḥ na jāyate tathā eva ajñāta vācyānām upalabdhe api vācake tasmāt na atīva vācyānām vācaka adhīna tā bhavet smāraka tvāt ca teṣu eva pāratantryam pratīyate 
SV_4.206ab–4.209ab	 tena sambandha velāyām artha ātmā yaḥ avasīyate śabdāt api saḥ eva iti na artha rūpam praṇaśyati pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yām śabdaḥ kurute matim tādātmyam tasya śabdasya na kathan cit pratīyate kara hasta ādi śabdebhyaḥ śabda rūpasya bhedataḥ bhinnaḥ arthaḥ sampratīyeta tad adhyāra upakalpane ātma adhyāsaḥ tu sādṛśyāt uparāgāt ca dṛśyate 
SV_4.209cd–4.212cd	 na tāvat artha sādṛśyam śabdasya iha pratīyate na ca anurāgaḥ śabdena bhinna deśasya yujyate dūra stha pratibimbam ca na arūpasya pratīyate śabda sarva gata tvena yadi artha prāptiḥ ucyate sarva arthānām bhavet śabdaiḥ sarvaiḥ eva anurañjanam na ca bhinna indriya grāhyam kiñ cit asti anurāga kṛt na hi lākṣā anurakte api sphaṭike dhīḥ tvac ādibhiḥ 
SV_4.213ab–4.216ab	 anumāna āgamau mithyā syātām adhyāsa kalpane nirūpaṇasya mithyātvāt sarva abhāvaḥ prasajyate tathā as tu iti yadi brūyāt mithyā sva vacane sati katham evam vadet arthaḥ na anṛtāt dhi pratīyate śūnya vāda uttarāt ca api yathārtham buddhi śabdayoḥ pravṛttiḥ na tu tat tantram artha rūpam kadā canaḥ tasmāt prāk api ye śabdāt bhiḥ nna eka tva ādi buddhibhiḥ 
SV_4.216cd–4.219cd	 gṛhyante sarvadā teṣām parama artha stitāḥ bhavet śabda abhyupāyake api arthe tad abhāve ca yadi api artha buddhiḥ na jāyeta na arthe rūpam praṇaśyati cakṣuḥ ādeḥ abhāve hi rūpa ādi ātmā na gṛhyate svarūpa nāśaḥ rūpa ādeḥ tāvat mātreṇa na iṣyate sambandhasya ca nitya tvāt na arethasya syāt arūpa tā yugapad na hi sarveṣām anya ākāra artha vedanam 
SV_4.220ab–4.223ab	 tad ākāre api tadvat ced dvaye sati parīkṣyatām kim nu arthasya ātathā bhāvaḥ grahītuḥ kim nu aśakta tā sat asat bhāvayoḥ arthe virodhi tvāt asambhavaḥ grahītṛ bhedāt śakta tvam aśakta tvam ca yujyate yathā andhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasya iti abhidhāsyate tena arthe dhvani upāyasya tadhīrna ani asya jāyate devadatta ādi śabde tu sambandhāt yatva darśanāt 
SV_4.223cd–4.226cd	 arthasya anitya tāyām ca tādrūpyasya api anitya tā tatra api autpattikī śaktiḥ tad rūpa pratyayam prati grāhya grāhakayoḥ iṣṭā niyogasya tu anitya tā tatra sarvaiḥ atādrūpyam prāc niyogāt pratīyate tena iṣṭam eva mithyātvam kaiḥ cit adhyāsa kalpane yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvam śabdāt pratīyate tādṛśa smaraṇe hetuḥ śabdaḥ tatra yathārtha tā 
SV_4.227ab–4.230ab	 niyogāt paratas vā api śabdena vyajyatām iyam tad grāhya śaktiḥ arthasya pārarūpyam na tāvatā sarva ākāra paricchedya śakte arthe vācake api vā sarva ākāra artha vijñāna samarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ tatra śabda artha sambandham pramātuḥ smarataḥ api yā buddhiḥ pūrva gṛhīta artha sandhānāt upajāyate cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe arthe na apratyakṣam asau bhavet 
SV_4.230cd–4.233cd	 viviktāḥ eva te api arthāḥ smṛti pratyakṣa gocarāḥ smaryete śabda sambandhau mā bhūt pratyakṣa tā tayoḥ tad apratyakṣa bhāvena na tu arthasya api vāryate gṛhītam api go tva ādi smṛti spṛṣṭam ca yadi api tathā api vyatirekeṇ apūrva bodhāt pratīyate vyakti kāla ādi bhedena tatra asti avasaraḥ miteḥ yaḥ pūrva avagatom aśaḥ atra sa na nāma pramīyate 
SV_4.234ab–4.237ab	 idānīn tanam astitvam na hi pūrva dhiyā gatam na hi smaraṇataḥ yat prāk tat pratyakṣam iti īdṛśam vacanam rājakī iyam vā vaidikam vā api vidyate na ca api smaraṇāt paścāt indriyasya pravartanam vāryate kena cit na atas tat tadānīm praduṣyati tena indriya artha sambandhāt prāk ūrdhvam vā api yat smṛteḥ vijñānam jāyate sarvam pratyakṣam iti gamyatām 
SV_4.237cd–4.240cd	 vimanaskā yadā ke cit sambaddham api ca indriyaiḥ na budhyante tathā ca anye sādṛśya ādi vimohitāḥ tatra yaḥ artham vivekena kauśalāt sadṛśeṣu api sūkṣmam vā api prapadyeta tasya bhrāntiḥ nam tāvatā yathā ṣaḍja ādi bhedena gāne laukika vaidike vivekena avagacchanti yeṣām tad saṃskṛtā matiḥ gāna mātram vijānanti tatra anadhikṛtāḥ tu ye 
SV_4.241ab–4.244ab	 tad ajñānāt na mithyātvam vaktum śakyam vivekinām te hi ṣaḍja ādi śabdebhyaḥ vinā api eṣam viviktatām yathāvat adhigacchanti tadvat go tva ādivaḥ tu api saṅkīrṇam artha mātram tu budhyante abhyāsarva jitāḥ vivekam pratipadyante ye śabda smṛti saṃskṛtāḥ yathā rūpa ādim ati arthe yasya eva asti yat indriyam sa tanmātram gṛhītvā anyat na gṛhṇāti anumānataḥ 
SV_4.244cd–4.247cd	 tathā viveka hetūnām yadā yam pratipadyate tad upeye tadā jñānam vartate tad anugrahāt tena yāvat pramātāṇām viveka upāya darśanam na syāt tāvat bhavet teṣām vijñānam nirvikalpakam tasmāt yatra prakalpyeta vastu vastu antarātmanā pramāṇa ābhāsa tā tatra na svadharma vikalpane pratyakṣa tvam atas siddham sāmānyasya tathā eva ca 
SV_4.248ab–4.251ab	 sambandhasya iti tat pūrvam anumāna ādi jāyate sarvam ca api anumāna ādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake na pravartate iti etad anumāne abhidhāsyate nanu evam sati yā api agneḥ dūrāt api auṣṇya kalpanā sā api pratyakṣam eva syāt yathā go tva ādi buddhayaḥ pratyāsannataram go tvam pratyakṣa tvena sammatam vijñānam na anyat asti iti pratyakṣam idam eva naḥ 
SV_4.251cd–4.254cd	 tatra api akṣaiḥ asambandham manvānasya upajāyate yadā buddhiḥ tadā na eva pratyakṣa tvena kalpyate sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣa tvena jāyate tasmāt yat indriyam yasya grāhaka tvena kalpitam tena eva sati sambandhe pratyakṣam na anyathā bhavet evam samāne api vikalpa mārge yatra akṣa sambandha phala anusāraḥ pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vinā api adaḥ lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham 
SV_5,1.1ab–5,1.4ab	 pratyakṣa ādau niṣiddhe api nanu loka prasiddhitaḥ dharma adharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇa ādi viveka vat dhārmikā dhārmika tvābhyām pīḍā anugraha kāriṇau prasiddhau hi tathā ca āha pārāśaryaḥ atra vastuni idam puṇyam idam pāpam iti etasmin pada dvaye ācaṇḍālam manuṣyāṇām alpam śāstra prayojanam nirmūlā sambhavāt atra pramāṇaiḥ sā eva mṛgyate 
SV_5,1.4cd–5,1.7cd	 kutas punar pravṛttā iti pratyakṣa ādi tu vāritam na ca etāni parityajya pṛthak loke pramāṇatā saṃsāra mocaka ādeḥ ca hiṃsā puṇya tva sammatā na paścāt puṇyam icchanti ke cit evam vigānataḥ mleccha āryāṇām prasiddha tvam na dharmasya upapadyate na ca āryāṇām viśeṣaḥ asti yāvat śāstram anāśritam tad mūla artha prasiddhiḥ tu tad prāmāṇye sthite bhavet 
SV_5,1.8ab–5,1.11ab	 tasmāt abhāvaktra sthau dharma adarmau na śknuyāt codanā ced samuddhartum grastau tena eva paśyatām upadeśaḥ hi bhavati jñānam tasya iti yojyate jñāyate yena tat jñānam eka adhikaraṇa tvataḥ autpattika girā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate abādhaḥ anyatirekeṇa svatas tena pramāṇatā sarvasya anupalabdhe arthe prāmāṇyam smṛtiḥ anyathā 
SV_5,1.11cd–5,1.14cd	 codanā ca upadeśaḥ ca vidhiḥ ca eka artha vācinaḥ vākya antare samarthe api kim artham vidhiḥ āśritaḥ sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ sarva ākhyāteṣu vidyate sarva vākyeṣu ca ākhyātam tena ākāṅkṣā nivartanāt pravṛtti siddhiḥ icchātaḥ pratiṣedhāt tu varjanam vidhā= ana āśrite sāhdyaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ na labhyate śruta svarga ādi bādhena dhātu arthaḥ sādhya tām vrajet 
SV_5,1.15ab–5,1.18ab	 vidhau tu tam atikramya svarga ādeḥ sādhyateṣyate tad sādhanasya dharma tvam evam sati ca labhyate sva pratyaya antara apekṣā syāt anāpta nara uktiṣu āpta uktiṣu nara apekṣāḥ na ubhayam codanāsu naḥ ādi śabdaḥ makāra antaḥ luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ nañadhyāhriyate sūtre saṅkarāt paricodanā pramāṇa lakṣaṇa ajñānāt vyabhicārāt parīkṣaṇam 
SV_5,1.18cd–5,1.21cd	 na etat pratyakṣam iti evam aparīkṣā upasaṃhṛtā tatra anyasya ayathārtha tvam pratyakṣe tu yathārtha tā yadābhāsam hi vijñānam tad saṃyoge tat iṣyate sampūrṇam lakṣaṇam hi etat tad satoḥ vyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ śobhana arthaḥ tu sat śabdaḥ yat vā ākhyāhāra kalpanā arthāpattyā itareṣām ca pratyakṣa ābhāsa lakṣaṇam bādhaka jñāna lābhaḥ hi pūrva ābādhe na sambhavet 
SV_5,1.22ab–5,1.26cd	 sa ca asti iti avabodha tve sati na anyonya saṃśrayam na ca anāgata bādhe ca pūrveṇa ātmā hi labhyate nimitta doṣa bodhena paścāt yatra api abādhanam bhavati eva hi tatra api nara antara viparyayaḥ sarveṣām sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāt tatra na bādhanam na hi kāraṇa duṣṭa tva buddhiḥ tatra balīyasī jāti ādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścāt asambhavāt nāśyate yuktibhiḥ tatra vyaktam anyonya saṃśrayam svatas prāmāṇyataḥ ca atra nirṇayaḥ astitva bodhanāt tad rūpa pratyaya utpatteḥ tad asat vādinām api 
SV_5,3.1ab–5,3.4ab	 pramāṇa tva apramāṇa tve puṇya pāpa ādi tad phalam vidhi artha vāda mantra artha nāmadheya ādi kalpanā sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣu evam sva pramāṇa gaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ vacana vyakti bhedena pūrva siddhānta pakṣatā karmabhyaḥ phala sambandhaḥ pāralaukya aihalaukike sarvam ityādi ayuktam syāt artha śūnyāsu buddhiṣu tasmāt dharma arthibhiḥ pūrvam pramāṇaiḥ loka sammataiḥ 
SV_5,3.4cd–5,3.7cd	 arthasya sat asadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyām prati yadā saṃvṛti satyena sarvam etat prakalpyate jñāna mātre api kasmāt vaḥ vṛthā āgrahaḥ artha kalpane saṃvṛteḥ na tu satya tvam satyabhedaḥ kutas anvayam satyā ced saṃvṛtiḥ kā iyam mṛṣā ced satya tā katham satya tvam na ca sāmānyam mṛṣā artha parama arthayoḥ virodhāt na hi vṛkṣa tvam sāmānyam vṛkṣa siṃhayoḥ 
SV_5,3.8ab–5,3.11ab	 tulya artha tve api tena eṣām mithyā saṃvṛti śabdayoḥ vañcanā arthaḥ upanyāsaḥ lālā vaktra āsava ādi vat nāstikya parihāra aṛtham saṃvṛtiḥ kalpanā iti ca kalpanā api tu abhinnasya na eva nirvastuke bhavet tasmāt yat na asti na asti eva yat tu asti paramārthataḥ tat satyam anyat mithyā iti na satya dvaya kalpanā svapna ādi bhoga vat ca api yā upabhoga tva kalpanā 
SV_5,3.11cd–5,3.14ab	 tad nivṛtti artham eva iha parama arthe kaḥ cit pravartate na hi svapna sukha ādi artham dharme kaḥ cit pravartate yādṛcchika tvāt svapnasya tūṣṇīm āsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ parama aṛtha phala avāptim icchadbhiḥ tena yatnatas pratipattiḥ vidhātavyāḥ yuktibhiḥ bāhya vastuṣu tatra artha śūnyam vijñānam yoga ācārāḥ samāśritāḥ 
SV_5,3.14cd–5,3.17cd	 tasya api abhāvam icchanti ye mādhyamika vādinaḥ tatra bāhya artha śūnya tvam tulyam tāvat dvayoḥ api nivṛttya asya tatas jñāne tadvat saṃvṛti kalpanā tasmāt sādhāraṇa tvena tad mūla tvena ca api ayam bāhya artha sat asadbhāve yatnaḥ bhāṣya kṛtā kṛtāḥ bāhya artha apahnave advaitam eka arthasya parīkṣaṇāt pramāṇam āśritaḥ ca ekaḥ tatra āstām yaḥ prameyataḥ 
SV_5,3.18ab–5,3.21ab	 pramāṇa sthaḥ tu mūla tvāt iha idānīm parīkṣyate prastutaḥ sa dvidhā ca atra prathamam tu anumānataḥ pratyakṣa bādhane ca ukte paścāt tad śakti avekṣaṇāt tatra anumānam āha idam nanu iti asya ca saṅgatiḥ tad samprayoga jam nāma pratyakṣam iti bhāṣitam tatra indriya artha sambandha bhedaḥ na paramārthataḥ kalpitaḥ samprayogaḥ tu svapna ādau api vidyate 
SV_5,3.21cd–5,3.24ab	 tad atad yoga janyasya vibhāgaḥ tena durlabhaḥ mithyātvam yat dvidhā eva uktam na ayathā iti atra ca ucyate sarvasya eva ca mithyātve kim viśiṣya abhidhīyate stambha ādi pratyayaḥ miththayā pratyaya tvāt tathā hi yaḥ pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapna ādi pratyayaḥ yathā siddha sādhana bhāvaḥ aṃśe dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ eva ca 
SV_5,3.24cd–5,3.27cd	 mā bhūtām eva śabdaḥ ca vyaarthaḥ aśeṣa prasādhane sarve eva iti tena atra jāgrat buddhi parigrahaḥ sva aṃśa abhyupagamāt ca api bāhya grāhya nivāraṇam pratyayasya iti sādhya aṃśa vyāpta hetu nidarśanam hetuḥ ca upanyena atra jāgrataḥ api iti darśataḥ vipakṣa abhāvataḥ ca atra vyatirekaḥ na kathyate sāmānyasya ca hetu tvāt kasmāt pakṣa eka deśa tā 
SV_5,3.28ab–5,3.31ab	 jāgrat jñāne viśeṣaḥ ayam yatas su pariniścayaḥ bāhya ālambana sambandhaḥ na prasiddhaḥ param prati tasmāt yat bhāṣya kāreṇa dattam uttam atra tu vikalpa sama tā vā syāt vaidharmya sama tā api vā dṛṣṭa tvāt pūrva pakṣasya jāti ukti kaiḥ cit āśritāḥ pratijñā doṣam eva āhuḥ ke cit pratyakṣa bādhanam śakṣyāmaḥ yadi vispaṣṭam sva aṃśa grāhya nivāraṇam 
SV_5,3.31cd–5,3.34cd	 tadā te śuddhaḥ eva syāt pakṣaḥ grāhya nivāraṇaḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ ca viṣayaḥ bāhyaḥ eva avatiṣṭhate tad niṣedha kṛtaḥ tasya taiḥ bhavet pakṣa bādhanam su niścayena ca eteṣām bādhaka pratyayāt ṛte pramāṇa ābhāsa tā na asti iti etasmāt katyate balam duṣṭa jñāna gṛhīta apratiṣedhaḥ hi yujyate gṛhīta mātra bādhe tu sva pakṣaḥ api na sidhyati 
SV_5,3.35ab–5,3.38ab	 agrāhya tvāt ca bhedena viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ aprasiddha ubhaya tvam vā vācyam anyatarasya vā vaktṛ śrotroḥ ca yat jñānam viśeṣaṇviśeṣyayoḥ tad nirālambana tvena sva vāc bādhaḥ dvyoḥ api sambhavaḥ na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ tasmāt nirūpaṇam na asti pratijñā arthasya śobhanam nirālambanatā nāma na kiñ cit vastu gamyate 
SV_5,3.38cd–5,3.41ab	 tena yat vyatireka ādau praśnaḥ na eva upapadyate yadi avastu katham tu asmān tvam bodhayitum icchasi budhyase vā sva buddhyā tvam kalpitā tu atha sādhyate asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛś kptau vastu prasajyate katham iṣṭam abhāve ced vastu saḥ api iti vakṣyate tathā pratyayaḥ iti eṣa karma bhāva ādi vā bhavet 
SV_5,3.41cd–5,3.44cd	 bhāva ādiṣu virodhaḥ syāt karma ced siddha sādhanam pratyāyyasya hi rūpa ādeḥ nirālambanatā iṣyate avijñāna ātmaka tvena kiñ cit na ālambate hi asau kartṛ tve karaṇa tve vā pakṣa tvam śabdayoḥ api tad nirālambana tvena pakṣa abhāvaḥ prasajyate pratyāyyena ca bhinnena vinā kartṛ ādi asambhavaḥ pratyaye tad nimitte vā bādhaḥ sva vacanena te 
SV_5,3.45ab–5,3.48ab	 atha api rūḍhi rūpeṇa pratyayaḥ syāt tathā api tu grāhakam vastu siddham naḥ pratyayaḥ anyasya vastunaḥ tam abhyupetya pakṣaḥ ced abhyupetam virudhyate viśeṣyasya aprasiddhaḥ ca tava asmākam atādṛśe ātma dharma svatantra tva kalpane api tathā bhavet na ca pratyaya mātra tvam kiñ cit asti anirūpaṇāt śabda artha mātra rūpeṇa yathā anyeṣām nirūpaṇam 
SV_5,3.48cd–5,3.51cd	 tathā ca bhavataḥ na syāt vācya bhedam anicchataḥ nirālambanatā ca api sarvathā yadi sādhyate viśeṣaṇa aprasiddhiḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca na vidyate kena cit ced prakāreṇa nirālambanatā ucyate rasa jñānasya rūpa ādi śūnya tvāt siddha sādhanam atha buddhiḥ yat ākārā tad ālambana vāraṇam su a ākārasya abhyupeta tvāt tad abhāvaḥ virudhyate 
SV_5,3.52ab–5,3.55ab	 bāhya anālambana tve api bāhyaḥ iti agrahaḥ yadi stambha ādau na eva tad buddhiḥ iti evam siddha sādhanam atha stambha ādi rūpeṇa nirālambanatā ucyate saṃvedanasya dṛṣṭa tvāt tad virodhaḥ prasajyate dvi candra ādiṣu tulyaḥ ced na indriya aprāptitaḥ hi naḥ tatra anālambana uktiḥ syāt na artha saṃvitti abhāvataḥ sarvatra artha indriyāṇām naḥ saṃyoga sada sat tayā 
SV_5,3.55cd–5,3.58cd	 saṃvittau vidyamānāyām sadasat grāhikā sthitiḥ bhavataḥ tu indriya ādīnām abhāvāt grahaṇāt ṛte na ālambanasya hetuḥ syāt niṣedhaḥ atas na yujyate bahirbhāva aprasiddha tvāt tena anālambanā matiḥ kathan cit sādhyate na eṣa pakṣaḥ hi jñāyate tadā yathā anya bodhana aśakteḥ na aprasiddhe viśeṣaṇe pakṣa siddhiḥ tathā eva syāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaṇe 
SV_5,3.59ab–5,3.62ab	 na aprasiddhe padārthe hi vākya arthaḥ sampratīyate tad pūrvaka tvāt pakṣaḥ ca vākya arthaḥ sthāpayiṣyate paryudāse niṣedhe vā vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ prameya tva ādi abhedena jagataḥ siddha sādhanam yadi ca atyanta bhedena nirālambanatā ucyate kathan cit ced virudhyeta prākpakṣaḥ kalpitena vastu ādi ākārataḥ ca api dhīḥ nirālambaneṣyate
