SV_5,3.62cd–5,3.65cd	 grāhakāt ced abhinna tvam śakti bhedaḥ virudhyate nirālambana buddheḥ ca yadi utpattiḥ prasādhyate dṛṣṭa tvāt sa iṣyate asmābhiḥ bāhya grāhya vivarjitāḥ samyaktvam punar etasyāḥ tvam na icchasi kathan canaḥ ātma aṃśe avasitāḥ hi eṣā mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi buddhi vat caitra ādi pratyayānām ca nirālamba natā yadi dharma bhūtāḥ na gṛhyeta sādhana utthitayā dhiyā 
SV_5,3.66ab–5,3.69ab	 tatas viṣaya nānā tvāt pratiyogi anirākṛtāḥ rūpāt sa ālambana prāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate yadi pratyaya śabdaḥ api pratyaya tvena gṛhyate saṃvitti ālambana tvam ca vāryate siddha sādhanam buddhi utpādana śaktiḥ ced vāryā sādhayam na sidhyati sādhanasya prayogaḥ atra bodhaka tvāt vinā na te na ca abhidhā asti asambandhāt ṛte bhedāt ca na asti asau 
SV_5,3.69cd–5,3.72cd	 na ca asau tad gatam bhedam bodhayantya dhiyā vinā prāśnikaiḥ agṛhīte ca vākyasya avayave pṛthak pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini sādhanasya aprayogaḥ syāt abhyupetya ucyate yadi pūrva abhyupagamena eva pratijñā bādhyate tatas dharma adharma ādi bhede ca na asiddhe paramārthataḥ śiṣya ātmanoḥ ca dharma ādeḥ upadeśaḥ avakalpate 
SV_5,3.73ab–5,3.76ab	 tad anuṣṭhānataḥ buddheḥ iṣṭaḥ bhedaḥ sphuṭam ca taiḥ sūtra antare abhyupeta tvāt bhavet āgama bādhanam sarva loka prasiddhyā ca pakṣa bādhaḥ atra te dhruvam kṛtsna sādhana buddhiḥ ca yadi mithyā iṣyate tatas sarva abhāvaḥ yatheṣṭam vā nyūna tā vā abhidhīyate teṣām sa ālambana tve vā taiḥ anaikāntikaḥ bhavet tad anyasya pratijñā ced tad anya pratyayaḥ mṛṣā 
SV_5,3.76cd–5,3.79cd	 tad mithyā tva prasaṅge ca sarvam pūrva na sidhyati stambha ādi sādhana jñāna bhedaḥ na hi tathā bhavet yāvat yāvat pratijñā iyam tad angasya pratīyate tāvat tāvat pareṣām syāt mithyātvāt anya bādhanam viruddha avi abhicāri tvam bādhaḥ vā api anumānataḥ ittham sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyam pratisādhanam bāhya artha ālambanā buddhiḥ iti samyak ca dhīḥ iyam 
SV_5,3.80ab–5,3.83ab	 bādhaka apeta buddhi tvāt yathā svapna ādi bādha dhīḥ sā api mithyā iti ced brūyāt svapna ādīnām abādhanāt tasmāt sādharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavataḥ sādhane na hi vijñāna astitva bhinna tva kṣaṇika tva ādi dhīḥ tathā samyak ced abhyupeyeta tadā anaikāntikaḥ bhavet tat mithyā abhyupapattau ca pakṣa bādhaḥ prasajyate tathā ca baddham ukta ādi vyavasthā na prakalpate 
SV_5,3.83cd–5,3.86cd	 tatas ca mokṣa yatnasya vaiphalyam vaḥ prasajyate vikalpa utpadyamānā ca jñāna astitva ādi dhīḥ yadi mṛṣeṣṭā na ca dṛṣṭā atra pramāṇa antarataḥ gatiḥ pramāṇa abhāvataḥ tena jñāna astitva ādi durlabham sarvam ca api asmad ādīnām mithyā jñānam vikalpanāt sānnidhya viprakṛṣṭa tve sattva asattve ca durlabhe mithyājñāna aviśeṣe api sāṃkhya ādi parivarjanāt 
SV_5,3.87ab–5,3.90ab	 bauddha darśanaḥ ekasmin pakṣapātaḥ na yujyate mṛṣātvam yadi buddheḥ syāt bādhaḥ kim na upalabhyate bādhāt vinā api tat ced syāt vyavasthā na prakalpate pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrat jñāne mṛṣā bhavet svapna ādi buddhiḥ asmākam tava bhedaḥ api kiṅkṛtaḥ na ca anyat pratiyogi asti jāgrat jñānasya śobhanam yad darśanena mithyātvam stambha ādi pratyayaḥ vrajet 
SV_5,3.90cd–5,3.93cd	 svapna ādi pratiyogi tvam sarva loka prasiddhitaḥ tadīya dharma vaidharmyāt bādhaka pratyayaḥ yathā yoginām jāyate buddhiḥ bādhikā pratiyoginī jāgrat stambha ādi buddhīnām tatas svapna ādi tulya tā prāptānām tām avasthām ca sarva prāṇabhṛtām api bādhaḥ ayam bhavitā tena siddhā sa pratiyogitā iha janmani keṣān cit na tāvat upalabhyate 
SV_5,3.94ab–5,3.97ab	 yogi avasthā gatānām tu na vidmaḥ kim bhaviṣyati yoginām ca asmādīyānām tvad ukta pratiyoginī tvad ukti viparītā vā bādha buddhiḥ bhaviṣyati īdṛś tve yogi buddhīnām dṛṣṭāntaḥ na tava asti ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ tu asmādīnām yaḥ gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate atha stambha ādi buddhīnām vadet sa pratiyogi tām bādhya tvam ca api buddhi tvāt mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi buddhi vat 
SV_5,3.97cd–5,3.100cd	 iṣṭam sa pratiyogi tvam mṛgatṛṣṇā ādi buddhibhiḥ tad ātmanā ca bādhya tvam grāhya antaratayā api ca bādhakaiḥ ca api anekāntaḥ tad anya tve ca pūrvavat mithyā adhī pratiyogi tvam svapna ādau iva te bhavet rāga ādi kṣaya yogi tva nimitta adhigatiḥ tathā yāvān viśeṣaḥ iṣṭaḥ ced sarva abhāvāt viruddha tā mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmba adhabuddhi vat 
SV_5,3.101ab–5,3.104ab	 vācyaḥ anumāna bādhaḥ vā yadi vā pratisādhanam pūrva sādhana doṣāḥ ca sandheyāḥ tasya ca adhunā sādhya abhedāt avācya tvāt hetoḥ na ubhaya siddha tā pratyaya tvam ca sāmānyam bhinna abhinnam na vidyate bhavataḥ atyanta bhinnam ca mad pakṣe api kathan canaḥ sārūpya anya nivṛttī ca na iti etat sādhayiṣyate tasmāt dhetuḥ na sāmānyam asti siddham dvayoḥ api 
SV_5,3.104cd–5,3.107cd	 viśeṣayoḥ ca hetu tvam pakṣa tad tulya saṃsthayoḥ na syāt anvaya hīna tvāt atad dharma tayā api ca na ca artha hīnā tad buddhiḥ hetu tvena bhaviṣyati āśraya asiddhi tā ca uktā viśeṣyasya aprasiddhitaḥ tathā hetoḥ viruddha tvam dṛṣṭānte sādhya hīna tā viśeṣaṇa aprasiddha tva vikalpena eva bodhite svapna ādi pratyaye bāhyam sarvathā na hi na iṣyate 
SV_5,3.108ab–5,3.111ab	 sarvatra ālambanam bāhyam deśa kālāni atha ātmakam janmani ekatra bhinne vā tathā kāla antare api vā tad deśaḥ vā anya deśaḥ vā svapna jñānasya gocaraḥ alāta cakre alātam syāt śīghra bhramaṇa saṃskṛtam gandharvanagare abhrāṇi pūrva dṛṣṭam gṛha ādi ca pūrva anubhūta toyam ca raśmi tapta ūṣaram tathā mṛga toyasya vijñāne kāraṇa tvena kalpyate 
SV_5,3.111cd–5,3.114ab	 dravya antare viṣāṇam ca śaśasya ātmā ca kāraṇam śaśaśṛṅga dhiyaḥ mauṇḍyam niṣedhe śirasaḥ asya ca vastu antaraiḥ asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ śūnyatā ādhiyaḥ kāraṇa tvam padārthānām asat vākya artha kalpane atyantān anubhūtaḥ api baddhyā yaḥ arthaḥ prakalpyate tasya utpattau kathan cit syuḥ pṛthivī ādīni kāraṇam 
SV_5,3.114cd–5,3.117cd	 eṣa pratyakṣa dharmaḥ ca vartamāna artha tā eva yā sannikṛṣṭa artha vṛttiḥ ca na tu jñāna antareṣu iyam katham utpādayet jñānam tatra āsan= ced kutas nu iyam arthasya avidyamānasya vijñāna utpatti aśakta tā bāhya ālamba natāyām nau vivādaḥ arthasya saṃnidhiḥ yadi na asti kim evam syāt asmad pakṣa nivartanam tasmāt yat anyathāsantam anyathā pratipadyate 
SV_5,3.118ab–5,3.121ab	 tad nirālambanam jñānam abhāva ālambanam ca tat bhāva antaram abhāvaḥ anyaḥ na kaḥ cit anirūpaṇāt bhavatā dvayam ati etat durnirūpam sa hetukam pratijñā doṣa vat ca api yojyā hetoḥ viruddha tā samasta vyasta dharma ādi svarūpa ādi viparyayāt dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ na hi eka vastuni tava sādhya aṃśa hetu aṃśa vyāpta dharma ādi sambhavaḥ 
SV_5,3.121cd–5,3.124cd	 ke cit vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ na asti iti api anuyuñjate tad abhāvāt avṛtteḥ ca na asti atra avasaraḥ tava vidhi rūpa pratijñāyām etat vaktum hi śkyate tatra avastu vipakṣe api prayogasya hi sambhavaḥ yasmin anitya tā na asti kārya tā api na vidyate tasmin yathā kha puṣpa ādau iti śakyam hi bhāṣitum atra tu avastu sādhya tvam vastunaḥ ca vipakṣatā 
SV_5,3.125ab–5,3.128ab	 tena syāt vyatirekaḥ asya vācyaḥ yaḥ ca api darśayet pratiṣedha dvayāt tena vidhiḥ eva pradarśitaḥ na ca śakyaḥ vidhiḥ vaktum vastuni asati kena cit evam sthite ca sarvajña niṣedha ādau iyam gatiḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ asāmarthyam tadīyasya asmad ādi vat vaidharmyā sambhave api etad anye tu āhuḥ adūṣaṇam vinā eva tad prayogeṇa hetuḥ aikāntikaḥ yatas 
SV_5,3.128cd–5,3.131cd	 sarvathā sat upāyānām vāda mārgaḥ pravartate adhikāraḥ anupāya tvāt na vāde śūnya vādinaḥ nanu sarvam bhavat siddham mayā idam sādhanam kṛtam kimartham tat asiddhyā tvam vikalpya atra āttha dūṣaṇam vipralipsuḥ iva aha evam kim artham nyāya vid bhavān na aśrauṣīḥ sādhana tvam kim prasiddhasya dvayoḥ api yaḥ api tāvat parāsiddhaḥ svayam siddhaḥ abhidhīyate 
SV_5,3.132ab–5,3.135ab	 bhavet tatra pratīkāraḥ svatas asiddhe tu kā kriyā tam sādhayan virundhyāt dhi pūrva abhyupagatam naraḥ asādhite tu sādhyaḥ arthaḥ na tena pratipadyate parāsiddhaḥ na paryāptaḥ pareṣām pratipattaye tena asādhana tā yuktāḥ svatas asiddhe tu kiṅkṛtā dvayoḥ siddhasya hetu tvam na adṛṣṭāya upadiśyate pratyeṣyanti sva siddhena sādhanena svayam yatas 
SV_5,3.135cd–5,3.138cd	 vadet katham asiddham ced iti anena api kim tava gṛhītam agṛhītam vā sādhyam vā sādhanā api vā mayā ucyate ced tu asiddham kim tvam na pratipadyase yatra syāt puruṣa adhīnā buddhiḥ tatra idam ucyate kutas asya pūrva vijñānam iti atretat na yujyate yadi ca evam bhavet atra pratijñā mātraḥ eva hi mad doṣa ajñāna mātreṇa pratipattiḥ bhavet tava 
SV_5,3.139ab–5,3.142ab	 yatas tu sādhana apekṣā tena asya eva pramāṇa tā tad smṛti utpatti mātre tu vākya vyāpāraḥ iṣyate tasmāt yathā eva sādhya aṃśa vyāpta hetu nidarśanāt sādhyam gṛhṇan na vaktāram apekṣeta tathā bhavān yat ca api bhavataḥ jñānam pratyaka ādiḥ kim atra te mad prasiddhā asti yuktiḥ vā sādhyam vā atra yathā icchasi tasmāt na viduṣām etat uttam yujyate yatas 
SV_5,3.142cd–5,3.145cd	 tava hetuḥ asiddhaḥ ayam mama tena na sādhanam satyam yadi mama eva atra pratipattiḥ phalam bhavet tadā tvad aprasiddhe api hetau mām prati hetu tā yadā tu jñāna mātra tva pratipattau bhavān mayā pṛṣṭaḥ kaḥ hetuḥ atra iti tadā evam na upapadyate svayam na hi agṛhītena mad prasiddhena vā bhavān hetunā sādhyam etat tu pratipannaḥ kathan canaḥ 
SV_5,3.146ab–5,3.149ab	 na ca vyāpriyate anyatra vacanam prāśnikān prati sva niścayāya yaḥ hetuḥ tasya eva pratipādanāt mad prasiddha tvam etasya kutas ca avagatam tvayā katham ca ittham vivakṣā te svayam artham ajānataḥ mayi jijñāsamāne api buddhi pūrva abhidhāyinaḥ iti jñātvā ca vaḥ vṛddhaiḥ bhāṣita ubhaya siddha tā tena yadvat mama etena tvam adhitsasi hetunā 
SV_5,3.149cd–5,3.152cd	 sādhya jñānam tathā eva aham ajñānam tava dūṣaṇaiḥ yathā eva ca bhavānīdṛś sādhyam uktvā asya sādhanam sādhya anurūpam ajñātvā vihataḥ pratipādanāt tathā eva pratipādyaḥ api tādṛś sādhya bubhutsayā manvānaḥ sādhanam duṣṭam tatas sādhyam na budhyate saṃvittyā sādhanam matvā tad sadbhāve dṛḍhe sthite sādhyasya asambhavāt eva tvad uktam na avabudhyate

SV_5,3.156cd–5,3.159cd	 katham pūrvam asau āsīt asan= ced sādhanam katham sādhanam ced avaśyam ca parama artha astitāḥ bhavet siddhiḥ na aparama arthena parama arthasya yujyate na dṛṣṭā śaśaśṛṅga ādeḥ samyak jñāna ādi hetu tā bāṣpa ādinā api adhūmena mithyā vahni ādi bodhanam tasmāt asatya hetoḥ yā parama arthe matiḥ tava sā api asatyāḥ na satyam hi satya ābhāsena gamyate 
SV_5,3.160ab–5,3.163ab	 ye api rekhā ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ varṇānām pratipādakāḥ na te svena api rūpeṇa parama artha tva varjitāḥ varṇa ātmanā na satyāḥ ced sarva bhāveṣu ayam vidhiḥ padārtha antara rūpeṇa na satyam kiñ cit iṣyate svarūpe vidyamāne tu yat api evam prakāśate sva rūpa abhāva kptau tu na satyam na api asatya tā hetu ādīnām tu bhavataḥ sva rūpeṇa api asatya tā

SV_5,3.177cd–5,3.180cd	 tvayā eva asmad abhipretā sva pakṣa asiddhiḥ āśritāḥ na ca asti vāsanā bhedaḥ nimitta asambhavāt tava jñāna bhedaḥ nimittam ced tasya bhedaḥ katham punar vāsanā bhedataḥ ced syāt prāptam anyonya saṃśrayam svacchasya jñāna rūpasya na hi bhedaḥ svatas asti te pramāṇam vāsanā astitve bhede vā api na vidyate kuryāt grāhaka bhedam sā grāhya bhedaḥ tu kiṅkutas

SV_5,3.198cd–5,3.202cd	 tasmāt saṃvṛti satyā eṣā kalpitā na asti tattvataḥ na ca īdṛśena bhavena kāryam utpadyate kva cit yasya tu avasthitaḥ jñātā jñāna abhyāsena yujyate sa tasya vāsanā ādhāraḥ vāsanā api saḥ eva vā kusume bījapūra ādeḥ yat lākṣa ādi upasicyate tad rūpasya eva saṃkrāntiḥ phale tasya iti avāsanāḥ yuktyā anupetām asatīm prakalpya yat vāsanām artha nirākriyā iyam āsthāni vṛtti artham avādi bauddhaiḥ grāham gatāḥ tatra kathan cit anye

SV_5,5.28ab–5,5.31ab	 jñāna pṛṣṭena yaḥ api ūrdhvam artha abhāve api parāmarśaḥ arthaḥ rūpasya sa katham vā upapadyate tad rūpam ārtham ālikhya yadi dhīḥ na upajāyate bhūta kāle ca yadi arthaḥ tat pūrvam na upalakṣitaḥ vaktāraḥ ca api dṛśyante varttamāna artha buddhiṣu nīlaḥ arthaḥ ayam yatas me atra tad rūpā jāyate matiḥ tasmāt pūrva gṛhītāsu buddhiṣu artha upalmbhanam 
SV_5,5.31cd–5,5.34cd	 na ca upalabdhiḥ asti ihi nirākārāsu buddhiṣu viveka buddhi abhāvāt ca sa ākārasya ca darśanāt ākāravat tayā bodhaḥ jñānasya eva prasajyate na hi evam kalpanā śakyā nirākārāt itas matiḥ gṛhyate arthaḥ tatas paścāt sa ākāraḥ sampratīyate ākāravat tva bhedaḥ hi jñātvā śakyeta bhāṣitum prāc buddhi grahaṇāt arthe saṃvittiḥ na iti sādhitam 
SV_5,5.35ab–5,5.38ab	 na ca artha ākāraḥ eva ayam jñāna ārūḍhaḥ pratīyate na hi saḥ antar praveśāya paryāptaḥ na artha hānaye ittham bhāve pramāṇam ca tasya vaktum na śakyate tadīya pratibimba tvam etasmāt eva na iṣyate niścandre bimba rūpam hi dṛṣṭam yena divā jalam sa rātrau khe ca tam dṛṣṭvā jānāti pratibimba tām vijñāne na kadā cit tu prāk nirākāra darśanam 
SV_5,5.38cd–5,5.41cd	 bāhye vā ākāravat tādhīḥ yena evam kalpanā bhavet śabda gandha rasānām ca kīdṛśī pratibimba tā jñāne ca gṛhyamāṇasya katham syāt artha dharmatā bāhya abhyantara deśa tvāt na ca artha jñānayoḥ mithas samparkaḥ asti yatas mohāt aviveka matiḥ bhavet asammūḍhasya ca adṛṣṭe na sammoha prakalpanā kalpyamāne atha vā api evam tat dvayoḥ avatiṣṭhate 
SV_5,5.42ab–5,5.45ab	 saṃsarga dhamaḥ ākāraḥ tasmāt eva na yujyate deśa bhedāt asaṃsargaḥ mūrā mūrta tayā tathā tailokyena prasaṅgāt ca saṃsargaḥ na eka kāla tā na ca api ārjavataḥ sthānam jñāne na arthasya vidyate sarvathā kalpanāyām ca cakṣuṣā api rasa ādayaḥ gṛhyeran sarva bhāvānām aṇu ākārāḥ ca tad gatāḥ na ca api viṣaya tvena sthāne saṃsarga kalpanā 
SV_5,5.45cd–5,5.48cd	 viṣaya tvam hi kīdṛś syāt prāc ākāra upalambhanāt na hi asañcetitaḥ bhāvaḥ viṣaya tvena kalpyate viṣaya tvāt tad ākāraḥ ākārāt viṣayaḥ ca saḥ dvayoḥ ākāra nirmuktam sattvam saṃsṛṣṭa tā tathā svarūpataḥ paricchidya vaktum ityādi yujyate na ca api asya iha sadbhāvaḥ prāk gṛhītaḥ na ca upari na hi ākāra vinirmuktam grāhyam asti iti bhāṣitam

SV_5,5.52cd–5,5.55cd	 hetu tvena upapannā iti sā eva jāgrat dhiyām api anvaya vyatirekābhyām evam jñānasya gamyate na hi bāhyasya jñāna apetaḥ nidarśyate bāhya apetaḥ mayā yadvat tasmāt saṃsargavāc iyam nirākāre api vijñāne vāsanāsu eva yujyate dvayoḥ api ekaḥ ākāraḥ iti etasya apramāṇa tā deśa bhedāt asaṃsargaḥ dvayoḥ ca anavadhāraṇāt 
SV_5,5.56ab–5,5.59ab	 evam eva artha buddhyoḥ syāt sādṛśyāt na avibhakta tā bhede jñāte hi sādṛśyam na ajñāte syāt kha puṣpa vat tathā dvi candra māyā ādau anyathā arthe vyavasthite yā syāt ākāra saṃvittiḥ na asau artha nibandhanāḥ nakṣatram tārakā tiṣyaḥ dārāḥ iti evamādiṣu na ekatra arthe viruddha tvāt liṅgāneka tva sambhavaḥ parivrāṭkāmukaśunām kuṇapa ādi matiḥ tathā

SV_5,5.66cd–5,5.69cd	 akṣa grahaṇa kāle tu grāhikā dhīḥ bhaviṣyati tasyām tu gṛhyamāṇāyām anyā dhīḥ grāhikā iṣyate nanu ātmā grāhakaḥ grāhyaḥ bhavatā abhyupagamyate kathañcid dharma rūpeṇa bhinna tvāt pratyayasya tat grāhaka tvam bhavet tatra grāhyam dravya ādi ca ātmanaḥ yaḥ tu na atyanta bhedaḥ atra kva vā asau iṣyate mayā pratyāsatti nimittā tu pratyagātma pravarttitā 
SV_5,5.70ab–5,5.73ab	 asmad prayoga sambhinnā jñānasya eva tu kartari bhavantī tatra saṃvittiḥ yujyeta api ātma kartṛkāḥ na ca atra karaṇa jñāna grāhaka ākāra vedanam grāhya tvam yena buddheḥ syāt abhinna tve api pūrvavat anya rūpā api saṃvittiḥ yadi anya viṣaya iṣyate jñāna ākārā api saṃvittiḥ kasmāt na arthasya kalpyate abhinna tvam yadā ca iṣṭam grāhya grāhaka vastunoḥ 
SV_5,5.73cd–5,5.76cd	 tadā anyatara saṃvittau dvi ākāram grahaṇam bhavet yadā tu grāhyam ākāram nīla ādi pratipadyate na tadā grāhaka ākārā saṃvittiḥ dṛśyate kva cit tasmāt abhinnatā ced syāt tasya api anubhavaḥ bhavet grāhyaḥ vā na anubhūyeta grāhakān anubhūti vat grāhaka grahaṇe api evam grāhya saṃvedanam bhavet śuddham eva nirākāram grāhakam saṃvid asti hi

SV_5,5.80cd–5,5.83cd	 bahis deśena sambandhaḥ na hetu tvāya kalpate tasmāt bahis iti iha idam niṣkṛṣṭam grāhaka aṃśataḥ saṃvedyam nīla pīta ādi pratyakṣa ādeḥ udāhṛtam na pūrvam jñāyate buddhiḥ iti atra etat vadiṣyate grāhakasya eva saṃvittiḥ lakṣyate grahaṇe kva cit na smarāmi mayā kaḥ api gṛhītaḥ arthaḥ tadā iti hi smaranti grāhaka utpāda grāhya rūpa vivarjitam

SV_5,5.159cd–5,5.162cd	 atītvā anuviddhaḥ hi smṛtyā grāhyaḥ anubhūyate tadvat eva bhavet atra svapne na syāt viparyayāt tatra hi avartamānaḥ api gṛhyate vartamāna vat bādha jñānāt idam bhrāntam na tu atra evam viparyayaḥ tasmāt pratyakṣa buddhīnām na atitaḥ viṣayaḥ bhavet atīta tvāt yathā eva āsām vṛttaḥ janma antareṣu yaḥ tad rūpa tvena vā jñānam hetuḥ bhāvi vat ucyate

SV_5,5.166cd–5,5.169cd	 kevala grāhaka tve tu viṣaya tvam na yujyate kim apekṣya ca tasya idam grāhaka tvam prakalpyate dvi ākāra tā nirastā eva saṃvedyeta tadā eva ca tatas ca uttara vijñānam na pratīkṣeta bodhakam dvi ākāra kalpanāyām ca parasya ātmā aṃśaḥ eva te pramāparyavasā anena na atītaḥ viṣayaḥ bhavet pūrva grāhya sarūpa tve grāhaka tvam prahīyate 
SV_5,5.170ab–5,5.173ab	 grāhaka ākāra mātre syāt viṣayaḥ nāsarūpataḥ na ca śakti arpaṇasya atra vyāpāraḥ upalabhyate śakti arpaṇasya ca abhāvaḥ yuṣmad pakṣe prasādhitaḥ santāna antara vat ca eṣām niṣedhyā hetu sādhya tā vāsya vāsaka bhāvaḥ ca jñāna tvāt eka santatau tasmāt yat bhāsakam rūpam tat grāhyāt tasya bhinna tā tad saṃvittau asaṃvitte rasa ādi grāhakam yathā 
SV_5,5.173cd–5,5.176cd	 grāhyam tat grāhakāt ca eva tad parāmṛśatā yatas na parāmṛśyate avaśyam rasa ādi grāhakam yathā dvayam paraspareṇa evam bhinnam sādhyam rasa ādi vat aika rūpyeṇa ca ajñānāt santāna antara buddhi vat jñānam sva aṃśam na gṛhṇāti jñāna utpatteḥ sva śakti vat grāhya tva pratiṣedhaḥ ca dvaya hīnāḥ hi vāsate caitra jñānam tad udbhūta jñāna aṃśa grāhya bodhakam 
SV_5,5.177ab–5,5.180ab	 jñāna tvāt na bhavet yadvat tasya deha antara udbhavam etayā eva diśā vācyā śakti dvaya nirākriyā pramāṇa antara siddha tvāt anyatra aneka śakti tā na tu atra kāraṇam tādṛś śakti bheda kṛt asti te tasmāt ubhaya siddha tvāt lāghavāt yaḥ parigrahaḥ upāya tvāt ca yat tasya pūrva grahaṇa kalpanam cakṣuḥ adīndriyaiḥ atra tat anaikāntikam bhavet 
SV_5,5.180cd–5,5.183cd	 yat api apratibaddha tvāt utpattau gṛhyatām iti tatra ātmanā na śaktyam tat na anya utpattiḥ tat asti vā tena etat kāraṇa abhāvāt tadānīm na anubhūyate na anyathā hi artha sadbhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ san= upapadyate jñānam ced na iti atas paścāt pramāṇam upajāyate na ca api apratibandhena kevalena grahaḥ bhavet viśiṣṭa kāraṇa abhāve api arthaḥ na eva anubhūyate 
SV_5,5.184ab–5,5.187ab	 vyāpṛtam ca artha saṃvittau jñānam na ātmānam ṛcchati tena prakāśaka tve api bodhāya anyat pratīkṣyate īdṛśam vā prakāśa tvam tasya artha anubhava ātmakam na ca ātmā anubhavaḥ asti asya iti ātmanaḥ na prakāśakam sati prakāśaka tve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā rūpa ādau cakṣuḥ ādīnām tathā atra api bhaviṣyati prakāśaka tvam bāhye arthe śakti abhāvāt tu na ātmani 
SV_5,5.187cd–5,5.190cd	 anyena vā anubhāve asau anavasthā prasajyate tatra tatra smṛtim dṛṣṭvā sarva anubhava kalpanā ekena tu anubhūta tve sarvam tatra eva sambhavet tatra api smṛtiḥ iti etat na loka anumatam vacaḥ na hi vijñāna santānam kaḥ cit smarati laukikaḥ ghaṭa ādau agṛhīte arthe yadi tāvat anantaram arthāpattyau abudhyante vijñānāni punar punar 
SV_5,5.191ab–5,5.194ab	 yāvat śramam tatas paścāt tāvatī eva smariṣyati tadā tu akalpite api evam smṛti varndhyā suta ādi vat smṛti bhrāntaḥ ca yā api atra paścāt jñāneṣu jāyate tadā eva artha smṛteḥ eṣām tajñāna ādi pramāṇa tā yāvat śramam ca tad buddhiḥ tad prabandhe mahati api śramāt rucya anya samparkāt vicchedaḥ viṣayeṣu iva tatra api smṛtiḥ iti eṣām prathame pratyaye yadi 
SV_5,5.194cd–5,5.197cd	 tanmātra grahaṇāt evam na anavasthā prasajyate smaraṇam tu atha sarveṣu tad siddhyai grahaṇam tathā pramāṇa vat tvāt āyātaḥ pravāhaḥ kena vāryate atha tāni ādya vijñāna viṣayāṇi iti kalpyate na uttarottara buddhīnām viśeṣaḥ upapadyate vijñāna viṣaya tvam ca yasya sarvāsu buddhiṣu ghaṭa vijñāna tajñāna viśeṣaḥ tena durlabhaḥ 
SV_5,5.198ab–5,5.200cd	 smaran yathā eva vijñānam nirākāram smarati ayam tathā smaran gṛhīta artham nirākāra tayā smaret jñāna pṛṣṭena yaḥ api ūrdhvam parāmarśaḥ bhavati asau tasya artheṣu abhyupāya tvāt na tu grāhya tva kāritaḥ pratyāsanna tva sambandhau grāhya tva asambhavāt cyutau viṣaya tvena vā api etau staḥ kim deśa avibhāgataḥ 
SV_5,5.201ab–5,5.204ab	 artha ākārasya yaḥ api uktaḥ mithyājñāneṣu asambhavaḥ dośa kālān yathāmātra sambhavaḥ keṣu cit kṛtaḥ pratyakṣāt anya vijñānam atīta anāgataiḥ api janyate arthe bhavantīṣu vāsanāsvasatīṣu vā yaḥ punar na anubhūtaḥ arthaḥ na vā api anubhaviṣyate vāsanā bhāvataḥ tatra tava api anubhavaḥ katham vinā api vāsanātas ced buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas 
SV_5,5.204cd–5,5.207cd	 vāsanāyāḥ nimitta tvam abhyupetam virudhyate vāsanā ced bhavet tatra sā ca saṃvitti pūrvikā tathā sati ca pūrvatra gṛhītaḥ kvāpi asau dhruvam evam ca na eva vaktavyam atyanta abhavanam kva cit anyathā anupapatyā hi siddhāḥ janma antare astitāḥ duṣṭa tvena ca vijñānam anyathā api vyavasthitam pṛthivī ādiṣu gṛhṇīyāt ākāram tad nibandhanam 
SV_5,5.208ab–5,5.210cd	 tāni apāsya tu na eva arthe kva cit ākāra kalpanā na jñānam hi anavaṣṭambham ātmānam labdhum arhati vijñānasya eva vā kāryam yadi eṣaḥ anye ca kalpitāḥ viśeṣaḥ kaḥ atra yena ayam atyanta āsan= itīṣyate tasmāt bhrāntiḥ api tu eṣām kalpayanti artham eva naḥ kalpayati anyathā santam na tu ātmānam vyavasyati 
SV_5,5.211ab–5,5.213cd	 tatas ca bādhaka jñānāt vācoyuktiḥ iyam bhavet arthe anyathā api sati eṣa dhiyākāraḥ pratīyate dvi candra ādi matiṣu evam tāraka ādimatau tathā strī tva adi anyatra dṛṣṭam syāt kathan cit vā iha sambhavet śabda mātra pratīyā vā dṛṣṭaiḥ vā kaiḥ cit iṅganāt saṃstyāna prasava sthānaiḥ yathā pātañjale mate 
SV_5,5.214ab–5,5.217ab	 tena liṅga trayasya atra sadbhāvaḥ syāt pramāṇavān apekṣā bhedataḥ ca atra virodhaḥ api na vidyate kuṇapa ādimatau ca evam sārvarūpye vyavasthite vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyaḥ vyavasthā ākāra darśane sva pratyaya anukāraḥ hi bahu ākāreṣu vastuṣu nirdhāraṇe bhavet dhetuḥ na apūrva ākāra kalpane tathā dīrgha ghaṭa tva ādau bhinna apekṣā nibandhanā 
SV_5,5.217cd–5,5.220cd	 ākāra bheda sampattiḥ aviruddhāḥ bhaviṣyati na aneka ākāra saṃvitteḥ nirākāra tva kalpanā yuktāḥ pratīti bhedāt tu bahu ākāra tva sambhavaḥ saṃvitteḥ ca viruddhānām ekasmin api sambhavaḥ eka ākāram bhavet ekam iti na īśvara bhāṣitam tathā eva tad upetavyam yat yathā eva upalabhyate na ca api aikāntikam tasya syāt eka tvam ca vastunaḥ 
SV_5,5.221ab–5,5.224ab	 tasmāt deśa ādi sadbhāva nimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak vastu ākārāḥ pratīyeran udbhava abhibhava ātmakāḥ yugapad grāhāṇām ca yaḥ yat ākāra vācinam śabdam smarati tena asau ākāraḥ sampratīyate nityam satsu tathā loke rūpa ādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak cakṣuḥ ādi anurodhena saṃvittiḥ vyavatiṣṭhate evam eva ghaṭa tva ādau sarvān prati bhavati api 
SV_5,5.224cd–5,5.227cd	 vācaka smṛti bhedena saṃvittiḥ vyavatiṣṭhate tasmāt bahis sthitaḥ api ātmā narāṇām cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ prāpya vā aprāpya vā buddheḥ viṣaya tvena kalpyate vadanti laukikā yat ca yādṛś jñānam tathā bahis te punar jñāna saṃvittyā tathā artham prati jānate grāhaka tvena vijñānam yathārtham naḥ samarpayet tādṛś arthaḥ saḥ iti evam teṣām vā tad upāyataḥ 
SV_5,5.228ab–5,5.231ab	 laiṅgikā sattvam aprāptaiḥ etaiḥ bāhya artha vādibhiḥ jñāna anubhavam utkramya bāhyaḥ eva pratīyate yathā loke ca tad buddhiḥ vācyam evam parīkṣakaiḥ na yādṛś antara ākāraḥ tādṛś bāhyaḥ avakalpate utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīḥ artha grahaṇe yadi pūrva pakṣasya kim siddham katham ca artha antaram vadet bāhya artha vādinam brūte bhavān kim na evam icchati 
SV_5,5.231cd–5,5.234cd	 pratibandhaḥ na tasya asti gṛhṇātyartha antaram yadā uttaram grahaka abhāvāt liṅga abhāvāt ca na asti naḥ tadā grahaṇam iti etat anyatarkeṣu ca ucyate teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānam artha kāle avagamyate tathā satyartha nāśaḥ syāt iti etat upadiśyate nanu iti etat asambaddham pareṣṭasya eva codanāt paurva aprya vibhāgaḥ api prāk uktena virudhyate 
SV_5,5.235ab–5,5.237cd	 kṣaṇika tvena yuktam syāt jñāta tvam atha ced tadā bhūta kāla āśrayāt brūyāt pṛthā uktasya punarvacaḥ atra api na sva siddhāntam ūce vyājāt parasya tu bhrānta tvāt anyathā pakṣam gṛhītvā iti sma pṛcchati saha utpatti upalabdhā hi jñānasya ekāntataḥ sthitiḥ prāk ūrdhvam vā artha saṃvitteḥ yugapad vā iti cintyate 
SV_5,5.238ab–5,5.241ab	 evam ca arthasya saṃvitteḥ paścāt jñāna avabodhanam bravītu nūnam etasya paścāt utpadyate api tat na ca etat śaktyate tasmāt utpatteḥ apakarṣaṇam karomi tāvat tad kālā saṃvittiḥ api setsyati prāk ca tad grahaṇe siddhe bāhya abhyantarayoḥ dhruvam viveka adarśanam tasmāt idam pūrvam ca coditam yugapad gṛhyamāṇe api na ākāraḥ arthasya lakṣyate 
SV_5,5.241cd–5,5.244ab	 tasmāt arthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvam yatnena sādhyate yaḥ tu etasya uttaraḥ granthaḥ prāk eva asau nirūpitaḥ na tu etat sādhanam sākṣāt pūrvam buddheḥ abodhane na parāmṛśyate artha ātmā jñātaḥ api ajñāta vat yatas tasān na grahaṇam pūrvam buddheḥ kim kena saṅgatam atas pūrva upalabdhyā yaḥ buddhi ākāraḥ atra vāñchitaḥ 
SV_5,5.244cd–5,5.247cd	 tad nirākaraṇena eva phalatvāt grantha varṇanā kāmam buddheḥ iti tu etad artha adhīna tvam ucyate na ca artha rūpāt bhedena dhiyām asti nirūpaṇam para rūpa nirūpyam ca na meyam mṛga toya vat asat grāhya anusāreṇa jñāna saṃvedya tā tava svaccha tvāt tu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām vāsanā upaplavāt tena na meyam pāramārthikam 
SV_5,5.248ab–5,5.251ab	 nimitta niyata tvam tu samānam ubhayoḥ api nija śakti anusāri tvāt jñāna bāhya artha vādinoḥ tantu arthaiḥ api kasmāt vaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ na ārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kim taiḥ mṛd piṇḍa arthena vā paṭaḥ tantu mṛd piṇḍa vijñāne hi anuyojye mate yadi artha paryanuyogaḥ api tadvat eva prasajyate artha ārambha vyavasthā ced sāmarthya niyama āśrayā 
SV_5,5.251cd–5,5.254cd	 jñāna ārambha vyavasthāyām sāmarthyam kena vāryate tasmāt yatra ubhayoḥ doṣaḥ parihāraḥ api vā samaḥ na ekaḥ paryanuyoktavyaḥ tādṛś artha vicāraṇe deśa kāla nimittāni vyañjakāni artha vādinaḥ śaktīnām kāraṇa sthānām sva kārya niyamam prati śaktayaḥ api ca bhāvānām kārya arthāpatti kalpitāḥ prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryam vyavsthitāḥ 
SV_5,5.255ab–5,5.258ab	 bhavataḥ tu na vijñānāt bhinna abhinnā nirūpyate śaktiḥ saṃvṛti sadbhāvam utsṛjya paramārthataḥ vāsanā eva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śakti śabdena gīyate nimitta niyata tvam ca vāsanāyā yat ucyate tasyāḥ ca asambhavena etat apārārthyāt ca durlabham deśa kāla nimitta ādi na ca te asti niyāmakam matvā etat api ca iti āha bhāṣya kāraḥ param prati 
SV_5,5.258cd–5,5.261cd	 tasmāt aparihāraḥ ayam tantubhyaḥ te yathā paṭaḥ tathā me tantu buddhibhyaḥ paṭa buddhiḥ iti īdṛśaḥ evamādya pramāṇābhyām na tāvat bāhya śūnyatā āgamasya tu na eva iha vyāpāraḥ atas anyathā api vā na upamā sadṛśa abhāvāt na artha āpattiḥ viparyayāt tasmāt abhāva gamya tvam śūnyatāyāḥ sthitam hi naḥ evam pramāṇataḥ asiddhāḥ yaiḥ prameya āśraya ucyate 
SV_5,5.262cd–5,5.264cd	 bāhyasya aṇu samūha ādeḥ grāhyasya asambhava īkṣaṇāt taiḥ āntara asambhavataḥ yathā uktāt jñeya tvam anyasya balāt upeyam grāhyāḥ na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavaḥ atas satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ iti bahis viṣaya pratipādanāt tad abhāva kṛtā mati saṃvṛtiḥ ubhaya tattva vidām paramārthataḥ kṣamam idam dhuri dharma vicāraṇe 
SV_5,6.1ab–5,6.4ab	 pratyakṣa avyabhicāri tvāt evaṃlakṣaṇakam ca yat prasiddham anumāna ādi na parīkṣyam tat api atas pramātā jñāta sambandhaḥ eka deśī atha vā ucyate karma dhāraya pakṣaḥ vā sambandhini eka deśa tā dvayam vā jñāta sambandham upalabdham parasparam tasya eka deśa śabdābhyām ucyete samudāyinau sambandhaḥ vyāptiḥ iṣṭā atra liṅga adharmasya liṅginā 
SV_5,6.4cd–5,6.7cd	 vyāpyasya gamaka tvam ca vyāpakam gamyam iṣyate yaḥ yasya deśa kālābhyām samaḥ nyūnaḥ api vā bhavet sa vyāpyaḥ vyāpakaḥ tasya samaḥ vā abhyadhikaḥ api vā tena vyāpye gṛhīte arthe vyāpakaḥ tasya gṛhyate na hi anyathā bhavati eṣā vyāpya vyāpaka tā tayoḥ vyāpaka tva gṛhītaḥ tu vyāpyaḥ yadi api vastutas ādhikye api aviruddha tvāt vyāpyam na pratipādayet 
SV_5,6.8ab–5,6.11ab	 vispaṣṭam dṛṣṭam etd ca go viṣāṇi tvayoḥ mitau vyāpya tvāt gamikā gāvaḥ vyāpikā na viṣāṇitāḥ tena yatra api ubhau dhrmau vyāpya vyāpaka sammatau tatra api vyāpya tā eva syāt aṅgam na vyāpitāḥ miteḥ tena dharmi antareṣu eṣā yasya yena eva yādṛśī deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpya tā prāk nirūpitā tasya tāvati tādṛś sa dṛṣṭaḥ dharmi antare punar 
SV_5,6.11cd–5,6.14cd	 vyāpya aṃśaḥ vyāpaka aṃśasya tathā eva pratipādkaḥ bhūyas darśana gamyā ca vyāptiḥ sāmānya dharmayoḥ jñāyate bheda hānena kva cit ca api viśeṣayoḥ kṛttikā udayam ālakṣya rohiṇī ā satti kpti vat vyāpteḥ ca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaḥ cit dharmaḥ prayojakaḥ asmin sati amunā bhāvyam iti śaktyā nirūpyate anye para prayuktānām vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ 
SV_5,6.15ab–5,6.18ab	 taiḥ dṛṣṭaiḥ api na eva iṣṭā vyāpaka aṃśa avadhāraṇāḥ ye tu tān api visrabdham sādhya siddhyau prayuñjate sulabhaiḥ pratihetu ādi doṣaiḥ bhrāmyanti te ciram teṣu āgama viruddha tvam svayam ca iṣṭa vighāti tā alaukika vivādāḥ ca varṇyaḥ te haitukaiḥ tatas niṣiddhi tvena hiṃsānām adharma tvam prayujyate tad abhāve na tad siddhiḥ hiṃsā tvāt aprayojakāt 
SV_5,6.18cd–5,6.21cd	 hetu dvaya prayukte ca mithyātve sarva buddhiṣu jñāna tva utpattimat tva ādi sādhakaḥ na prayojakaḥ traivarṇika prayuktā ca yāga ādeḥ svarga hetu tā na manuṣya tva mātreṇa śūdra sthena prayujyate kṛta sāvayava tva ādi prayuktā ca niāśitā prayatna anantara jñāna sadṛśaiḥ na prayujyate jātimat tva indriya tva ādi vastu sanmātra bandhanam 
SV_5,6.22ab–5,6.25ab	 śada anitya tva siddhi artham kaḥ vadet yaḥ na tārkikaḥ tasmāt yaḥ eva yasya arthaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sādhana śaktitaḥ saḥ eva gamakaḥ tasya na prasaṅga anvitaḥ api yaḥ upāttaḥ ca eka deśābhyām dharmī api atra eka deśa tā apārārthye hi dhūma ādeḥ svarūpaiḥ na eka deśa tā saḥ eva ca ubhayātamā ayam gamyaḥ gamakaḥ eva vā asiddhena eka deśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ 
SV_5,6.25cd–5,6.28cd	 atas pṛthak abhinnaḥ vā aprayoktāṇām vivakṣaya anityaḥ kṛtakaḥ yasmāt dhūmavān agnimān iti dharmya bhinnam upādānam bhedaḥ atra agniḥ iti īdṛśe eka deśa viśiṣṭaḥ ca dharmī eva atra anumīyate na hi tad nirapekṣa tve sambhavati anumeya tā na dharma mātram siddha tvāt tathā dharmī tathā ubhayam vyastam vā api samastam vā svātantryeṇa anumīyate 
SV_5,6.29ab–5,6.32ab	 eka deśasya liṅga tvam sādhyena anugamaḥ asya ca dvaym ca na syāt iṣṭam sat pakṣeṣu eṣu yathākramam anitya tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ na hi dhvaninā anugamaḥ na eṣām na ubhayasya ubhayena vā sambandhaḥ api anupādānāt nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyā api vā mitau na ca api anugamaḥ tena liṅgasya iha nidarśyate na ca ākāra dvayam tasya sādhya sādhana bhāj bhavet 
SV_5,6.32cd–5,6.35cd	 tasmat artha gṛhīta tvāt matubarthasya gamyatā na svāntantryeṇa mantavyāḥ yathā daṇḍya ādi śabdataḥ viśīṣṭa artha pratītau syāt sambandhaḥ na antarīyakaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvam āpannau dvau imau atas gamyau aṅga aṅgi bhāvaḥ tu kaiḥ cit iṣṭaḥ vikalpataḥ sarvathā dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ dharmeṇa tu avagamyate viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tve na viśeṣaḥ avadhāryate 
SV_5,6.36ab–5,6.38cd	 tatra utaram vadanti anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam hetu dharmeṇa samandhaḥ tasya aprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ pradhāna tvāt dhi dharmeṇa sambandhaḥ vākyataḥ bhavet tatra asambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyaḥ asau dharminā saha dhvaneḥ iti atha vā vācyam anvayasya tu darśane bheda upāttasya dharmasya guṇa abhāvaḥ na duṣyati 
SV_5,6.39ab–5,6.42ab	 agneḥ deśa viśiṣṭa tve na ca etat pakṣa lakṣaṇam viśiṣṭa tā asya deśena bhavet evamprakārikā yaḥ agniḥ saḥ asti kva cit deśe yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yatra tatra vā agniḥ pūrva anubhūtaḥ vā deśa mātreṇa saṅgataḥ yaḥ agniḥ saḥ anena yuktaḥ vā yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anena saḥ atha vā yaḥ ayam sa deśa mātreṇa yuktaḥ pūrveṇa vā api ayam etad deśa viśiṣṭaḥ vā yaḥ ayam agniḥ iti iha tu 
SV_5,6.42cd–5,6.45cd	 pūrvayoḥ siddha sādhya tvam pareṣu syāt viruddha tā vyāptiḥ etena deśena sarva agnīnām na yujyate na api pūrvasya na api eṣa vahniḥ sarvaiḥ viśiṣyate deśaiḥ pūrveṇa vā api asya na deśena viśeṣyatā etad deśa viśiṣṭaḥ ayam iti etat kathyate katham yadā deśa anapekṣaḥ agniḥ na ayam iti avadhāryate agneḥ pūrvataram ca atra deśaḥ eva avadhāryate 
SV_5,6.46ab–5,6.49ab	 tad jñāna kāla buddhaḥ ca na deśaḥ syāt viśeṣaṇam deśasya parvata ādeḥ tu svarūpe pāvakāt ṛte gṛhīte agni viśiṣṭasya punar jñānam na duṣyati tasmāt dharma viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameya tā sā deśasya agni yuktasya dhūmasya anyaiḥ ca kalpitā nanu śabda vat eva sytāt liṅgamyam viśiṣaṇam na evam na hi atra liṅgasya śakti aneka tva kalpanā 
SV_5,6.49cd–5,6.52cd	 na ca tasya anumeya tvam viśeṣyaḥ ca avadhāritaḥ viśiṣṭa tvena ca ajñānāt tanmātrasya anumeya tā nanu dhūma viśeṣya tve hetoḥ pakṣa eka deśa tā na etat asti viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānya hetu tā dhūma tad jāna sambandha smṛti prāmāṇya kalpane phalena viṣaya eka tvam tad vyāpārāt purā uditam prameya dhī pramāṇa tvam bhāṣya kāraḥ tu manyate 
SV_5,6.53ab–5,6.56ab	 pratyakṣa aniyama uktaḥ ca sarvatra eva anuṣajyate anumāna gṛhītasya tena eva pratipādanam parebhyaḥ vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ yathā uditaḥ tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhya dharmaḥ vidhīyate niyamaḥ tad vipakṣāt ca kalpyate na avirodhinaḥ asat nikṛṣṭa vācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam tādrūpyeṇa paricchittiḥ tad viparyayataḥ api ca 
SV_5,6.56cd–5,6.59cd	 pramitasya pramāṇe hi na apekṣā jāyate punar tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇam niṣphalam param vaiparītya paricchinne na avakāśaḥ parasya tu mūle tasya hi anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayaḥ hṛtaḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ ca ṣaṭkasya yena eva arthaḥ avadhāritaḥ tena eva uttara bādhaḥ syāt vikalpa ādeḥ asambhavāt agrāhyatā tu śabda ādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate 
SV_5,6.60ab–5,6.63ab	 teṣām aśrāvaṇa tva ādi viruddham anumānataḥ na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇa avagamyate sa anvaya vyatirekābhyām gamyate badhira ādiṣu tridhā śabda virodhaḥ syāt pratijña ādi vibhāgataḥ pratijñā pūrva sañjalpa sarva loka prasiddhitaḥ yāvajjīvam aham mauni iti ukti mātreṇa bādhyate sarva vākyam ṛṣā tve tu dharma uktyā eva ātma bādhanam 
SV_5,6.63cd–5,6.66cd	 dharmī uktyā aham yatas jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama bauddhasya śabda nitya tvam pūrva upetena bādhyate candra śabda abhidheya tvam śaśinaḥ yaḥ niṣedhati sa sarva loka siddhena candra jñānena bādhyate jñāta goga vaya ākāram prati yaḥ sādhayet idam na goḥ gavaya sādṛśyam tasya bādha upama ānataḥ geha avagata nāstitvaḥ jīvan caitraḥ yadā bahis 
SV_5,6.67ab–5,6.70ab	 na asti iti sādhyate bādhaḥ tatra artha āpattitaḥ bhavet agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde ca anabhidhāyake śrotra ādinā astitāyām ca śabda anitya tva sādhane śruta arthāpatti bādhaḥ atra yat ā āpta ukti nivārite divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātri bhojanam śaśaśṛṅga ādi sadbhāva virodhaḥ anupalabdhitaḥ evam ca dharma sambandha bādhaḥ tāvat udāhṛtaḥ 
SV_5,6.70cd–5,6.73cd	 dharma dharmī u bhayeṣām ca svarūpa sva viśeṣayoḥ śruti artha ākṣiptayoḥ vākye vācyaḥ sarva pramāṇakaḥ tṛṇa ādi vikriyā hetoḥ agni mat hima sādhane pratyakṣa avagatāt śaityāt tad viśeṣa uttha bādhanam adharmaḥ vihitaḥ duḥkham karoti alpam iti iha tu vihita tvāt adharmasya svarūpasya eva bādhanam tathā duḥkha nimitta tvam viśeṣaḥ tasya bādhyate 
SV_5,6.74ab–5,6.77ab	 ayathārthāḥ dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ iti ukte dvaya bādhanam svarūpa sva viśeṣābhyām tat hī mithyātva sādhanāt kṣaṇikā atyanta mithyā tve viśeṣau ca dvayoḥ iha darśanāt eka deśasya iti anena etat vyudasyate yatra ekasya ubhayoḥ vā api saṃśaya adhī vi paryayāḥ śaityāt na dāhakaḥ bahniḥ cākṣuṣa tvāt anitya tā śabdasya iti evamādau tu dvayoḥ siddhaḥ viparyayaḥ 
SV_5,6.77cd–5,6.80cd	 kṛtaka tva guṇa tva ādau para ukte yājñikam prati sva ukte ca evamprakāre syāt asiddhaḥ anyatarasya tu bāṣpa ādi bhāva sandigdhaḥ dvayoḥ anyatarasya vā dhūmaḥ tridhā api asiddhaḥ syāt evam tāvat svarūpataḥ ete eva prakārāḥ syuḥ āśraya asiddhi kalpane jñāte api hi svarūpeṇa na atad dharme asti hetu tā sarvatra dṛṣṭa kārya tvāt ātmā sarva gataḥ tu iti 
SV_5,6.81ab–5,6.84ab	 bauddham pratyāśraya asiddhaḥ laukika ādeḥ tu saṃśayaḥ bāṅmātra asiddhi mātreṇa vyavahāra aprakalpanāt dvābhyām yaḥ asattvataḥ jñātaḥ tad vacaḥ dūṣaṇam matam itarat sādhanam tu syāt vādinā yadi sādhyate nirākaraṇa siddhau vā dūṣaṇam prativādinaḥ sandeha viparīta tva hetū ca atra nirākṛtau jñāta sambandha vacanāt trayaḥ saṃśaya hetavaḥ 
SV_5,6.84cd–5,6.87cd	 san sādhye tad abhāve vā dvābhyām vyāvṛttaḥ eva ca dvau viruddha artha sambaddhau yau ekatra eka deśini prameya anitya tā mūrti dharmāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ dvayoḥ nitya āyatna uttha yatna uttha anityeṣu dvis anityataḥ nityāḥ bhūḥ gandhavat tvena syāt asādhāraṇaḥ tu ayam niścaya eka aṅga vaikalyāt eṣa saṃśaya kāraṇam sādhāraṇaḥ yathā dṛṣṭaḥ buddhi dvaya nimittakaḥ 
SV_5,6.88ab–5,6.91ab	 viruddha ekān avāpteḥ ca saṃśaye kāraṇam matam atra asādhāraṇaḥ na asti tad abhāva mukhena tu dvaya asattva virodhāt ca mataḥ saṃśaya kāraṇam sandigdha hetu tā ca eṣām viṣaya apekṣayā ucyate nirṇayasya api hetu tvam dṛṣṭam sādhya antare yatas vyavaccheda anvayau labdhvā niṣkriya ādau amūrti vat kṣiti eka deśa siddha tve gandhavat tvasya hetu tā 
SV_5,6.91cd–5,6.94cd	 yatra apratyakṣatā vāyoḥ arūpatvena sādhyate sparśāt pratyakṣatā vā asau viruddha avyabhicāritā ke cit jāti antaram ca enām varṇayanti apare punar sādhāraṇa tvam aṃśena samastam vā api ananvayam pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrva uktaiḥ yasya sādhanaiḥ tat parājayataḥ kāryaḥ nirṇayaḥ bādha varjanāt kva cit saṃśaya hetū yau pratyeka tvena lakṣitau 
SV_5,6.95ab–5,6.98ab	 saṅghāte nirṇayaḥ tābhyām ūrdhva tā kāka vat tva vat pratyekam saṃhatau vā api gamakau= avirodhinau tasmāt bhinnau viruddha arthau hetū ca atra nidarśitau ṣoḍhā viruddha tām āhuḥ caturddhā vaikadhā api vā śruti artha uktasya bādhāyām pratijñā arthasya hetunā nitya tve kṛtaka tvasya dharma bādhāt viruddha tā bādhaḥ dharma viśeṣasya yadā tu evam prayujyate 
SV_5,6.98cd–5,6.101cd	 arthavat śabda rūpam syāt prāc sambandha avadhāraṇāt vibhaktimat tvāt paścāt vat svarūpeṇa iti ca āśrite asvarūpa artha yogaḥ tu paścāt śabdasya dṛśyate tena prāk api sambandhāt asvarūpa artha tā bhavet iha pratyaya hetu tvāt dravya ādeḥ vyatiricyate samavāyaḥ yathā iha ayam ghaṭaḥ ityādi saṅgatiḥ atra api asamavāya tvam saṃyogasya iva sidhyati 
SV_5,6.102ab–5,6.105ab	 tena dharmi svarūpasya vaiparītyāt viruddha tā yat ca sat tāvat eka tvam samavāyasya kalpitam tatra saṃyoga vat bhedāt syāt viśeṣa viruddha tā nityam ātma astitā kaiḥ cit yadā sautra antikam prati sādhyate avayava abhāvāt vyoma vat dvaya bādhanam tadā ubhaya viśeṣasya bādhaḥ ayam sādhyate yadā pārārthyam cakṣuḥ ādīnām saṅghātāt śayana ādi vat 
SV_5,6.105cd–5,6.108cd	 śayane saṅgha pārārthyam bhautika vyāpta hetuke ātmānam prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam asaṃhata para artha tve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatā api ca anahaṅkārika tvam ca cakṣuḥ ādeḥ prasajyate gamakasya eka deśasya vyāptiḥ gamya iti bhāṣitum sādhya sādharmya vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate tatra hetu artham uddiśya sādhya upādānam iṣyate 
SV_5,6.109ab–5,6.112ab	 uddeśyaḥ vyāpyate dharmaḥ vyāpakaḥ ca itaraḥ mataḥ yat vṛttayoḥ prāthamyam iti ādi uddeśa lakṣaṇam tad vṛttam eva kāraḥ ca syāt upādeya lakṣaṇam vadati artham sva śaktyā ca śabdaḥ vaktra napekṣayā sādhya hetu tvam arthānām vyāpti śakti anurodhataḥ tatra ajñānāt yadā vakta sahacāra vivakṣayā viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāpta tvam vivakṣati 
SV_5,6.112cd–5,6.115cd	 vivakṣan api vā śabdam tat yogyam na vadet yadi ghaṭe kṛtaka nāśi tve na aśi vyāptam kṛtena vā na tadā iṣṭasya hetu tvam syāt aniṣṭasya ca eva tat tasmāt vyāpya tva rūpeṇa vācyaḥ hetu tva sammataḥ yadā samyak prayukte api vākye arthaḥ na tathā bhavet sādhya hetu ubhaya vyāpti śūnya tvāt paramārthataḥ nityaḥ dhvaniḥ amūrtta tvāt karma vat paramāṇu vat

SV_5,6.122cd–5,6.125cd	 dhūma bhāve agni bhāvena vyāpte anagniḥ tatas cyutaḥ adhūmaḥ eva vidyeta iti evam vyāpya tvam aśnute tathā anagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmaḥ tata cyutaḥ anyatra anavakāśa tvāt vyāpyate dhruvam agninā vyāpakau tu yadā ucyete bhāva abhāvau tadā tatas na eva vyāpyāt vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet tasmāt dhūmena sādhya tvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā

SV_5,6.139ab–5,6.142ab	 āditye anupalabdhiḥ ced na deśe api adhunātane kva cit tatra upalabdhiḥ ced devadatte api dṛśyatām yadi dharmi antara apekṣā tatra sāmānya dṛṣṭa tā syāt agni dhūmayoḥ sā eva tasmāt evam pracakṣate pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa sambandham yayoḥ eva viśeṣayoḥ gomaya indhana tad janya viśeṣa ādi matiḥ kṛtā tad deśa sthena tena eva gatvā kāla antare api tam

SV_5,6.149cd–5,6.152cd	 na ca liṅga vinirmuktam anumānam pravartate asāmānyasya liṅga tvam na ca kena cit iṣyate na ca anavagatam liṅgam kiñ cit asti prakāśakam tasya vā api anumānena syāt anyena gatiḥ punar tad utpattiḥ ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānya jñāna saṃhitāt tasya ca api anumāna tvāt bhavet liṅgena ca udbhavaḥ anumāna antarāt eva jñānena evam ca kalpane 
SV_5,6.153ab–5,6.156ab	 liṅga liṅgī anumānānām ānantyāt eka liṅgini gatiḥ yuga sahasreṣu bahuṣu api na vidyate atha sāmānya bhūte api liṅge anyasmāt gatiḥ bhavet pramāṇāt apramāṇāt vā tathā liṅgi gatiḥ bhavet evam api anumānasya nitya ucchedaḥ prasajyate pramāṇa antaram eva syāt sāmānyasya avabodhakam apramāṇau= abuddhāt vā liṅgāt liṅgini yā matiḥ 
SV_5,6.156cd–5,6.159cd	 sā api mithyā bhavet nityam bāṣpa jāta agni buddhi vat nanu apramāṇa bhūtā api sambandha smṛtiḥ iṣyate yathā liṅgi gatau hetuḥ tathā liṅga gatiḥ bhavet tatra yat pūrva vijñānam tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate tad upasthāna mātreṇa smṛteḥ syāt caritārtha tā na tu liṅga gatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate tad abhāva asmṛtiḥ ca atra na kathan cit pravartate 
SV_5,6.160ab–5,6.163ab	 smārtam etat abhedena vijñānam iti yaḥ vadet tasya vandhyā sute api asti nūnam smaraṇa śakta tā na ca asādhāraṇaḥ artha ātmā sāmānya jñāna kāraṇam yasmāt na asya avinābhāvaḥ tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathan canaḥ syāt vā sambandha dṛṣṭyā asau sāmānyam kṛtaka tva vat na hi asādhāraṇam vastu pūrvatra iha ca vidyate na ca api avyapadeśasya vikalpa rahitasya ca 
SV_5,6.163cd–5,6.166cd	 vinā pūrva anusandhānāt liṅga tvam upapadyate kalpyante ca viśeṣāḥ ye te api aliṅgam ananvayāt etasmāt eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasya api aliṅga tā sāmānya rūpa tāyām vā tathā eva anavadhāraṇam kva cit vā dṛṣṭa sambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyakaḥ bhavet sambandha anubhavaḥ avaśyam eṣitavyaḥ ca liṅganaḥ anumāna pravṛtteḥ tu prāk jñānam tatra na asti te 
SV_5,6.167ab–5,6.170ab	 na ca api vāsanā mātrāt liṅga jñānasya sambhavaḥ liṅgi jñānam ca tadvat syāt tri rūpāt liṅgataḥ na tat tatra abhāvasya liṅga tvam na ca asau ānumānikaḥ pramāṇa antara gamya tvāt tatra doṣaḥ na jāyate pratyakṣa avagatāt liṅgāt yasya liṅgi gatiḥ bhavet tasya na atas adhikam kiñ cit prārthanīyam prasajyate yatra api anumitāt liṅgāt liṅgini grahaṇam bhavet 
SV_5,6.170cd–5,6.173cd	 tatra api maulikam liṅgam pratyakṣāt eva gamyate liṅga tvam kṛtaka tva ādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā pratyakṣa tvam ca tasya iṣṭam iti dūram na gamyate evam śabda upamāna ādau sāmānya āśrayatā yatas tad daussthityena daussthityam sarvatra atas prasajyate tasmāt pratyakṣa pūrva tvam pramāṇa antaraḥ iṣyate pratyakṣa tvam ca sāmānye na anyathā hi gatiḥ bhavet 
SV_5,6.174ab–5,6.177ab	 pratyakṣa ālambana tvam ca viśeṣasya katham bhavet yadā vastu antara apekṣaḥ sāmānya aṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate rūpa ādayaḥ hi sāmānyam sarve nīla ādi apekṣayā sva viśeṣa anapekṣya atha nīla ādīnām samāna tā te ca api tāvat sāmānyam yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ dvi aṇukasya api yat rūpam tat dhi sādhāraṇam dvayoḥ na ca antyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ asti kasya cit 
SV_5,6.177cd–5,6.180cd	 na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā bhedena āgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedaḥ grāhyatām vrajet na ca bhinneṣu abhinnatva buddheḥ grāhya tva sambhavaḥ samudāyaḥ na vā api asti bhavatām na ca sarvadā sarveṣām asata arthena pratyaya utpatti sambhavaḥ na ca eka jāti yogena vinā asti samudāyatā samudāye api ca aṇu tvam na eteṣām apagacchati 
SV_5,6.181ab–5,6.184ab	 sāmānyam iti adṛśye api tena sāmānyaḥ eva naḥ vyāsaṅginī bhavati eṣā dhīḥ vinā api eka kalpanāt vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathā indriyaiḥ grahaṇam tadvat eva syāt prativyakti niveśinaḥ mīmāṃsakaiḥ ca na avaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ yat balena upalabdhasya mithyātvam kalpayet bhavān samūha rūpam pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ 
SV_5,6.184cd–5,6.188cd	 yaḥ apahnute śaśasya api saḥ abhāvam śṛṅgataḥ vadet samūha parama artha tve sthite tad siddhi hetukāḥ yadi nāma avagamyeta paramāṇu astitā punar tasmāt yat gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā tat tathā eva abhyupetavyam sāmānyam atha vā itarat sattā ādi sāmānyam apekṣya sarvam go tva ādi sādhāraṇa tām upaiti tasmāt asādhāraṇam akṣa gamyam vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta sāmānya rupeṇa na gṛhyate ced kim vā asti asādhāraṇa buddhiḥ atra yat vastu lokaḥ pratipadyate asmin dvidhā api tat śakti atas eva vaktum 
SV_5,7.1ab–5,7.4ab	 pratyakṣa ādiṣu vaktavyam śabda mātrasya lakṣaṇam adati tvaritena iha kim śāstrāt abhidhīyate sāmānya lakṣaṇam tyaktvā viśeṣasya eva lakṣaṇam na śakyam kevalam vaktum itas api asya na vācya tā yat ca uktam śabda vijñānāt arthe jñānam iti īdṛśamū aviśiṣṭam viśiṣṭasya na tad śāstrasya lakṣaṇam pravṛttiḥ vā nivṛttiḥ vā nityena kṛtakena vā 
SV_5,7.4cd–5,7.7cd	 puṃsām yena upadiśyeta tat śāstram abhidhīyate svarūpa kathanam yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate tad aṅga tvena tasya api śāstra tvam avagamyate bhāvanāyām samastāyām vākyāt eva upajāyate pravṛttiḥ vā nivṛttiḥ vā tat śāstram na padāt yatas aparīkṣā āmiṣeṇa api lakṣaṇāni vadan= ayam na svatantra upayogi tva nirapekṣāṇi jalpati 
SV_5,7.8ab–5,7.11ab	 tatra yat loka vākya stham kathayet śabda lakṣaṇam vedam vyākhyātu kāmasya tat na atīva upayujyate pratyakṣa ādi upayogam tu varṇa mātra āditaḥ puras śāstra artha jñāna velāyām matvā tad lakṣaṇam kṛtam yat tu gāmānaya ityādi vākya stham śabda lakṣaṇam tasya na iha upayogaḥ asti tasmāt śāstra gatam kṛtam veśeṣaḥ ca na sāmānyam antareṇa asti kaḥ cana 
SV_5,7.11cd–5,7.14cd	 tasmāt tam api udāhṛtya sāmānyam lakṣayet sukham sāmānya rūpam api etad adhikārāt viśiṣyate codanā ca upadeśaḥ ca śāstram eva iti udāhṛtam yathā ca codanā śabdaḥ vaidikyām eva vartate śabda jñāna artha vijñāna śabdau śāstre tathā sthitau pratyakṣa ādi a parīkṣya tve tad antarbhāva hetukam śāstrasya api aparīkṣya tvam anayā eva dhiyā uditam 
SV_5,7.15ab–5,7.18ab	 tatra anumānam eva idam bauddhaiḥ vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam bhedaḥ sāṃkhya ādibhiḥ tu iṣṭaḥ na tu uktam bheda kāraṇam pūrva saṃskāra yukta antya varṇa vākya ādi kalpanā vivakṣā ādi ca dhūma ādau na asti iti etena bhinna tā yaiḥ uktā tatra vaidharmya vikalpa sama jāti tā dhūma anitya viṣāṇi ādi viśeṣāt na hi bhinna tā taila kṣaṇya parityāgaḥ yāvat na pratipādyate 
SV_5,7.18cd–5,7.21cd	 tāvat viśeṣa mātreṇa vadataḥ jātitāḥ bhavet yathā iṣṭa viniyogena pratītiḥ yā api śabdataḥ na dhūma ādeḥ iti iha api vyabhicāraḥ aṅga vṛttibhiḥ hasta saṃjñā ādayaḥ ye api yad artha pratipādane bhaveyuḥ kṛta saṅketāḥ te na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ puruṣa ākṣipta tayām ca tathā eva vyabhicāritā pada vaidika vākyānām na satya vyāpitā bhavet 
SV_5,7.22ab–5,7.25ab	 sambandhātubhavaḥ ca ayam saḥ anyatra api vilakṣaṇaḥ etasmin puruṣa apekṣā deśa apekṣā agni dhūmayoḥ kāla ādi apekṣayā ca anyaḥ uktā ca anyaiḥ abhinnatā āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumānataḥ na ca apūrva ādi śabdānām bhedāt sarvatra bhinna tā na ca iha aśva ādi śabdebhyaḥ bhedaḥ teṣām pratīyate na ca api ajñāta sambandham padam kiñ cit prakāśakam 
SV_5,7.25cd–5,7.28cd	 sambandhān anubhūtyā atas na syāt ananumāna tā tulya ākāra tayā api atra śabda jñāna artha tad dhiyām agni dhūmeṣu adṛṣṭa tvāt na bhedaḥ tad nivāraṇāt pratibimbeṣu anaikāntaḥ bimbam yādṛś hi darpaṇe tādṛś mukha ādi budhyante na ca atra ananumāna tā pratyakṣatā tadā api atra tadā anyaiḥ vyabhicāritā yatra pāda ādi bambena gatānām anumīyate 
SV_5,7.29ab–5,7.32ab	 eka vākyāt sakṛt ca uktān na api anekasya tad kṣaṇam syāt viruddha aviruddhasya bodhāt etasya bhinnātā liṅgasya api hi tādrūpyam dṛṣṭam hetu viruddhayoḥ virodhāt na anumānam ced syāt anāgamatā api te yatra ca ekārtha tā vākye tatra syāt anumāna tā sakṛt uccarite ca asmin vivakṣā ekā eva dṛśyate yaḥ tu anirdhānam ca dhūma ādau vyabhicāritam 
SV_5,7.32cd–5,7.35ab	 sa liṅge api asphuṭe dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt na etena bhidyate dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānam ca dhūma ādau vyabhicāritam prasiddha tvāt dhi tatra api na dṛṣṭāntaḥ abhidhīyate anabhyaḥ te tu apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim atra pratyuktaḥ iti evam budhyante hi cirāt kva cit para uktā hetavaḥ ca atra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ 
SV_5,7.35cd–5,7.38cd	 śabda anumānayoḥ aikyam dhūmāt agni anumāna vat anvaya vyatirekābhyām eka pratyakṣa darśanāt sambandha pūrvaka tvāt ca pratipattiḥ itas yatas pratyakṣa anyapramāṇa tvāt tad adṛṣṭa artha bodhanāt sāmānya viṣaya tvāt ca traikālya viṣaya āśrayāt kaiḥ cit mīmāṃsakaiḥ uktaḥ bhedaḥ atra viṣaya antarāt pūrvābhyām hi aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate 
SV_5,7.39ab–5,7.42ab	 tatra api na āgama tvam syāt puruṣa ukte tathā as tu ced pratyayaḥ kid nimittaḥ arthe vaktṛ buddheḥ kutas nu asau na śabda arthasya sa āliṅgam na śabdaḥ asyāḥ kathan canaḥ viśeṣaḥ gamyate tābhyām na ca etasya anumeya tā tena vaktuḥ abhiprāye pratyakṣa ādya nirūpite puruṣoktiḥ api śrotuḥ āgama tvam prapadyate na ca api ananumeya tvam āgama arthasya śakyate 
SV_5,7.42cd–5,7.45cd	 liṅgam hi śabdaḥ eva asya dhūmaḥ agneḥ iva kalpyate na ca api ananumeyavāt pramāṇa antara gamya tā rūpasya aśrāvaṇa tvena na hi apratyakṣata iṣyate evam sati sva yūthyāḥ na ke cit na ati prapañcinaḥ anumāna viśeṣaḥ ayam īdṛś dharmasya bodhakaḥ bhaviṣyati artha rūpam tu liṅgam dharme nirākṛtam saṃjñā anumāna tā icchā tu na duṣyet āgame api naḥ 
SV_5,7.46ab–5,7.49ab	 lakṣaṇena tu abhinna tvam yadi śabda anumānayoḥ veda jñāna apramāṇa tvam syāt atad lakṣaṇa tvataḥ āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyān nṛvacassu hi lakṣaṇena anumāna tvāt prāmāṇyam siddhim ṛcchati vede tu āpta nara abhāvāt sambandha anubhavāt ṛte lakṣaṇam na anumānasya iti aprāmāṇyam prasajyate nanu eka deśa satya tve tasya syāt anumāna tā 
SV_5,7.49cd–5,7.52cd	 veda tvāt agni hotra ādau vāyu kṣepiṣṭha vākya vat na āditya yūpe anaikāntāt tadvat vā gauṇa tā bhavet na atas pratyanumānānām evam pūrva uktayā viśā tasmāt lakṣaṇa bhedena yadi śabda pramāṇa tā samā loke ca vede ca siddhā veda pramāṇa tā tena ca āpta upadeśa tvam na syāt āgama lakṣaṇam na āptasya sambhavaḥ vede loke na asmāt pramāṇa tā 
SV_5,7.53ab–5,7.56ab	 purastāt varṇitam hi etat tsmāt śabdena yā matiḥ tasyāḥ svatas pramāṇa tvam na ced syāt doṣa darśanam anumānena ca etasya prāmāṇyam kevalam samam pade tāvat kṛtaḥ yatnaḥ paraiḥ iti atra varṇyate viṣayaḥ anyādṛśaḥ tāvat dṛśyate liṅga śabdayoḥ sāmānya viṣaya tvam ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati dharma adharma viśiṣṭaḥ ca liṅgī iti etat ca sādhitam 
SV_5,7.56cd–5,7.59cd	 na tāvat anumānam hi yāvat tad viṣayam na tat sāmānyāt atiriktam tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ sāmarthyāt anumeya tvāt aśrute api pada antare saṃkhyā ādimān padārthaḥ ced na tāvat saḥ avyaya ādiṣu yatra api te pratīyante tatra vyakteḥ viśeṣaṇam pada antara abhidheyasya tādarthyāt ca kriyā ātmanaḥ vākya arthe api padam yatra gomada ādi prayujyate 
SV_5,7.60ab–5,7.63ab	 sati api atra viśeṣṭa tve siddha tvāt na evaa pakṣatā tāvān eva hi tatra arthaḥ yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ bheda buddheḥ ca vaiṣamtham prakṛti pratyaya arthayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya artha svātantrya grahaṇam na ca viśeṣya pūrvikā tatra buddhiḥ ca atra viparyayaḥ atha śabdaḥ arthavat tvena pakṣaḥ kasmāt na kalpyate pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hi hetuḥ tatra prasajyate 
SV_5,7.63cd–5,7.66cd	 pakṣe dhūma viśeṣe ca sāmānyam hetuḥ iṣyate śabda tvam gamakam na atra go śabda tvam niṣetsyate vyaktiḥ eva viśiṣyātaḥ hetuḥ ca ekā prasajyate bhavet vyañjaka bhedāt ced na tu evam pratyayaḥ asti naḥ katham ca asya viśiṣṭa tvam na tāvat deśa kālataḥ tad pratīti viśiṣṭaḥ ced param kim anumīyate na pratyāyana śaktiḥ ca viśeṣasya anumīyate 
SV_5,7.67ab–5,7.70ab	 viśeṣāṇām na śaktiḥ hi sa eka deśe agni jāti vat sāmānyasya eva śakta tvam pakṣaḥ hetuḥ tat eva ca tasmāt artha viśiṣṭasya na śabdasya anumeya tā katham ca pakṣa dharma tvam śabdasya iha nirūpyate na kriyā kartṛ sambandhāt ṛte sambandhanam kva cit rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ saḥ ucyate vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tāḥ vā tatra iti tasya tāḥ 
SV_5,7.70cd–5,7.73cd	 deśe agnimati dhūmasya kartṛ tvam bhavanam prati kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate na ca anavagata ākāraḥ sambandhaḥ asti iti gamyate na ca asti asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhī tatpuruṣaḥ api vā tasmāt na pakṣa dharmaḥ ayam iti śakyā nirūpaṇāḥ nivṛtte anyatra sambandhe ye api tad viṣaya ātmanā vadeyuḥ pakṣa dharma tvam śabdasya anupalabdhi vat 
SV_5,7.74ab–5,7.77ab	 taiḥ api etat nirūpyam tu śabdaḥ tad viṣayaḥ katham na tad deśa ādi sadbhāvaḥ nābhi mukhya ādi tasya vā tasmāt utpādayati eṣa yatas artha viṣayāḥ matim tena tad viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ iti dharma tva kalpanā tatra vācaka tāyām ca siddhāyām pakṣa dharma tā na prati iti aṅga tām gacchet na ca evam anumāna tā gamakatāt ca dharma tvam dharma tvāt gamakaḥ yadi 
SV_5,7.77cd–5,7.80cd	 syāt anyonya āśraya tvam hi tasmāt na eṣā api kalpanā na ca agṛhīta sambandhāḥ sva rūpa vyatirekataḥ śabdam jānanti yena atra pakṣa dharma matiḥ bhavet na ca sva rūpa mātreṇa dhūma ādeḥ pakṣa dharma tā na ca api pūrva sambandham apekṣya eṣā prasajyate dhūmavān ayam iti evam apūrvasya api jāyate pakṣa dharma matiḥ tena bhidyeta uttara lakṣaṇāt 
SV_5,7.81ab–5,7.83cd	 na tu atra pūrva sambandhāt adhikā pakṣa dharma tā na ca artha pratyayāt pūrvam iti anaṅgam iyam bhavet na ca dharmī gṛhītaḥ atra yena tad dharmatā bhavet parvata ādiḥ yathā deśaḥ prāc dharma tva avadhāraṇāt yaḥ ca atra kathyate dharmī prameyaḥ asya saḥ eva naḥ na ca anavadhṛte tasmin tad dharma tva avadhāraṇam 
SV_5,7.84ab–5,7.87ab	 prāk sa ced pakṣa dharma tvāt gṛhītaḥ kim tatas param paṣa dharma ādibhiḥ jñātaiḥ yena syāt anumānitā anvayaḥ na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvita tvam pratīyate yatra dhūmaḥ asti tatra agneḥ astitvena anvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ na tu evam yatra śabdaḥ asti tatra arthaḥ asti iti niścayaḥ na tāvat tatra deśe asau tad kāle vā avagamyate 
SV_5,7.87cd–5,7.90cd	 bhavet nitya vibhu tvāt ced sarva artheṣu ca tat samam tena sarvatra dṛṣṭa tvāt vyatirekasya ca āgateḥ sarva śabdaiḥ aśeṣa artha pratipattiḥ prasajyate atha evam deśa kālābhyām asatya tva prakalpane vācaka pratyayam kaḥ cit brūyāt artha dhiyā anvitam na evam api asti dṛṣṭaḥ hi vinā api artha dhiyā kva cit vācaka pratyayaḥ asmābhiḥ avyutpanna narān prati 
SV_5,7.91ab–5,7.94ab	 dvitīya ādi prayoge ca bhavet anvaya kalpanā śata kṛtvas prayukte api na ca dṛṣṭa artha dhīḥ kva cit nanu ye jñāta sambandhāḥ teṣām dṛṣṭaḥ anvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ yadi evam anvayāt pūrvam sambandhaḥ kaḥ api kalpitaḥ na aṅgam artha dhiyām eṣā bhavet anvaya kalpanā anvaya adhīna janma tvam anumānasya ca sthitam jñāte pratīti sāmarthye tad vaśāt eva jāyate

SV_5,7.101cd–5,7.104ab	 pramite ca prayukta tvāt anuvādaḥ adhikāt vinā adṛṣṭa pūrve tu ajñānam sambandha pratyayaḥ api vā sambandhaḥ na ca tasya arthaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ sa tu anya gocaraḥ parokṣe ananubhūte ca na abhidheye matiḥ bhavet parokṣaḥ ca anubhūtaḥ ca yaḥ tatra smṛtiḥ iṣyate pramite ca pravṛtta tvāt smṛteḥ na asti pramāṇatā 
SV_5,7.104cd–5,7.107cd	 pariccheda phala tvāt dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate tādātvika pariccheda phala tvena pramāṇatā pratyabhijñāna vat kasmāt smṛteḥ api na kalpyate yāvān pūrva paricchinnaḥ tāvān eva avadhāryate smṛtyā tad anusāreṇa tadā asattve asya na eva dhīḥ padam abhyadhika abhāvāt smārakāt na viśiṣyate pada ādhikyam bhavet kiñ cit tad padasya na gocaraḥ 
SV_5,7.108ab–5,7.111cd	 prāṇam anumānam vā yadi api syāt padāt mitiḥ vākya arthasya āgama artha tvāt doṣaḥ na āgama vādinām vākya arthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandha anubhavāt ṛte buddhiḥ utpadyate tena bhinnā asau= akṣa buddhi vat vākya adhikaraṇe ca asya hetoḥ siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati sarveṣām ca paroktānām vākya buddhau= asiddha tā vākyeṣu adṛṣṭeṣu api sārthakeṣu padārtha vid mātra tayā pratītim dṛṣṭvā anumāna vyatireka bhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padā bheda vicāraṇāyām 
SV_5,8.1ab–5,8.4ab	 kīdṛś gavayaḥ iti evam pṛṣṭaḥ nāgarikaiḥ yadi bravīti āraṇyakaḥ vākyam yathā gauḥ gavayaḥ tathā etasmin upamāna tvam prasiddham śabare punar tasya āgamā bahirbhāvāt anyathā eva upavarṇitam puruṣa pratyayena eva tatra arthaḥ sampratīyate tadīya vacana tvena tasmāt āgamaḥ eva saḥ sadṛśāt upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśa antare 
SV_5,8.4cd–5,8.7cd	 dhyāna ādi smṛti tulya tvāt sā pramāṇam katham bhavet deśa kāla ādi bhedena yathā anyatra viśiṣyate prameyam na evam asti atra nagara stha anusārataḥ śruta atideśa vākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ yā sa upamānam keṣān cit go sādṛśya anurañjitāḥ pratyakṣaḥ gavayaḥ tāvat sādṛśya smṛtiḥ atra tu nanu sādṛśya yukte arthe na smṛtiḥ na indriyāt gatiḥ 
SV_5,8.8ab–5,8.11ab	 pūrva vākya artha vijñānāt na ādhikyam gavaye yadi smaraṇāt aviśiṣṭa tvāt saṅgateḥ na pramāṇatā atha tu adhika tā kā cit pratyakṣa ādi vaśāt bhavet yāvat hīndriya sambandhaḥ tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam syaryamāṇasya ca aṃśasya vivedena apramāṇa tā śruta atideśa vākya tvam na ca atīva upayujyate ye api hi aśruta tad vākyāḥ teṣām api bhavati ayam 
SV_5,8.11cd–5,8.14cd	 pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa go tvānām vane gavaya darśinām atha saṃjñā anusandhānam teṣām na asti iti varṇyate na nāma vastu tat tāvat sarvathā taiḥ pratīyate na ca śabda artha sambandhaḥ prameyaḥ atra tat eṣyate sādṛśya avadhṛte vākye vākyāt avagataḥ hi asau na ca asya pratyabhijñānam punar utpadyate vane śaktyoḥ atīndriya tvena smṛtiḥ eva hi seṣyate 
SV_5,8.15ab–5,8.18ab	 śabda anuviddha bodhe api pratyakṣam upapāditam tasmāt sādṛśya yukta arthaḥ prameyaḥ apūrvaḥ ucyatām vyavasāya ātmaka tvam tu pratyakṣasya yat eṣyate jāti ādi vat tadā tena sādṛśyam kim na mīyate pratyakṣa ābhāsam etat tu nirvikalpaka vādinām prameya vastu abhāvāt ca nābhi pretā pramāṇa tā sādṛśyasya api vastu tvam na śakyam apabādhitum 
SV_5,8.18cd–5,8.21cd	 bhūyas avayava sāmānya yogaḥ jāti antarasya tat sadṛśa avayava tvam tu yatra padma dala akṣi vat tat sva avayava sāmānya bhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati evam jāti guṇa dravya kriyā śakti svadharmataḥ ekaika dvi tri sāmastya bhedāt etasya citra tā na dharmāḥ eva sādṛśyam bhūyas tāḥ vā tad āśrayā bhūyas tva vat hi jāti ādi sadṛśa tvena dṛśyate 
SV_5,8.22ab–5,8.25ab	 yamayoḥ katham etat ced dṛṣṭa tvāt kim iha ucyate kva cit dhi bhūyasām etat kva cit alpīyasām api na etāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastu tvam tasya hīyate sāmānyāni api ca etāni na aśīni āśraya nāśataḥ ananta āśraya yogāt ca na nāśaḥ anyatra vidyate tena sarvam na sāmānyam nitya tvena prakalpyate sāmānyānām na vā nāśaḥ kva cit abhyupagamyate 
SV_5,8.25cd–5,8.28cd	 sarvasya hi āśrayaḥ kaḥ cit asti deśa antara ādiṣu teṣām bhūyas tayā ca idam sādṛśyam atiricyate tāni vyastāni santi evam pratyakṣe api kva cit kva cit sadṛśa avayava tvam tu yatra nāma pratīyate tat api avayavānām syāt samāna vayava antaraiḥ evam tāvat yatas na asti parābheda prakalpanā tatas param tu sāmānyam bhavet sādṛśya varjitam 
SV_5,8.29ab–5,8.32ab	 pradhānānām tu sāmānyam yatra ekam sampratīyate saḥ eva iti bhavet tatra tad bhede sadṛśa tu adhīḥ citra ādau yatra sādṛśyam sāmānyam tatra kim bhavet tatra api pṛthivī varṇa viśeṣa ādi samāna tā rūpa gandha rasānām ca kasya cit tulya tā kva cit na avaśyam sarva sāmānyāt sādṛśyam upajāyate pṛthivī ādiṣu ca eteṣām satām eva svabhāvataḥ 
SV_5,8.32cd–5,8.35cd	 pariṇāma ādibhiḥ vyaktiḥ yathādṛṣṭi avadhāryate na hi śakti ātmanā kiñ cit asajjama prapadyate dharmāṇām na ca nānātvam asti ca avāntara ra sthitiḥ vastu tve sati ca asya evam sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā dvayoḥ ekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣa tvam na vāryate sāmānya vat ca sādṛśyam eka ekatra samāpte pratiyogini adṛṣṭe api tasmāt tat upapadyate

SV_5,8.39cd–5,8.42cd	 viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvena na anumāna apramāṇa tā yatra tu asadṛśāt eva kalpayitvā upajāyate sādṛśya pratyayaḥ tatra tad ābhāsa tva kalpanā bādhaka pratyayāt ca eṣā sādṛśya ābhāsa tā matā yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyam kuñjara ādinā samīpa sthaḥ api jānāti sādṛśyam na iti tatra hi na bādhyate samīpa ādau yat tu sādṛśyam eva tat

SV_5,8.46cd–5,8.49cd	 sādṛśyena saha eva asmin tadā eva utpadyate matiḥ śṛṅgi tva ādeḥ atha ucyeta sambandhāt liṅgatā gavi na teṣām gavaya jñāna vyāpāram pratyupakṣayāt yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syāt niḥsādṛśya eva sā bhavet na gauḥ śṛṅga ādi sadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu sadṛśa pratyayam dṛṣṭvā śṛṅga ādi pratyayāt param gavaya pratyayāt eva go jñānam upajāyate

SV_5,9.54ab–5,9.56cd	 abhāva śabda vācya tvāt pratyakṣa ādeḥ ca bhidyate pramāṇānām abhāvaḥ hi prameyāṇām abhāva vat abhāvaḥ vā pramāṇena sva anurūpeṇa mīyate prameya tvāt yathā bhāvaḥ tasmāt bhāva ātmakāt pṛthak karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvaiḥ yathāvat ca yad aṅga kāṇḍaiḥ na saṅgatāni iha parasparam ca na aṅgam tat etat prabhavam kratūnām

SV_5,10.1ab–5,10.4ab	 para loka phalāḥ pūrvam ākṣiptāḥ codanāḥ paraiḥ idānīm aihikākṣepaḥ sūtrakāreṇa codyate citrā paśu phala tva ādi viṣayāḥ codaṇā mṛṣā pratyakṣa ādi adhikāre api taiḥ artha asaṅgatiḥ yatas yadi īdṛś tat mṛṣā dṛṣṭam vipralipsoḥ yathā vacaḥ nadī tīre phalāni iti tatra adṛśyāni tāni ced na vā paśuphalā citrā sva kāle tat adānaḥ 
SV_5,10.4cd–5,10.7cd	 snāna bhujya ādi vat te api tad sādhyāḥ na bhavanti vā tad utpattau= asadbhāvāt svarge tṛpti sukha ādi vat vaidharmyeṇa ubhayatra api bhavetām sukham ardane ānantaryam ayuktam ced na sāmarthya avabodhanāt śabda eka deśa bhūtena tena tat pratipāditam kāla antara anupādānāt karma svābhāvyataḥ api ca codyamānasya citra ādeḥ ānantaryam viśeṣaṇam 
SV_5,10.8ab–5,10.11ab	 atra tāvat asaṃvādaḥ virodhaḥ ca uttarasya tu svarga yāna viruddhaḥ hi bhasmībhāvaḥ atra dṛśyate yajña āyudhi vacaḥ mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ sādharmyeṇa śilā vākyam vaidharmyeṇa āpta bhāṣitam śarīrāt yadi ca anyaḥ syāt na asau yajña āyudhī bhavet na ca asya yajamāna tvam sadbhāvaḥ api ca durlabhaḥ yadi syāt vidhi śabdaḥ atra na eva adarśanataḥ bhavet 
SV_5,10.11cd–5,10.15cd	 viśeṣaḥ asya iti bhedena na upāttam syāt idam tatas vidhi śabde bhaviṣyat tvam phalasya parikalpya hi virodha parihāraḥ syāt vartamāne api na asti asau phalam ca na bhavet evam bhasmībhāvāt vidhau api tad sāmarthyena yā ca anyā kalpanā tām niṣedhati prāyas ca evamprakāra tvam artha vādeṣu dṛśyate mantreṣu ca iti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnaḥ evam sati agnihotra ādi vākyeṣu api mṛṣā artha tā veda vākya eka deśa tvāt citra ādi vacaneṣu api 
SV_5,11.1ab–5,11.4ab	 sva pakṣa sādhanam tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikam vacaḥ sva arthe vaktra napekṣa tvāt padārtha pada buddhi vat tad kṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyak nitya vākya udbhava tvataḥ vākya buddhi vat eva atra pūrva uktāḥ ca api hetavaḥ nityān śabda artha sambandhān āśritya uktena hetunā svatas prāmāṇya siddhi artham aprāmāṇye niḥ kṛte asambandha udbhava tvena paraḥ mithyātvam abravīt 
SV_5,11.4cd–5,11.7ab	 sambandhaḥ asti ca nityaḥ ca iti uktam autpattika ādinā mithyā tu asya nirāsa artham tad paraiḥ na iṣyate dvayam na eva ca asti atra sambandhaḥ kṛtakaḥ vā iti vakṣyate asambhavena śeṣāṇām saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate asmin eva ca sambandhe pratītiḥ laukikaḥ dhruvāḥ tat niṣedham atas prāha na śabdaḥ arthena saṅgataḥ 
SV_5,11.7cd–5,11.10cd	 tad deśa anantara adṛṣṭeḥ vindhyaḥ himavatā yathā evam arthaḥ dvayam vā api sādhanīyam asaṅgatam kṣura ityādi ca siddhi artha hetoḥ uktam atha aparaḥ śakti rūpam gṛhītvā āha saṃśleṣaḥ yadi vāryate sambandha siddha sādhya tvam atha sambandha mātrakam pitāputra ādi sambandhaiḥ anekāntaḥ prasajyate eka bhūmi ādi sambandhāt dṛṣṭānte sādhya hīna tā 
SV_5,11.11ab–5,11.14ab	 vācya vācaka sambandha niṣedhe loka bādhanam virodhaḥ ca sva vākyena na hi sambandha varjitaiḥ pratijñā artham padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayitum paraḥ abhidhāna kriyāyām hi karma tvam vācya saṃśritam śabdānām karaṇa tvam vā kartṛ tvam vā nirūpitam pratipattau upādānāt sāhitye ca vivakṣite niyamyate yat ekasyām sambandhaḥ saḥ artha śabdayoḥ 
SV_5,11.14cd–5,11.17cd	 tatra yadi api asambandhaḥ kārakāṇām parasparam tathā api yat kriyā tasyām upakārya upakāritā sa kriyā saṅgateḥ paścāt sambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ na ca atra api avinā abhāvaḥ upayogi iti sādhitam saṃjñā iti gamaka tvam ced na tad aṅgam iyam bhavet gamayantīm śrutim dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ na ca eṣā gamayati artham sambandhe anavadhārite 
SV_5,11.18ab–5,11.21ab	 tasmāt gamakatā paścāt dhūma ādeḥ iva jāyate sa anaṅgam tadvat eva syāt na iyam dhūma ādibhiḥ samāḥ nirūpite avinā abhāve tatra tad kāritā hi asau gamaka tvena pūrvam ca tatra na utpadyate matiḥ iha vācaka tāyāḥ prāk na avinā bhāvita amatiḥ yat eva ca iha sambandham vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate tadā eva gamakaḥ asya ayam iti na anya svarūpataḥ 
SV_5,11.21cd–5,11.24cd	 kathayanti kva cit tāvat boddhavyaḥ asmāt ayam tu iti kva cit vācakaḥ iti evam vācyaḥ ayam iti ca ucyate kva cit uccaritāt śabdāt dṛṣṭvā artha viṣayām kriyām keṣān cit tatra boddhṛ tvam anumānāt pratīyate etena asmāt yatas śabdāt arthaḥ ayam avadhāritaḥ tena nūnam imau siddhau vācya vācaka śaktikau ittham vācaka tā siddhā saṅkīrṇā api tatas param 
SV_5,11.25ab–5,11.28ab	 anvaya vyatirekābhyām niṣkṛṣṭe arthe niyamyate bahu jāti guṇa dravya karma bhedau= alamvinaḥ pratyayāt sahasā jātā śrautala akṣaṇika ātmakāt na lokaḥ kāranā bhāvān nirdhārayitum icchati bala abala ādi siddhi artham vākya jñāḥ tu viviñcate kakṣa antarita sāmānya viśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ sāmānya vacanaḥ śabdaḥ jāyate lakṣaṇā bālāt 
SV_5,11.28cd–5,11.31cd	 tena avaśyam vivektavyam jāyate lakṣaṇa abalāt kiyat vā nitya sambandhāt abhidheyena lakṣyate tatra prayoga bāhulyāt tad viśeṣeṣu asatsu api prayogāt para sāmānye sati vācya prayogataḥ sāsnādi eka artha sambandhi go tva mātrasya vācakaḥ go śabdaḥ iti vijñānam anvayavyatireka jam tasmāt gamaka tā eva ādau abhidhāyaka tā punar 
SV_5,11.32ab–5,11.35ab	 tad nimittā iti sambandhaḥ saṃjñā saṃjñi tva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandha niyamaḥ ayam tu yā avinā abhāvita ucyate sambandha grahaṇāt pūrva yasmāt na gamayati atas gavā ādeḥ na abhidhā śaktiḥ devadatta pade yathā yathā eva gamakaḥ śabdaḥ vyavahārāt pratīyate tathā eva śakti vijñānam tasya upāyaḥ avagamyate svarūpa grahaṇam ca asya yathā vyāpriyate phale 
SV_5,11.35cd–5,11.38cd	 tathā sambandhi vijñānam na aśaktiḥ tad kṛtā bhavet yat sādhakatama tvena kasya cit kiñ cit ucyate tasya anugrāhaka apekṣā na sva śakti vighātinī na hi tat kāraṇam loke vede vā kiñ cit īdṛśam itikartavya tā sādhye yasya na anugrahe arthitā pratyātma niyata tvāt ca yathā eva karaṇam bhavet bāhya antara vibhāgena kva cit syāt vā vivakṣayā 
SV_5,11.39ab–5,11.42ab	 udvignaḥ hi andhakāreṇa kaḥ cit evam bravīti api kim cakṣuṣā mama etena dṛṣṭam dīpena yat mayā nitya vṛttau tu na andhānām dṛṣṭiḥ dīpa śataiḥ api rūpa ādi darśane yasmāt tasmāt cakṣuḥ prakāśakam śarīra ātma manaḥ yogāt asādhāraṇa ātābalāt vijñāna asatti bhāvāt ca cakṣuḥ kāraṇam iṣyate tathā eva iha api sambandha jñānam aṅgam prasiddhitaḥ 
SV_5,11.42cd–5,11.46cd	 gauravāt karaṇa tvena matam ced kena vāryate yathā cakṣuḥ iti idam tu vyabhicāri tvam ucyate devadatte api ca avyaktām śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ prakāśe avasthite bāhye na andhaḥ rūpam pratīyate phala anantaryatas ca api cakṣuḥ karaṇñam iṣyate puruṣa adhīna vijñānaḥ tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ yaḥ saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandhaḥ sa ca iṣṭaḥ ced dhruvam kṛtaḥ bhinna deśa ādi adhiṣṭhānāt yathā rajju ghaṭa ādiṣu samam na asti anayoḥ kiñ cit tena asaṅgatatā svatas 
SV_5,12.1ab–5,12.4ab	 ādhāra ātmani viñāte sukham ādheya bodhanam tasya eva tāvat prastāvāt atha gauḥ iti atas abravīt pratyakṣe api visaṃvādaḥ yeṣām kaḥ svayam uttaram tebhyaḥ dadyāt iti jñātvā vṛddhānām matam abravīt tatra artha pratyaya dvāram kṛtam śabda nirūpaṇam yaiḥ āsatām tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate pratyakṣam na asamartham naḥ tena ca arthe avadhārite 
SV_5,12.4cd–5,12.7ab	 na hetuḥ balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tatas tasmāt śrotra paricchinnaḥ yadi artham gamayet na vā sarvathā tasya śabda tvam loka siddham na hīyate yadi tu artha gatau śaktiḥ na syāt asya tatas punar vastu antaram prakalpyeta vinā śabda prasiddhitaḥ agni ādīn gamayantaḥ api śabdāḥ dhūma ādayaḥ na hi 
SV_5,12.7cd–5,12.10cd	 na vā apratyāyaka tvāt syāt eka varṇeṣu aśabda tā na ca prāc artha vijñānāḥ chotra grāhye na śabda dhīḥ na ca artha jñānataḥ paścāt aśrautre api ca śabda tā paraspara anapekṣāḥ ca śrotra buddhyā svarūpataḥ varṇāḥ eva avagamyante na pūrva apara vastunī alpīyasā api yatnena śabdam uccaritam matiḥ yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇam vā sakalam sphuṭam 
SV_5,12.11ab–5,12.14ab	 pṛthak na ca upalabhyante varṇasya avayavāḥ kva cit na ca varṇeṣu anusyūtāḥ dṛśyante tantu vat paṭe teṣām anupalabdheḥ ca na jñātā liṅga saṅgatiḥ na āgamaḥ tad paraḥ ca asti na adṛṣṭe ca upamā kva cit na ca api anupapattiḥ syāt varṇasya avayavaiḥ vinā yathā anya avayavānām hi vinā api avayava antaraiḥ pratyakṣeṇa avabuddhaḥ ca varṇaḥ avayava varjitaḥ 
SV_5,12.14cd–5,12.17ab	 kim na syāt vyoma vat ca atra liṅgam tat rahitā matiḥ tadvat ca asya ekabuddhi tvāt deśa bhede api abhinnatā nanu bheda matiḥ na syāt tava api eka tvadhīḥ kutas sāmānyeṣu mama ekā dhīḥ tad vyaktiṣu ca bheda dhīḥ na hi iṣṭam bheda mātram hi na syāt eka tva dhīḥ yatas vyakteḥ tāvat na sāmānyam bhinna rūpam pratīyate 
SV_5,12.17cd–5,12.20cd	 varṇeṣu anyatra śabda tvāt na anyat ced varṇaḥ eva saḥ saḥ eva iti matiḥ na api sādṛśyam na ca tat kva cit vinā avayava sāmānyāt varṇeṣu avayavāḥ na ca pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt ca na anya apohaḥ api yujyate vācakaḥ ca atra liṅgam vā na tadānīm pratīyate gakāra ādiṣu sāmānyam śabda tvam kalpyate yathā go tvam ca śābaleya ādau tathā etat kim na kalpyate 
SV_5,12.21ab–5,12.24ab	 śābaleyaga kāra dīn niṣpannān vyakti rūpataḥ sāmānya dhīḥ na gṛhṇāti iti atas jātiḥ api iṣyate na tu druta ādi bhede api niṣpannā sampratīyate gavyakti antara vyāvṛttā gavyaktiḥ aparā sphuṭāḥ tena ekatvena varṇasya buddhiḥ ekopajāyate viśeṣa buddhi sadbhāvaḥ bhavet vyañjaka bhedataḥ yathā eva tava gatvā ādi gamyamānam druta ādibhiḥ 
SV_5,12.24cd–5,12.27cd	 viśeṣaiḥ api na anekam evam varṇaḥ api naḥ bhavet tvayā api vyañjaka vyakti bhedāt bhedaḥ abhyupeyate mama api vyañjakaiḥ nādaiḥ bheda buddhiḥ bhaviṣyati tena yat prārthyate jāte tat varṇāt eva labhyate vyakti labhyam ca nādebhyaḥ iti gatvā ādi dhīḥ yathā kalpayitvā api tad paścāt vibhu tvā eka tva nitya tāḥ pratyeka vṛtti tā ca asya bhaveyuḥ mahataḥ śramāt 
SV_5,12.28ab–5,12.31ab	 dvaya siddhaḥ tu varṇa ātmā nitya tva ādi yathā eva ca kalpitasya iṣyate tadvat siddhasya eva abhyupeya tām pratyeka samavāye ca kleśaḥ na eva bhaviṣyati vyañjaneṣu ca dhī bhedaḥ na eva tādṛś pratīyate dṛśyate ajanurāgeṇa bhedaḥ yaḥ nāma tatra naḥ vivedaḥ asti eva na hi eṣa kevalānām pratīyate akṣu api evam para upādhiḥ druta ādi pratyayaḥ yathā 
SV_5,12.31cd–5,12.34cd	 varṇāḥ aaśrita tvāt varṇa tva vyañjana pratyayaḥ yathā gakāraḥ atyanta niṣkṛṣṭa gatvā ādhāraḥ na gamyate gānyabuddhi anirūpya tvāt paraiḥ kalpita gatva vat avastu tvena sādhya tvāt niṣedhāt dhetu sādhyayoḥ sa pakṣe anyatara asiddhiḥ na doṣāya atra jāyate varṇa tvāt ca api sādhyaḥ ayam yakāra ādi vat eva ca vyatirekasya ca adṛṣṭeḥ na atra dṛṣṭam nirvartakam 
SV_5,12.35ab–5,12.38ab	 go tva ādi vāraṇe tu eva dṛṣṭa bādhaḥ sphuṭaḥ bhavet na anyathā hi matiḥ tatra syāt sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ na ca api atra eka vastu tve bhedaḥ vyañjaka bhedataḥ na piṇḍa vyatirekeṇa vyañjakaḥ atra dhvaniḥ yathā piṇḍavyaṅgyā eva go tva ādiḥ jātiḥ nityam pratīyate tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātiḥ ekā pratīyate nanu yasya dvayam śrotram tasya buddhi dvayam bhavet 
SV_5,12.38cd–5,12.41cd	 bhavataḥ atīndriya tvāt tu katham nādaiḥ viśeṣa dhīḥ nādena saṃskṛtāt śrotrāt yadā śabdaḥ pratīyate tad upaśleṣaḥ tat asya bodham ke cit pracakṣate na eva vā grahaṇam teṣām śabde buddhiḥ tu tad vaśāt saṃskāra anukṛteḥ saḥ api mahatva ādi avabudhyate madhuram tikta rūpeṇa śvetam pītatayā tathā gṛhṇanti pitta doṣeṇa viṣayam bhrānta cetasaḥ 
SV_5,12.42ab–5,12.45ab	 tathā vegena dhāvantaḥ nāvi ārūḍhāḥ ca gacchataḥ parvata ādīn vijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataḥ ca tān maṇḍūka vasayā akta akṣāḥ vaṃśa anuraga buddhibhiḥ vyakti alpa tva mahat tvābhyām sāmānyam ca tad āśrtayam gṛhṇanti yadvat etāni nimitta grahaṇāt vinā vyañjaka stham abudhvā eva vyaṅgye bhrāntiḥ bhaviṣyati varṇa antara tvam eva āhuḥ ke cit dīrgha plupta ādiṣu 
SV_5,12.45cd–5,12.48cd	 na hi druta ādi vat tatra prayohaḥ na antarīyakaḥ tathā ca sati sāmānyam triṣu atvam kaiḥ cit iṣyate sāmānya kalpanā tu anyaiḥ na yuktā iti abhidhīyate atvam iti ucyamānam hi na dīrgha plutayoḥ bhavet ātvam na hrasva plutayoḥ traimātryam na ca pūrvayoḥ sarva sādhāraṇa tvena tat vijñātum na śkyate pratyekam śābaleya ādi rūpe go tvam yathā sphuṭam 
SV_5,12.49ab–5,12.52ab	 avarṇa kula śabdaḥ api sthāna sāmyāt vana ādi vat samudāya artha vācī iti na jāti vacanaḥ bhavet svatas hrasva ādi bhedaḥ tu nitya vāde virudhyate sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa katham mātrikaḥ svayam tasmāt uccāraṇam tasya mātrā kālam pratīyate dvi mātram vā tri mātram ā na varṇaḥ mātrikaḥ svaym dīrgha ādeḥ nanu anaṅga tvam vācaka adharmataḥ bhavet 
SV_5,12.52cd–5,12.55ab	 ittham pratīyamānāḥ syuḥ varṇāḥ na pratipādakāḥ yādṛśāt pūrva dṛṣṭaḥ asau arthaḥ gamyate tādṛśāt bhrāntyā katham pratītiḥ ced na asau artham iti prati yathā aśva ādi javaḥ puṃsām kārya aṅga tvam prakalpayet para dharmaḥ api varṇānām dhvani dharmāḥ tathā eva naḥ nanu dīrgha ādi anitya tvāt anityaḥ vācakaḥ bhavet 
SV_5,12.55cd–5,12.58cd	 ānupūrvīvat eva asya parihāraḥ bhaviṣyati tathā udātta ādi bhedānām saṃskāra vaśagā matiḥ teṣām dīrgha ādi vat bhedaḥ na kadā cit pratīyte tatra eka varṇa rūpa tve bhedaḥ api syāt druta ādi vat na atra varṇa antara vyaktiḥ iva dhvani antara udbhavaḥ te eva mṛdu tīvra tva śīghra tva ādi samanvitāḥ abhede ca api varṇasya dhvanīnām dvi prakāra tā 
SV_5,12.59ab–5,12.62ab	 ke cit svarūpa bodha arthāḥ ke cit bodha anuvartinaḥ yugapad krama rūpeṇa saṃskāra utpāda hetavaḥ tatra dīrgha ādi bodhaḥ syāt pūrveṣām pracayaḥ yadā varṇa ātmā eva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate yugapad pracitaiḥ taiḥ ca syāt udātta ādi kalpanā pracaye tu itareṣām syāt vati bhedaḥ druta ādikaḥ varṇa ātmani avabuddhe api tad rūpām eva te matim 
SV_5,12.62cd–5,12.65cd	 śanais utpādayanti iti na anyaḥ varṇaḥ pratīyate vyakti ākṛti kṛtaḥ bhedaḥ yadi api ekāntataḥ bhavet varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣaḥ tathā api na virudhyate nitya tva yatnaḥ sarvaḥ api gatvā ādiṣu bhaviṣyati gakāra ādi vacaḥ ca etat teṣu eva na virotsyate vicchinna yatna vyaṅgyaiḥ ca nityaiḥ sarva gataiḥ api vyatirikta pada ārambhaḥ varṇaiḥ na atra upapadyate 
SV_5,12.66ab–5,12.69ab	 anārabdhe ca go śabde go śabda tvam katham bhavet varṇa sāmānya vat ca api na tad kalpanam arhati varṇa ātmanām abhedāt ca siddhā sāmānya dhīḥ api samudāyaḥ api tebhyaḥ asyaḥ vā araṇīyaḥ anayā diśā abheda samudāyaḥ tu teṣām dharmaḥ na duṣyati teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam artha pratyāyanam prati yāvantaḥ yādṛśaḥ ye ca yad artha pratipādane 
SV_5,12.69cd–5,12.72cd	 varṇāḥ prajñāta sāmarthyāḥ te tathiva avabodhakāḥ teṣām tu guṇa bhūtānām artha pratyāyanam prati sāhityam eka kartṛ ādi kramaḥ ca api vivakṣitaḥ kartrā eka tve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam prayuñjānasya yat pūrvam vṛddhebhyaḥ krama darśanam yaugapdyam tu aśakya tvāt na eva teṣām iha āśritam kartṛ bhedaḥ ca tatra syāt na ca evam dṛśyate abhidhā 
SV_5,12.73ab–5,12.76ab	 yugapad dṛśya sāmarthyāḥ na eva śaktāḥ krame yathā bhāvāḥ tathā krame śaktāḥ yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ca pūrṇamāsa ādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatya kāriṇaḥ abhyāsānām ca loke api svādhyāya grahaṇa ādiṣu sādhana ādi trayāṇām ca vyāpārasya eka kālatā sarvatra asti iti na iha syāt upālambhaḥ kramam prati niṣpannāḥ eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarve eva hi 
SV_5,12.76cd–5,12.79cd	 sūkṣmāḥ vyāpāra bhedāḥ tu dṛśyate na kadā canaḥ eka sādhana sāṃsthāḥ ca vyāpāra avayavāḥ yadā svarūpataḥ nirīkṣyante yaugapadyam asat tadā kim punar bahavaḥ bhinnāḥ bhinna sādhana saṃśritāḥ bhaveyuḥ yaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ krama vartinaḥ yadā tu ādya parispandāt prabhṛtyā phala lābhataḥ kriyā pūrva parībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā 
SV_5,12.80ab–5,12.83ab	 tena atra api vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā artha avabodhanāt sākalyena īkṣyamāṇe syāt vyāpāre varttamāna tā pratyekam ye punar tatra vyāpārāḥ tad nirūpaṇam phala aniṣpattitaḥ na syāt nāstitvam na ca tāvatā phala anumeya tāyām ca vyāpārasya phalam prati kārakāṇām yathāsthānam vyāpāre vartamāna tā avaśyam bhāvinī nityam pratyāsattiḥ ca kasya cit 
SV_5,12.83cd–5,12.86cd	 na tāvatā vyapeta tvāt itareṣām anaṅga tā dvi antara eka antara tvena gakārau kārayoḥ dhruvam artham pratyāyane śaktiḥ tatra sthau gamakau yatas yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śakta tā tathā eva itarayoḥ śaktiḥ ānantarye na vidyate na ca yatra ekaśas aśaktiḥ tatra sarveṣu aśakta tā tathā hi aṅgāni dṛśyante śāli ādi vahana ādiṣu 
SV_5,12.87ab–5,12.89cd	 śaktiḥ tatra asti kā cit dhi vahane sā samṛddhyate saṅghātena tu varṇānām pratyekam kā cidīkṣyate na hi artha avayavaḥ kaḥ cit pratyekam taiḥ pratīyate samastasya atha vā kaḥ cit bodha leśaḥ atra jāyate rathasya api tu yat kāryam śāli ādi vahanam na tat pratyekam dṛśyate kiñ cit manāk api yathā īhitam 
SV_5,12.90ab–5,12.93ab	 ath a yat kiñcid ucyeta vahane tat iha api naḥ sva ātma pratyaya hetu tvam varṇeṣu arthe api vā kva cit yasya anavayavaḥ sphoṭaḥ vyajyate varṇa buddhibhiḥ saḥ api paryanuyogena vā eva etena vimucyate tatra api prativarṇam hi pada sphoṭaḥ na gamyate na ca avayavaśas vyaktiḥ tad abhāvāt na ca atra śrīḥ pratyekam ca api aśaktānām samudāye api aśaktayā 
SV_5,12.93cd–5,12.96cd	 tatra yaḥ parihāraḥ te sa naḥ atra api bhaviṣyati sadbhāva vyatirekau ca tathā avayava varjanam tava adhikam bhavet tasmāt yatnaḥ asau artha buddhiṣu na anyathā anupapattiḥ ca bhavet artha matim prati tat eva asyāḥ nimittam syāt jāyate yat anantaram sā ca varṇa dvaya jñāne atīte antya jñānataḥ parā bhavati iti īdṛś eva asyāḥ nimittam avakalpate 
SV_5,12.97ab–5,12.100ab	 vinā saṃskāra kalpena tad anantara vṛttitaḥ kṛta anugraha sāmarthyaḥ varṇaḥ antyaḥ pratipādakaḥ eṣaḥ eva tu saṃskāraḥ iti ke cit pracakṣate adṛsṭa kalpanā atītam tāvat mātram hi dṛśyate atha vā vāsanā eva astu saṃskāraḥ sarve eva hi dṛḍha jñāna gṛhīte arthe saṃskāraḥ asti iti manvate tasya artha buddhi hetu tve visaaṃvādaḥ asya nirṇaye 
SV_5,12.100cd–5,12.103cd	 tad bhāva bhāvitā hetuḥ anyatra iva pratīyate saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrva vṛt tattva kalpanam niṣpramāṇakam eva iti na anugraha phalam bhavet yadi api smṛti hetu tvam saṃskārasya vyavasthitam kārya antareṣu sāmarthyam na tasya pratiṣidhyate tena saṃskāra sadbhāvaḥ na anena evam prakalpyate tasya artha buddhi hetu tvam adṛṣṭam kevalam kṛtam 
SV_5,12.104ab–5,12.107ab	 śabda pakṣe api tat ca etat adṛṣṭa tvāt na mucyate kārya bodhana śakta tvam tulyam saṃskāra śabdayoḥ kṣīṇa arthāpattiḥ evam ca na sphoṭam parikalpayet saṃskāra kalpanā pūrvam avaśyam bhāvinī hi te dhvanibhyaḥ api aparaḥ tāvat neṣyeta artha matim prati te vā yadi upalabhyeran varṇāḥ pratyakṣataḥ na ca varṇānām yaugapadyena yadi ca avaśyam arthitā 
SV_5,12.107cd–5,12.110cd	 nitya tvāt sarvadā tat syāt na tu kāraṇa tā tathā ittham krama gṛhītānām yugapad yā atha vā parā sthitiḥ sā kāraṇam tu syāt nityam arthadhiyam prati yat vā pratyakṣatas pūrvam krama jñāneṣu yat param samasta varṇa vijñānam tad artha jñāna kāraṇam tatra jñāne ca varṇānām yaugapadyam pratīyate na avaśyam yaugapadyena pratyakṣa sthena tat bhavet 
SV_5,12.111ab–5,12.114ab	 citra rūpām cā tām buddhim sat asat varṇa gocarām ke cit āhuḥ yathā varṇaḥ gṛhyate antar pade pade antya varṇe api vijñāte pūrva saṃskāra kāritam smaraṇam yaugapadyena sarveṣu anye pracakṣate sarveṣu ca evam artheṣu mānasam sarva vādinām iṣṭam samuccaya jñānam krama jñāneṣu satsu api na ced tadā abhyupeyeta krama dṛṣṭeṣu na eva hi 
SV_5,12.114cd–5,12.117cd	 śata ādi rūpam jāyeta tat samuccaya darśanam tena śrotram anobhyām syāt kramāt varṇeṣu yadi api pūrva jñānam parastāt tu yugapad smaraṇam bhavet tad ārūḍhāḥ tatas varṇāḥ na dūre artha avabodhanāt śabda artha matiḥ tena laukikaiḥ abhidhīyate citra buddhyā anayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyaḥ vyatirekataḥ paścāt gauḥ iti vijñānam pratyakṣam kaiḥ cit iṣyate 
SV_5,12.118ab–5,12.121ab	 vailakṣaṇyam tu tasya iṣṭam ekaika jñānataḥ sphuṭam varṇa rūpa avabodhāt tu na tad artha antaram bhavet yadi ca artha antara tvam syāt ekaikasmāt trayasya tat varṇa traya parityāge buddhiḥ na anyatra jāyate gauḥ iti ekam ati tvam tu na eva asmābhiḥ nivāryate tad grāhya ekārthatābhyām ca śabde syāt eka tā matiḥ śaidhyāt alpa antara tvāt ca go śabde sā abhavet api 
SV_5,12.121cd–5,12.124cd	 deva datta ādi śabdeṣu sphuṭaḥ bhedaḥ pratīyate na gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti evam grantha sambandhanam bhavet asi akṣareṣu hetu tvam tat param vacanam hi tat śabdāt iti ca hetu tvam pañcamya atrā abhidhīyate bhavat pakṣe api ca ekāntāt jñānena vyavadhiḥ bhavet gauṇaḥ anyathā prasiddhaḥ vā prayujyeta anyathā yadi na ca anyādṛś nimitta tvam kasya cit sampratīyate 
SV_5,12.125ab–5,12.128ab	 sva vyāpāra vyavāyaḥ hi sarvasmin eva kārake dṛṣṭaḥ vyāpāraḥ īdṛś tu śabdasya iti avyavetatā gakāra ādeḥ yadā ca anyaḥ na loke śabdaḥ ucyate tadā tasmāt pratīte arthe śabdāt iti katham bhavet śabda jñāna ādi saṃskāra vyakta sphoṭa kṛte atha vā pratyaye śabda janya tvam iti gauṇam prasajyate saṃskāra janana artham ca na śabda uccāraṇam matam 
SV_5,12.128cd–5,12.131cd	 artha pratītim uddiśya prayuktasya kramāt ayam tasmāt tādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate samuccaya avabodhe tu vyavadhānam na kena cit yadi ca apūrva saṃskāraḥ itikartavyatā iṣyate varṇaḥ antyaḥ gamakaḥ tasya śabda tvāt mudhyatā bhavet varṇāḥ vā dhvanayaḥ vā api sphoṭam na pada vākyayoḥ vyañjanti vyañjaka tvena yathā dīpa prabhā ādayaḥ
