SV_5,12.132ab–5,12.137cd	 sattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat ca iti sādhanāni yathāruci laukika vyatirekeṇa kalpite arthe bhavanti hi na arthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭaḥ varṇebhyaḥ vyatirekataḥ ghaṭa avivat na dṛṣṭena virodhaḥ dharma siddhitaḥ pratiṣedhet tu yaḥ varṇān tad jñāna anantara udbhavān dṛṣṭa bādhaḥ bhavet tasya śaśi candra niṣedha vat varṇa utthā vā artha dhīḥ eṣā tad jñāna anantara udbhavāḥ yā īdṛśī sā tad utthāḥ hi dhūma ādeḥ iva bahni dhīḥ dīpa vat vā gakāra ādiḥ gavā ādeḥ pratipādakaḥ dhruvam pratīyamāna tvāt tat pūrvam pratipādanāt varṇa atiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandam phalam ādadhāti kāryāṇi vākya avayava āśrayāṇi satyāni katum kṛtaḥ eṣa yatnaḥ 
SV_5,13.1ab–5,13.4ab	 ākṛti vyatirikte arthe sambandhaḥ nityatā asya ca na sidhyetām iti jñātvā tat vācya tvam iha ucyate tad sadbhāva prasiddhi artham atra tāvat prayatyate vācya tve vakṣyate yuktiḥ vyaktyā saha bala abale jātim eva ākṛtim prāhuḥ vyaktiḥ ākriyate yayā sāmānyam tat ca piṇḍānām eka buddhi nibandhanam tad nimittam ca yat kiñcit sāmānyam śabda gocaram 
SV_5,13.4cd–5,13.7cd	 sarve eva icchati iti evam avirodhaḥ atra vādinām sarva vastuṣu buddhiḥ ca vyāvṛtti anugama ātmikā jāyate dvi ātma tvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati viśeṣa mātre iṣṭe ca na sāmānya matiḥ bhavet sāmānya mātra bodhe tu nirnimittāḥ viśeṣa dhīḥ na ca api anyatarā bhrāntiḥ upacāreṇa ca iṣyate dṛḍha tvāt sarvadā buddheḥ bhrāntiḥ tad bhrānti vādinām 
SV_5,13.8ab–5,13.11ab	 mukhyayoḥ ca api adṛṣṭa tvāt na upacāreṇa kalpanā bāhya artha viṣaya tvam ca buddhīnām pratipāditam anyonya apekṣitā nityam syāt sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ viśeṣāṇām ca sāmānyam te ca tasya bhavanti hi nirviśeṣam na sāmānyam bhavet śaśa viṣāṇa vat sāmānya rahita tvāt ca viśeṣāḥ tadvat eva hi tad anātmaka rūpeṇa hetū vācyau= imau punar 
SV_5,13.11cd–5,13.14cd	 tena tātyanta bhedaḥ api syāt sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sāmānya buddhi śakti tvam viśeṣeṣu eva yaḥ vadet vinā vastu antarāt tena vācyā śaktiḥ tu kīdṛśī grāhyā kim vā api asambodhāḥ bhinna ekā vā tathā eva ca gṛhyate yadi sā ekā ca jātiḥ eva anya śabdikā bhavet nirviṣayā buddhiḥ yadi śaktiḥ na gṛhyate na hi sadbhāva mātreṇa viśayaḥ kaḥ cit iṣyate 
SV_5,13.15ab–5,13.18ab	 paraspara vibhinna tvāt viśeṣāḥ na eka buddhibhiḥ gṛhyante viṣaya asattvāt śaktiḥ ca eṣām na vidyate bhinna tve vā api śaktīnām eka buddhiḥ na labhyate viśeṣa śakti abhede ca tāvat mātra matiḥ bhavet bhinnā viśeṣa śaktibhyaḥ sarvatra anugatā api ca pratyekam samavetā ca tasmāt jātiḥ api iṣyatām tena ātma dharmaḥ bhedānām ekadhī viṣayaḥ asti naḥ 
SV_5,13.18cd–5,13.21cd	 sāmānyam ākṛtiḥ jātiḥ śaktiḥ vā saḥ abhidhīyatām nanu bhinne api sattā ādau sāmānyam iti jāyate buddhiḥ vinā api sāmānyāt anyasmāt sā katham bhavet vana upanyāsa tulyaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ tvayā bhrānti tvena hi na etasyāḥ bhrāntiḥ go tva ādi dhīḥ api śabdāt pūrvam hi sarveṣu gavā ādau iva na eka dhīḥ vastu tvam ca atra sāmānyam dharmam ke cit pracakṣate 
SV_5,13.22ab–5,13.25ab	 evam tu kalpyamāne syāt sāmānyānām ananta tā punar tena saha anyeṣu sāmānya matiḥ asti hi viśeṣeṣu api vastu tvāt sāmānyam iti dhīḥ bhavet sattā ādiṣu iva ttena etat sāmānyam na upapadyate tasmāt ekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttiḥ tad nibandhanaḥ sāmānya śabdaḥ sattā ādau ekadhīkaraṇena vā piṇḍeṣu eva ca sāmānyam na antarā gṛhyate yatas 
SV_5,13.25cd–5,13.28cd	 na hi ākāśa vat icchanti sāmānyam nāma kiñ cana yat vā sarva gata tve api vyaktiḥ śakti anurodhataḥ śaktiḥ kārya anumeyāḥ hi vyakti darśana hetukāḥ tena yatra eva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktam tat eva tu tena eva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣu etat pratīyate bhinna tve api hi kāsān cit śaktiḥ kāḥ cit aśaktikāḥ na ca paryanuyogaḥ asti vastu śakteḥ kadā canaḥ 
SV_5,13.29ab–5,13.32ab	 vahniḥ dahati na ākāśam kaḥ atra paryanuyujyatām na ca anyā mṛgyate yuktiḥ yathā sandṛśyate tathā na hi yukti antaram na asti iti etat jñānam anarthakam dharmaḥ ca avyabhicāryasya na mṛgyaḥ upalakṣaṇe na anumānau= agamyam tat pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim svābhāvikaḥ ca sambandhaḥ jāti vyaktyoḥ na hetumān tena etasya prasiddhi artham na anyat sāmānyam iṣyate 
SV_5,13.32cd–5,13.35cd	 śakti siddhi vat etasya svabhāvaḥ atra na vāryate yat vā naimittika tve api tāvat mātra pratīkṣaṇāt viśeṣeṣu eva labdheṣu keṣu cit na anyavāñchanam na vyañjanti apare kasmāt yatas teṣu na dṛśyate tebhyaḥ api na nivṛtti artham mṛgyaḥ hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ sāmānyam na anyat iṣṭam ced tasya vṛtteḥ niyāmakam go tvena api vinā kasmāt go buddhiḥ na niyamyate 
SV_5,13.36ab–5,13.39ab	 yathā tulye api bhinna tve keṣu cit vṛtti apekṣitāḥ go tva ādeḥ animitte api tathā buddhiḥ bhaviṣyati viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnām vinā na utpattiḥ iṣyate viśeṣāt anyat icchanti sāmānyam tena tat dhruvam tāḥ hi tena vinā utpannāḥ mithyāḥ syuḥ viṣayāt ṛte na tu anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasya iha duṣyati aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabda anumānayoḥ 
SV_5,13.39cd–5,13.42cd	 na eva syāt na hi sambandhaḥ bhedaiḥ ānantyataḥ bhavet anubhūta tayā vā asau puruṣasya upayujyate jāti vyaktyoḥ tu sambandhe na anubhūtyā prayojanam siddhe viṣaya rūpe ca go tva ādau indriyaiḥ punar arthāpatti upalabdhā syāt śaktiḥ ekā niyāmikā na ca ātma hetum eva asau siddham bādhitum arhati śaktiḥ ca na etayā buddhyā na indriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate 
SV_5,13.43ab–5,13.46ab	 sāmānya antara yogānām aniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate tayā sāmānya nāśaḥ syāt sa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate sambandhaḥ tasya hetuḥ vā tad grahe na ca kāraṇam svarūpataḥ gṛhīte arthe paścāt etat vikalpyate sāsnādi eka artha sambandhi go tvam iti upalakṣaṇam na ca sva samavāyi eva kevalam cihnam iṣyate sāsnādibhyaḥ tu piṇḍasya bhedaḥ na atyantataḥ yadā 
SV_5,13.46cd–5,13.49cd	 sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyaḥ tadā syāt etat uttaram kasmāt sāsnādi matsu eva go tvam yasmāt tad ātmakam tādātmyam asya kasmāt ced svabhāvāt iti gamyatām upalabdhi anusāreṇa vyavasthā siddhiḥ īdṛśī svatas go tva ādi bhedaḥ tu na tu vyañjaka bhedataḥ sā bhūt druta ādi vat mithyā nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ bhedaḥ hasti ādi piṇḍebhyaḥ svatas ced iha tad samam 
SV_5,13.50ab–5,13.53ab	 vyaṅgya jāti viśeṣāt ced prāptam anyonya saṃśrayam tasmāt svābhāvikaḥ bhedaḥ jāti vyaktyoḥ pratīyate aneka ananya vṛtti t tvāt na sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ eka vastu ātma tā yuktāḥ varam tena aupacārikam bhinnebhyaḥ ca api abhinna tvāt bhedaḥ tat sva ātma vat bhavet ekasmāt vā api abhinna tvāt vyakti eka tvam pratīyate eka aneka tvam ekasya tathā anya ananyatā katham 
SV_5,13.53cd–5,13.56cd	 tat sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca iti evamādi ca duṣkaram virodhaḥ tāvat ekāntāt vaktum atra na yujyate sāmānya ananya vijñāte viśeṣe na eka vṛtti tā sāmānyān anya vṛtti tvam viśeṣa ātmā eka bhāvataḥ evan ca parihartavyā bhinna abhinna tva kalpanā kena cit dhi ātmanā eka tvam nānātvam ca asya kena cit sāmānyasya tu yaḥ bhedam brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ 
SV_5,13.57ab–5,13.60ab	 darśayitvā abhyupetavyam viśeṣa aikyam ca jātitaḥ yathā kalmāṣa varṇasya yatheṣṭam varṇa nigrahaḥ citra tvāt vastunaḥ api evam bheda abheda avadhāraṇam sāmānya aṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedaḥ yena prasādhyate tasya hetoḥ asiddha tvam siddhaḥ ced siddha sādhanam bhedebhyaḥ ananya rūpeṇa sāmānyam gṛhyate yadā tadā aviśeṣa mātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate 
SV_5,13.60cd–5,13.63cd	 tad udbhūtyā ca sāmānyam tad bhāva anuguṇam sthitam sat api agrāhya rūpa tvāt asadvat pratibhāti naḥ viśeṣān api sāmānyāt yadā bhedena buddhyate tadā sāmānya mātra tvam evam eva pratīyate yadā tu śabalam vastu yugapad pratipadyate tadā anyān anya bheda ādi sarvam eva pralīyate na ca tat tādṛśam kaḥ cit śabdaḥ śknoti bhāṣitum 
SV_5,13.64ab–5,13.67ab	 sāmānya aṃśān apoddhṛtya padam sarvam pravarttate samastavastu apekṣām ca padārthānām apoddhṛtim ke cit āhuḥ asat rūpam aṃśa tvam tu na vāryate sārūpyam eva sāmānyam piṇḍānām yena kalpyate tena sārūpya śabdena kim punar pratipadyate samāna rūpa bhāvaḥ ced jātiḥ sā asmābhiḥ iṣyate sādṛśyam atha sārūpyam kasya kena iti kathyatām 
SV_5,13.67cd–5,13.70cd	 na tāvat śālaleyena bāhuleya ādayaḥ samāḥ viśeṣa rūpataḥ ye api tad saṃsthāna ādibhiḥ samāḥ śābaleyaḥ iva iti syāt tatra buddhiḥ na gauḥ iva śābaleyaḥ ayam iti vā bhrāntyā gauḥ iti na asti dhīḥ śābaleya svarūpam ca na gauḥ iti avatiṣṭhate tad anyeṣu hi go buddhiḥ na syāt su sadṛśeṣu api dṛśyate sā na ca anyatra go rūpam tatra vidyate 
SV_5,13.71ab–5,13.76ef	 na ca anyaḥ gauḥ prasiddhaḥ asti tad sādṛśyena dhīḥ bhāvet na ca api saḥ iti jñānam sadṛśeṣu asti sarvadā sarva puṃsām atas bhrāntiḥ na eṣā bādhaka varjanāt sarva jñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante atra kalpane viśeṣa grahaṇa abhāvāt eva gauḥ kaḥ ca kathyatām babhūva yadi asau pūrvam asmad ādeḥ tad agrahāt sādṛśya avadhṛtiḥ na asti iti atas godhīḥ na labhyate na ca avayava sāmānyaiḥ vinā sādṛśya kalpanā sāmānya pratyaya utpādaḥ na viśeṣeṣu jāyate vyaktitaḥ ca atirekaḥ asya syāt na vā iti vicārite sāmānyam eva sādṛśyam bhavet vā vyakti mātrakam tena na atyanta bhinnaḥ arthaḥ sārūpyam iti varṇitam granthe vindhya nivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyam ucyate 
SV_5,14.1ab–5,14.4ab	 agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyam vācyam yaiḥ parikalpitam go tvam vastu eva taiḥ uktam agaḥ apoha girā sphuṭam bhāva antaram abhāvaḥ hi purastāt pratipāditaḥ tatra aśva ādi nivṛtti ātmā bhāvaḥ kaḥ iti kathyatām na iṣṭaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ tāvat viṣayaḥ nirvikalpanāt tathā ca śābaleya ādeḥ asāmānya prasaṅgataḥ śābaleya ādi rūpam hi na sāmānyam parasparam 
SV_5,14.4cd–5,14.7cd	 na vā ekam itareṣām vaḥ tatra ananta artha tā bhavet na ca sākṣāt viśeṣasya te apohyāḥ iti yuktimat na śābaleya vijñānam ago vyāvṛtti bandhanam nivṛttyā bāhuleya ādeḥ tat vijñānam pravartate kuryāt agonivṛttim ced na apoheta ātma vat dhi tān tena aṃśena anapohaḥ ca svarūpeṇa api apohanam kalpyate ced virodhaḥ syāt samam ākṣepa vāraṇe 
SV_5,14.8ab–5,14.10cd	 tasmāt prātyātmikaiḥ rūpaiḥ agaḥ apohaḥ na yujyate samudāye api na eteṣām ago vyāvṛtti sambhavaḥ sarva upalabdhau tad buddhiḥ vyāsa jya evam pravartate na pratyekam bhavet eṣā na samasteṣu aśaktitaḥ tasmāt sarveṣu yat rūpam pratyekam pariniṣṭhitam go buddhiḥ tad nimittā syāt go tvāt anyat ca na asti tat 
SV_5,14.11ab–5,14.14ab	 nanu ca prāc abhāva ādau sāmānyam vastu na iṣyate sattā eva hi atra sāmānyam anutpatti ādi rūṣitā tām utpatti ādi anusyūtām sat tā iti pratijānate anya apoha anuviddhā tu sā eva abhāvaḥ pratīyate anitya tvam vināśa ākhya kriyā sāmānyam ucyate abrāhmaṇa tvam kin tu syāt bhinneṣu kṣattriya ādiṣu puruṣa tvam catur saṃstham viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ 
SV_5,14.14cd–5,14.17cd	 sāmānya pratyayaḥ ca eṣu pratyekam upajāyate tena atra brāhmaṇa abhāvaḥ sāmānyam syāt avastu tat go tva ādau api tena eva sāmānya pratyayaḥ bhavet kaiḥ cit tu atra eka śabda tvam akṣa ādau iva kalpitam jāti trayasya na evam tu sambhavati aghaṭa ādiṣu na atra hi anantake bhede sādhāraṇyam nirūpyate tasmāt kriyā guṇāḥ ke cit dhetavaḥ ananya vartinaḥ 
SV_5,14.18ab–5,14.21ab	 puruṣa tvam nañā ca etat brāhmaṇebhyaḥ nivartitam cāturvarṇya prasaktam sat gamyate artha ādibhiḥ yathā yadi api avāntarā na asti triṣu jātiḥ vyavasthitāḥ nañsāmārthyāt nara tvam tu tri ādhāram sampratīyate śabda sāmarthya bhedena varṇeṣu mati bhinna tā puṃstve tri catur ādhāre paryudāsa svarūpataḥ dūra antike kṣaṇe śaktiḥ gṛdhra vāyasa cakṣuṣoḥ 
SV_5,14.21cd–5,14.24cd	 yathā rūpe tathā puṃstve puma bra āhmaṇa śabdayoḥ brāhmaṇa vyatirikta artha vṛtti puṃstvam iti īdṛśam vākyam yatra pravarteta tatra abrāhmaṇa dhī pade pārthiva tva ādi sāmānyam evam eva aghaṭa ādiṣu ghaṭa tva ādi vinirmuktam viṣayaḥ sampratīyate asādhāraṇa bhāvāt ca nañā śabdaḥ viśeṣitaḥ tāvat mātreṇa rahite sāmānye vyavatiṣṭhate 
SV_5,14.25ab–5,14.28ab	 viśeṣe pratiṣiddhe hi sāmānyam yat anantaram sāmānya ākāṅkṣiṇam śabdam niruṇad dhi tad ātmani prathama atikrame tasya kāraṇam na eva vidyate brāhmaṇa tvāt atas apetam nara tvam avaśiṣyate vyudasya brāhmaṇa tvam ca nañi jāte viśeṣaṇe nara tva udasanam yat tu kalpeta aśrutam eva tat tasmāt yasya eva te bhedāḥ niṣiddhyeran tad arthataḥ 
SV_5,14.28cd–5,14.31cd	 bheda antara stham sāmānyam loke api evam pratīyate prasaṅginyām ca tad buddhau niṣedhaḥ arthāt api iṣyate tanmātra rahite ca arthe sādṛśyāt tad matiḥ bhavet sādṛśyam eva vā vācyam iṣṭam abrāhmaṇa ādiṣu tat ca avayava sāmānyāt vinā api etena lakṣyate kva cit vinā api sādṛśyāt sāhacarya ādi hetukāḥ nañyukta śabda vṛttiḥ syāt yathā vakṣyati anīkṣaṇe 
SV_5,14.32ab–5,14.35ab	 īkṣaṇa vyatiriktā hi kriyā tatra api apekṣitāḥ pratyāsatteḥ na saṅkalpam atikramya pratīyate nāma dhātu artha yogī ca na eva nan pratiṣedhakaḥ vadataḥ abrāhmaṇa adharmau anya mātra virodhinau yatra api ākhyāta sambandhāt pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate tatra audāsīnyavastu eva pratipattā avalambate tasmāt vastuni apohāḥ syuḥ api ca avastu kalpane 
SV_5,14.35cd–5,14.38cd	 prāgntyebhyaḥ viśeṣebhyaḥ na kiñ cit vastu labhyate na ca antyaiḥ vyavahāraḥ asti śakyam na eṣām nirūpaṇam apoha śabda vācyā atha śūnyatā anya prakārikā tasyām ca aśva ādi buddhīna ātma aṃśa grahaṇam bhavet tatra anya apoha vācya tvam mudhā eva abhyupagamyate sāmānyam vastu rūpam hi buddhi ākāraḥ bhaviṣyati śabda arthaḥ artha anapekṣaḥ hi vṛthā apohaḥ prakalpitaḥ 
SV_5,14.39ab–5,14.42ab	 vastu rūpā ca sā buddhiḥ śabda artheṣu upajāyate tena vastu eva kalpeta vācyam buddhi anapohakam asati api ca bāhye arthe vākya artha pratibhā tathā padārthe api tathā eva syāt kim apohaḥ prakalpyate buddhi antarāt vyavacchedaḥ na ca buddheḥ pratīyate svarūpa utpāda mātrāt ca na anyam aṃśam bibharti sā bhinna sāmānya vacanāḥ viśeṣa vacanāḥ ca ye 
SV_5,14.42cd–5,14.45cd	 sarve bhaveyuḥ paryāyāḥ yadi apohasya vācya tā nanu bhedāt apohānām prasaṅgaḥ ayam na yujyate sāmānya apoha kptyā ced vastu mātre samam tava bhidyante mama vastu tvāt sāmānyāni parasparam asaṅkīrṇa svabhāvāni na ca eka tvam vitanvate saṃsṛṣṭa eka tva nānātva vikalpa rahita ātmanām avastu tvāt apohānām tva syāt bhinna tā katham 
SV_5,14.46ab–5,14.49ab	 yadi vā bhidyamāna tvāt vastu asādhāraṇa aṃśa vat avastu tve tu anānātvāt paryāya tvāt na mucyate nanu ca apohya bhedena bhedaḥ apohasya setsyati na viśeṣaḥ svatas tasya paratas ca aupacārikaḥ tena eva ādhāra bhedena api asya bhedaḥ na yujyate na hi sambandhi bhedena bhedaḥ vastuni api iṣyate kim utāvastu asaṃsṛṣṭam anyatas ca anivartitam 
SV_5,14.49cd–5,14.52cd	 anavāpta viśeṣa aṃśam yat kim api anirūpitam tasmāt yathā eva bhede api piṇḍānām na eva bhidyate tathā eva apohya bhede api na anekaḥ ayam bhaviṣyati bhede vā pratipiṇḍam syāt agaḥ apohaḥ tathā sati sāmānyam śābaleya ādeḥ iti na iṣṭam prasidhyati saṃsargiṇaḥ api ca ādhārāḥ yam na bhindanti rūpataḥ apohyaiḥ sa bahis bhūtaiḥ bhidyeta iti ati kalpanā 
SV_5,14.53ab–5,14.56ab	 aga vya śvātiḥ ekaḥ syāt anaśvaḥ ca gavādhikaḥ śeṣam hasti ādi apohyam tu dvayoḥ api na bhidyate tatra eka bhedāt bhedaḥ astu bahu abhedāt abhinnatā bhūyasām syāt sadharma tvam iti abhedaḥ prasajyate gauḥ ca hasti ādi apohena na aśva rūpāt viśeṣyate karoti tat apoham ced aikarūpyam virudhyate sarva śabdeṣu ca ekaikam apohyam atiricyate 
SV_5,14.56cd–5,14.59cd	 tatra asādhāraṇa tvena tanmātra apohyatā bhavet tatas aśva apoha rūpa tvāt siṃha ādiḥ sarve eva te tad nimittam agaḥ apoham bibhrat ucyeta gauḥ iti sarva apohaḥ yadīṣyeta sa vaktavyaḥ katham punar yadi pratyeka rūpeṇa na apohya ananta tā bhavet bhinna tvāt ca api apohyānām bhinnaḥ apohaḥ prasajyate tatra ekasmin bhavet piṇḍe ananta jāti samanvayaḥ 
SV_5,14.60ab–5,14.63ab	 tatas gauḥ iti sāmānyam vācyam ekam na sidhyati jāti antara matiḥ ca eṣu bhavet jāti antareṣu iva samudāya ātmanā na api bhavet eṣām apohyatā samudāyaḥ hi na ekena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate na api eka deśa tā teṣām asti na api eka kāla tā vyatiriktaḥ ca saṅghātaḥ teṣām kaḥ cit na vidyate yadi tu avyatiriktaḥ syāt ānanyam tat avasthitam 
SV_5,14.63cd–5,14.66cd	 yadi sāmānya rūpeṇa te apohyante na vastu tāḥ katham vā vastu apohyeta na abhāvaḥ bhāvam ṛcchati apohyamāne ca abhāve bhāvaḥ eva avaśiṣyate apohya bheda kptiḥ ca na abhāva abhedataḥ bhavet tad bhedaḥ apoha bhedāt ced prāptam anyonya saṃśrayam go sāmāni asya bhinna tvāt agauḥ iti eṣa bhidyate agauḥ iti asya bhedena go sāmānyam ca bhidyate 
SV_5,14.67ab–5,14.70ab	 agāvaḥ aśva ādayaḥ ca syuḥ te api abhāva ātmakāḥ punar karkā ādi apekṣayā te api tathā iti evam na gamyate kim apohyam kva ca apohaḥ gopiṇḍeṣu evam eva ca tatra syāt dvayam api etat antyeṣu paramāṇuṣu na ca antyeṣu dvayoḥ asti vyavahāraḥ bhidām prati gavā aśva paramāṇūnām viśeṣaḥ ca na vidyate sva rūpa jāti saṃsthāna parimāṇa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ 
SV_5,14.70cd–5,14.73cd	 kim apohyam kva ca apohaḥ tatra api na viśiṣyate na ca aprasiddha sārūpya anapoha viṣaya ātmanā śaktaḥ kaḥ cit api jñātum gavā ādīn a viśeṣataḥ apohyān api ca aśva ādīn eka dharma anvayāt ṛte na nirūpayitum śaktiḥ tatra apohaḥ na siddhyati na ca anvaya vinirmukte pravṛttiḥ liṅga śabdayoḥ tābhyām ca na vinā apohaḥ na ca asādhāraṇe anvayaḥ 
SV_5,14.74ab–5,14.77ab	 apohaḥ ca api aniṣpannaḥ sāhacaryam kva dṛśyatām tasmin adṛśyamāne ca na tayoḥ syāt pramāṇatā na ca adarśana mātreṇa tābhyām pratyāyanam bhavet sarvatra eva hi adṛṣṭa tvāt pratyāyyam na avaśiṣyate atha asati api sārūpye syāt apohasya kalpanā gavāśvayoḥ ayam kasmāt agaḥ apohaḥ na kalpyate śābaleyāt ca bhinna tvam bāhuleya aśvayoḥ samam 
SV_5,14.77cd–5,14.80cd	 sāmānyam na anyat iṣṭam ced kvāgaḥ apohaḥ pravartatām indriyaiḥ na api agaḥ apohaḥ prathamam vyavasīyate na anyatra śabda vṛttiḥ ca kim dṛṣṭvā sa prayujyatām pūrva uktena prabandhena na anumā api atra vidyate sambandha anubhāvaḥ api asya tena na eva upapadyate nivṛtti vācinaḥ śabdāḥ na prasiddhāḥ ca yān prati teṣām agoḥ asiddha tvāt na sāmānya nirākriyā 
SV_5,14.81ab–5,14.84ab	 ago śabda abhidheya tvam gamyatām ca katham punar na dṛṣṭaḥ yatra go śabdaḥ sambandha anubha vakṣaṇe ekasmāt tarhi gopiṇḍāt yat anyat sarvam eva tat bhavet apohyam iti evam na sāmānyasya vācya tā siddhaḥ ca āgauḥ apohyeta go niṣedha ātmakaḥ ca saḥ tatra gauḥ eva vaktavyaḥ nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate sa ced agonivṛtti ātmā bhavet anyonya saṃśrayaḥ 
SV_5,14.84cd–5,14.87cd	 siddhaḥ ced gauḥ apohya artham vṛthā apoha prakalpanā gavya siddhe tu agauḥ na asti tad abhāve ca gauḥ kutas na ādhāra ādheya vṛtti ādi sambandhaḥ ca api abhāvayoḥ na ca asādhāraṇam vastu gamyate apoha vat tayā katham vā parikalpyeta sambandhaḥ vastu avastunoḥ sva rūpa sattva mātreṇa na ca kiñ cit viśeṣaṇam sva buddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyam tat viśeṣaṇam 
SV_5,14.88ab–5,14.91ab	 na ca api aśva ādi śabda ibhaḥ jāyate apoha bodhanam viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ iṣṭā iha na ca ajñāta viśeṣaṇā na ca anya rūpam anyādṛś kuryāt jñānam viśeṣaṇam katham ca anyādṛśe jñāte tat ucyeta viśeṣaṇam atha anyathā viśeṣye api syāt viśeṣaṇa kalpanā tathā sati hi yat kiñcid prasajyeta viśeṣaṇam abhāva rūpa gamye ca na viśeṣye asti vastu tāḥ 
SV_5,14.91cd–5,14.94cd	 viśeṣitam apohena vastu vācyam na te asti atas yadi api apoha nirmukte na vṛttiḥ śabda liṅgayoḥ yuktā tathā api buddhiḥ tu jñātuḥ vastu avalambate na ca asādhāraṇam vastu buddhau viparivarttate na ca api nirvikalpa tvāt tasya yuktā viśeṣyatā śabdena āgamyamānam ca viśeṣyam iti sāhasam tena sāmānyam eṣṭavyam viṣayaḥ buddhi śabdayoḥ 
SV_5,14.95ab–5,14.98ab	 yadā ca aśabda vācya tvāt na vyaktīnām apohyatā tadā apohyeta sāmānym tasya apohāt ca vastu tāḥ na apohya tvam abhāvānām abhāva abhāva varjanāt vyaktaḥ apoha antare apohaḥ tasmāt sāmānya vastunaḥ abhāvasya ca yaḥ abhāvaḥ sa ced tasmāt vilakṣaṇaḥ bhāvaḥ eva bhavet no ced gauḥ agauḥ te prasajyate yadi api aneṣu śabdeṣu vastunaḥ syāt apohyatā 
SV_5,14.98cd–5,14.101cd	 sat śabdasya tu abhāva ākhyān na apohyam bhinnam iṣyate tatra asataḥ api bhāva tvam iti kleśaḥ mahān bhavet tad asiddhau na sattā asti na ca asattā prasidhyati na ca api vāsanā bhedāt bhedaḥ sat rūpa tā api vā apohānām prakalpyeta na hi avastuni vāsanā smṛtim muktvā na ca asti asyāḥ śakti yogaḥ kriyā antare tasmāt na anyādṛśe sārthe karoti anyādṛśīm matim 
SV_5,14.102ab–5,14.105ab	 bhavadbhiḥ śabda bhedaḥ api tad nimittaḥ na labhyate na hi asādhāraṇaḥ śabdaḥ vācakaḥ prāk adṛṣṭitaḥ bhinna tvāt ca api na eva ekā vāsanā taiḥ prakalpyate na ca asti śabdavastu ekam vāsanām yat kariṣyati tatra śabda antara apohe sāmānye parikalpite tathā eva avastu rūpa tvāt śabda bhedaḥ na kalpyate vācakānām yathā ca evam vācya vācakayoḥ mithas 
SV_5,14.105cd–5,14.108cd	 na ca api apohya bhedena bhedaḥ asti iti upapāditam na agṛhītaḥ ca gamakaḥ śabda apohaḥ kathan canaḥ pratyakṣam na ca tat śaktam na ca staḥ liṅga vācakau yatas syāt grahaṇam tasya liṅga ādīnām ca kalpane na vyavasthā iti vācya evam vinā pratyakṣa mūlataḥ na gamya gamaka tvam syāt avastu tvāt apohayoḥ bhavat pakṣe yathā loke kha puṣpa śaśa śṛṅgayoḥ 
SV_5,14.109ab–5,14.112ab	 vṛṣṭi megha asatoḥ dṛṣṭvā yadi anaikāntikaḥ vadet vastu eva atra api mad pakṣe bhavat pakṣe api adaḥ kutas vidhi rūpaḥ ca śabda arthaḥ yena na abhyupagamyate na bhavet vyatirekaḥ api tasya tad pūrvakaḥ hi asau niṣedha dvaya yogi tvāt asataḥ yā api abhāvatā sa vastuke bhavet sā api na tucche buddhi asambhavāt nanu yukti ā ānayā eva ayam vastunā api na bhidyate 
SV_5,14.112cd–5,14.115cd	 apohaḥ tena doṣaḥ atra pūrva uktaḥ na bhaviṣyati siddham evam madiṣṭam syāt na eva anyā gatiḥ asti hi abhāve vastu buddhiḥ vā yat vā vastuni abhāva dhīḥ tatra abhāva ātmaka tve syāt nirnimitta eva vastu dhīḥ vastuni abhāva bodhaḥ tu sidhyati anyam apekṣya tu apoha mātra vācya tvam yadi ca abhyupagamyate nīlotpala ādi śabdeṣu śabala artha abhidhāyiṣu 
SV_5,14.116ab–5,14.119ab	 viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tva sāmāna adhikaraṇyayoḥ na siddhiḥ na hi anīlatva vyudāse anutpala cyutiḥ na api tatra itaraḥ tasmāt na viśeṣya viśeṣaṇe śabdayoḥ na api te syātām abhidheya anapekṣayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca na bhinna tvāt apohayoḥ arthataḥ ca etat iṣyeta kīdṛśi a ādheya tā tayoḥ na ca asādhāraṇam vastu gamyate anyat ca na asti te 
SV_5,14.119cd–5,14.122cd	 agamyamānam aikārthyam śabdayoḥ kva upayujyate atha anya apoha vat vastu vācyam iti abhidhīyate tatra api paratantra tvāt vyāptiḥ śabdena durbalāḥ khaṇḍe bhinna vyapohya tvāt yathā eva madhura ādibhiḥ śukla ādi vyāpti abhāvena na ākṣepaḥ na viśeṣaṇam tathā eva asat vyudāsa aṃśa avacchinnā artha avadhāraṇe na aghaṭa ādi nivṛtti aṃśa vyāptiḥ śabdāt pratīyate 
SV_5,14.123ab–5,14.125cd	 vyāptiḥ ced artha rūpeṇa sat tayā evam hi sā bhavet na ghaṭa tva ādimān arthaḥ kaḥ cit na vyāpyate tayā na ca vastu tayā vyāptiḥ tayā śabdasya vāryate pratītim prati tulyaḥ tu vyāpāraḥ vastu avastunoḥ nirbhāgaḥ api hi vastu ātmā śabdaiḥ bhāgena gamyate na hi sat śabda vijñānāt ghaṭa ādi arthaḥ pratīyate 
SV_5,14.126ab–5,14.129ab	 tena anākṣepa doṣaḥ asti bhākta doṣaḥ ca vidyate viśeṣaṇa tvāt mukhya tvam apohasya hi jāti vat tasmāt tadvati gauṇa tvāt na abhidheya tva sambhavaḥ avastu tvāt na mukhyaḥ ced na syāt evam viśeṣaṇam bhedāḥ ca apohavantaḥ syuḥ teṣām ca avācya ta uditā ānantya vyabhicārābhyām anyaḥ na asti tu apohavān na apohavat tvam anyat dhi bheda apoha antare asti te 
SV_5,14.129cd–5,14.132cd	 tat ca api kalpyamānam syāt abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ eva vā vastu ced jātiḥ eva syāt avastu tve api pūrvavat sambandhaḥ vā eṣa kalpyeta tasya ceṣṭā na vācya tā na ca ekaḥ apohavān arthaḥ vartate artha antare kva cit tasmāt api na sāmānyam vācyam na ca viśeṣaṇam na ātmani avidyamāna tvāt viśeṣaḥ apoha sūcakaḥ tasmāt na taiḥ viśeṣya tvam prakṛṣṭa tvena nīla vat 
SV_5,14.133ab–5,14.136ab	 artha ākṣepaḥ api na asti eva sandehāt liṅga liṅgi vat na sāmānya ātmanā apohaḥ taiḥ vinā na ca siddhyati evam eva tu anākṣepaḥ syāt apohena vastunaḥ yatas śaśa viṣāṇe api tad apohasya sambhavaḥ liṅga saṃkhyā ādi sambandhaḥ na vā apohasya vidyate vyakteḥ avyapadeśya tvāt tad dvāreṇa api na asti asau na hi asādhāraṇa tvena sa apohena api gamyate 
SV_5,14.136cd–5,14.139cd	 na ca api agamyamānasya vastunaḥ syāt viśeṣyatā liṅga saṃkhyā ādi apohānām na upakāraḥ svarūpataḥ vastunaḥ ca upakārya tvam katham śabdaiḥ pratīyate na vinā anupalabdhyā ca syāt abhāva matiḥ kva cit na ca abhāva prameya tvam go tva ādeḥ iha gamyate ākhyāteṣu ca na anyasya nivṛttiḥ sampratīyate na paryudāsa rūpam hi niṣedhyam tatra vidyate 
SV_5,14.140ab–5,14.143ab	 na na iti hi ucyamāne api niṣedhasya niṣedhanam pacati iti aniṣiddham tu svarūpeṇa avatiṣṭhate sādhya tva pratyayaḥ ca atra tathābhūta ādi rūpaṇam niṣpanna tvāt apohasya nirnimittam prasajyate vidhi ādau artha rāśau ca na anya apoha nidarśanam nañaḥ ca api nañā yuktāt apohaḥ kīdṛśaḥ bhavet ca ādīnām api nañyogaḥ na eva asti iti anapohanam 
SV_5,14.143cd–5,14.146cd	 vākya arthaḥ anya nivṛttiḥ ca vyapadeṣṭum na śakyate ananya apoha śabda ādau vācyam na ca nirūpyate prameya jñeya śabda ādeḥ apohyam kutas eva tu apohya kalpanāyām tu varam vastu eva kalpitam jñāna ākāra niṣedhāt ca na antara artha abhidheya tā na ca api apohyatā tasmāt na apohaḥ teṣu sidhyati evam ityādi śabdānām na vā apohyam nirūpyate 
SV_5,14.147ab–5,14.150ab	 virodhi tvena bhedānām apohaḥ yadi kalpyate virodhaḥ apohataḥ tatra virodhāt ca api apohanam na sāmānya apahāri tvam vidhi rūpeṇa tatra te palaśa ādīn apohyātas vṛkṣam harati śiṃśapā sāmānya ādi anapohaḥ ca na avirodhena kalpyate na hi śabda svarūpāṇām syāt viruddha aviruddhatā na ca vastu svarūpeṇa tasya śabdaiḥ asaṅgateḥ 
SV_5,14.150cd–5,14.153cd	 prāk śabda vyāpṛteḥ na api sa apohānām pratīyate anyena anavabuddhe arthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate sāmānya ātmaka tā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate śabda anurūpataḥ ced syāt anya apoha nirūpaṇam bhinna tvāt vṛkṣatarva ādeḥ apohaḥ kena vāryate śabda spṛṣṭeḥ vinā apohaḥ na ca liṅgena gamyate na viruddha aviruddha tvam tasya liṅgāt ca sidhyati 
SV_5,14.154ab–5,14.157ab	 adṛṣṭa tvāt vyudāsaḥ tu purastāt eva vāritaḥ sāmānya śabdaḥ bhedena na iṣyate vācaka ātmanā vyudāsaḥ tatra durvāraḥ kathan cit dṛṣṭa tā punar brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasya api paryudāsaḥ prasajyate ākāṅkṣaṇāt atha atyāgaḥ tulyaḥ dravya kriyā ādiṣu vṛkṣeṇa atas anapohaḥ syāt tiṣṭhati ādeḥ asaṃśayam puruṣasya tathā rājñaḥ vyudāse na viśeṣyatā 
SV_5,14.157cd–5,14.160cd	 avyudāsa tva pakṣe ca syāt nīlotpala tulya tā vṛkṣa tva pārthiva dravya sat jñeyeṣu yat ucyate prātilomya ānulomyena vidhau sarva artha bodhanam tat ayuktam na sarvaḥ hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate deśa avibhāgataḥ vṛttiḥ netrasya api rasa ādiṣu grāhaka tvena vṛttiḥ tu pratijāti vyavasthitāḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vat eva atra saṅkaraḥ na bhaviṣyati 
SV_5,14.161ab–5,14.164ab	 nivṛtta ceṣṭe śabde ca vyāpti avyāpti kṛtam punar sattva ādeḥ bodhaka tvam syāt eka nyūna atirekataḥ tava eva doṣaḥ syāt eṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate sāmānya śabdaḥ vācyānām bhedaḥ na api asti vastutas api ca eka tva nitya tva pratyeka samavāyitāḥ nirupākhyeṣu apoheṣu kurvataḥ asūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ tasmāt yeṣu eva śabdeṣu nañyogaḥ teṣu kevalam 
SV_5,14.164cd–5,14.167cd	 bhavet anya nivṛtti aṃśaḥ sva ātmā eva anyatra gamyate jñeya arthānyān apoha tvam pramāṅga tvāt tvac ādi vat yena uktam tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syāt vyabhicāritā pakṣīkuryāt yadā sarvān tadā atha avīta hetubhiḥ anaikāntaḥ virodhaḥ ca sarva loka prasiddhitaḥ na apohataḥ iti idam ca kāraka tvena ced bhavet kevala apoha buddheḥ vā tatas syāt siddha sādhya tā 
SV_5,14.168ab–5,14.171ab	 atha anya apohavati arthe vṛttiḥ na asti iti sādhyate tatas prāk pakṣa bādhaḥ syāt go tve atha aśva ādi abhāvataḥ sādhya hīnaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi api tasya hi varttate apohavati eva tam yadi api na budhyate atha anya apoha nirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddha sādhanam apoha rūpam api etat vastu iti eva hi gamyate atha apoha nimitta asya vṛttiḥ arthe niṣidhyate 
SV_5,14.171cd–5,14.176cd	 vyatireka aṅgateṣṭa tvāt punar prāk pakṣa bādhanam anumāne tathā ca etat iti anaikāntikaḥ bhavet sandeha bādha jātena pratyakṣeṇa api cetasā viruddha tā ca hetoḥ syāt śabdaḥ śrotra ādi vat yatas ātma antaḥ karaṇa ākāśaiḥ sva vāci tvam jahāti vāḥ vidhi rūpa pravṛtiiḥ vā śabdaḥ apohena varttate anumāna aṅga bhūta tvāt yathā eva pratiṣedhakaḥ jātim vā na bravīti eṣa vyaktim vā tad viśeṣitām pramāyām aṅga bhūta tvāt tvac śrotra ādi yathā eva ca evam sādhana mārgeṇa vācya avācya nirūpaṇāḥ na avātiṣṭhate iti atra kathyate loka vartmanā 
SV_5,15.1ab–5,15.4ab	 sāsnādibhiḥ viśiṣṭa tvam ākṛteḥ ucyate katham yadā avayavi sambandhi go tvam na avayave sthitam eka avayavi sambandhaḥ teṣām go tvena vidyate tena asādhāraṇa tvāt te syuḥ go tvasya upalakṣaṇam piṇḍe sattā ādi jātīnām bahvīnām samaveta tā tābhyaḥ viśiṣyate go tvam sāsnādibhiḥ asaṃśayam na ca ete vyañjakāḥ tasya guṇavat vā viśeṣaṇam 
SV_5,15.4cd–5,15.7cd	 tathā hi na agṛhīteṣu teṣu syāt go tva bodhanam teṣām ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punar grahaṇa kalpanā tathā sati anavasthā syāt na syāt go tva avadhāraṇam sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavet matiḥ go tve na ca eṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhi sambhavaḥ tasmāt sadbhāva mātreṇa mahat tva ādau yathā eva dhīḥ kriyate avayavaiḥ piṇde tathā jāti guṇa ādiṣu 
SV_5,15.8ab–5,15.11ab	 yadi evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kim sā na jāyate tad deśa vyatirekeṇa grāhyam yena na vidyate gṛhyamāṇe tu go tva ādau na antarīyaka hetukaḥ sāsnādeḥ kasya cit bodhaḥ tad deśa tvena jāyate tad anatyanta bhedāt vā tad viśiṣṭa iti kīrtyate bādhaḥ para anumānasya na pratyakṣā iti bodhyate pareṣām sādhanam hi atra na ākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak 
SV_5,15.11cd–5,15.14cd	 tat hīhānau avijñānāt paṅkti yūtha vana ādi vat sarvatra loka siddha tvāt na vācyam sādhanam svayam niṣedha tām pareṣām tu virodham lokataḥ vadet visaṃvādaḥ na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatā ākṛteḥ pramāṇe api visaṃvādāt tārkikeṣu kutas nu iyam rūpa ādau api teṣām hi pratyakṣa tvena sammate vivādaḥ na eva lokaḥ tu jātau vipratipadyate 
SV_5,15.15ab–5,15.18ab	 vyavahārāḥ hi dṛśyante sāmānya artha nibandhanāḥ dadhi takra ādi dāna ādau kauṇḍinya brāhmaṇa ādiṣu ākṛtiḥ jātiḥ eva atra saṃsthānam na prakalpyate na hi vāyu agni śabda ādau kiñ cit saṃsthānam iṣyate anyat anyat ca saṃsthānam pratipiṇḍam pratīyate saṃyoga ātmaka tāyām tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati atha saṃsthāna sāmānyam aśva ādau api tad samam 
SV_5,15.18cd–5,15.21cd	 na go tvena vinā hi etat vyavacchinnam pratīyate sarva pratikṛtīnām ca saṃsthāne sati api īdṛśe na go tva ādi matiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tasmāt jātiḥ pṛthak tatas rucaka ādiṣu sāmānyam rucaka tvāt yudāhṛtam bhinneṣu ca eṣu sāmānyam suvarṇa tvam pratīyate vardhamānaka bhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā tadā pūrva arthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiḥ ca api uttara arthinaḥ 
SV_5,15.22ab–5,15.25ab	 hema arthinaḥ tu mādhyastham tasmāt vastu traya ātmakam na utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām abhāve syāt mati trayam na nāśena vinā śokaḥ na utpādena vinā sukham sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam tena sāmānya nitya tā mudga māṣa tila ādau ca yatra bhedaḥ na lakṣyate tatra ekabuddhi nirgrāhyā jātiḥ indriya gocaraḥ ārāt dṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandehaḥ brāhmaṇa ādiṣu 
SV_5,15.25cd–5,15.28cd	 na syāt yadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyam cakṣuḥ ādinā tasya upalakṣaṇam ca api kva cit kena cit iṣyate rūpa ādīnām viśeṣeṇa deśa kāla ādi apekṣayā suvarṇam bhidyate rūpāt tāmra tva ādeḥ asaṃśayam tailāt ghṛtam vilīnam ca gandhena ca rasena ca bhasma pracchāditaḥ vahniḥ sparśanena upalabhyate aśva tva ādau ca dūra sthe niścayaḥ jāyate svanaiḥ 
SV_5,15.29ab–5,15.32ab	 saṃsthānena ghaṭa tva ādi brāhmaṇa tva ādi yonitaḥ kva cit ācārataḥ ca api samyak rāja anupālitāt pratyeka samaveta tvam dṛṣṭa tvāt na virotsyate tathā sati api nānātvam na eka buddheḥ bhaviṣyati na hi sambandhi bhedena svarūpa eka tva bādhanam vibhu tva avayava abhāvau pratipādyau ca śabda vat yathā ca vyatirekā eva dṛśyamānā punar punar 
SV_5,15.32cd–5,15.35cd	 kāla bhede api abhinnā eva jātiḥ bhinna āśrayā satī kārtsya avayavaśas vṛttiḥ praṣṭum jātau na yujyate na hi bheda vinirmukte kārtsnya bhāga vikalpanam tasmāt vyaktiṣu jātīnām vṛttiḥ asti iti gamyate viśeṣa avasara abhāvāt tanmātrā eva avatiṣṭhate yā ca avayavaśas vṛttiḥ sraj sūtra ādiṣu dṛśyate bhūta kaṇṭha guṇa ādeḥ ca pratipiṇḍam samāptitaḥ 
SV_5,15.36ab–5,15.39ab	 tatra avayava yogi tvam avibhu tvaṃca kāraṇam ākṛteḥ tad abhāvena na prasakta madaḥ dvayam na ca dvaividhyam eva iti vṛtteḥ asti niyāmakam trividhā api hi dṛṣṭa tvāt sambhavet dvividhāḥ yathā itaratra na dṛṣṭam ced sraj ādiṣu api tad samam na eva hi anyonya tulya tvam tayoḥ na api anayā saha na hi anyasmin adṛṣṭa tvāt vahneḥ auṣṇyam praṇaśyati 
SV_5,15.39cd–5,15.42cd	 na ca anumāna gamyā iyam vāñchet yena nidarśanam sva rūpataḥ ca dṛṣṭāyāḥ vṛtteḥ na para rūpataḥ nirākriyā upapadyeta tad viśeṣam apaśyatām aṅga aṅga asambhavāt ca api yā pradhāna nirākriyā sā ayuktā eva anumānena pratyakṣa jñāna bādhanāt tasmāt asambhavaḥ yasya tanmātrasya eva bādhanam yuktam na tāvatā anyaḥ api sambhavan bādham arhati 
SV_5,15.43ab–5,15.46ab	 tena vaiśeṣika uktā api jātiḥ sarva gatā satī vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇa vat tatra gṛhyate tasmāt piṇḍeṣu go buddhiḥ ekago tva nibandhanā gavā ābhāsa eka rūpya ābhām eka gopiṇḍa buddhi vat na śābaleyāt go buddhiḥ tatas anya ālambanā api vā tad abhāve api sadbhāvāt ghaṭe pārthiva buddhi vat pratyeka samaveta artha viṣayā vā api gomatiḥ 
SV_5,15.46cd–5,15.49cd	 pratyekam kṛtsna buddhi tvāt pratyeka vyakti buddhi vat pratyeka samavetā api jātiḥ eka eka buddhitaḥ nañyukteṣu api vākyeṣu brahmaṇā ādi nivartanam na ca sādṛśya viṣayāḥ godhīḥ tādrūpya janmataḥ prāmāṇye sati yadvat dhi pratyabhijñā eka vastuni na eka rūpa matiḥ go tve mithyā vaktum ca śakyate na atra kāraṇa doṣaḥ asti bādhaka pratyayaḥ api vā 
SV_5,15.50ab–5,15.53ab	 yadā vyakti atirekeṇa grāhya tvāt anyatā ākṛteḥ vanavat na asti anaikāntāt tatra asambaddhatā katham sādhanam ced mayā ucyeta yujyeta vyabhicāritā dūṣaṇa tva dhiyā tu etat asambaddha tvam ucyate na astitva hetoḥ uktā eṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddha tā parasya sādhanam hi atra yat tat pūrvam udāhṛtam pratyakṣa ābhāsa tā ca atra na eva asti vana buddhi vat 
SV_5,15.53cd–5,15.56cd	 kasya cit na hi mithyātvāt sarvam mithyā iti asaṅgatiḥ yathā vana ādi buddhīnām mithyātvāt na rasa ādi dhīḥ mithyā evam jāti buddhiḥ syāt viśeṣaḥ vā abhidhīyatām vṛkṣebhyaḥ vyatirekeṇa vane yā eka matiḥ bhavet dūra tva doṣāt tatra syāt ākṛtau tu na vidyate sannikṛṣṭasya vṛkṣeṣu buddhi eka tvam nivartate kena cit tu prakāreṇa jāti buddhiḥ na naśyati 
SV_5,15.57ab–5,15.60ab	 yā eka tva dhīḥ vinā śabdāt sā evam tāvat nirākṛtāḥ vana śabda anuraktā tu madhyasthasya api jāyate mithyātva kalpanā tu asyāḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ asambhavāt jātiḥ sarva pramāṇaiḥ tu tad rūpā eva avagamyate pramāṇa antara dṛṣte ca padam arthe prayujyate tasmāt dṛṣṭe prayuktasya mithyātvam syāt vana ādiṣu ke cit nityam vana eka tvam śabda gamyam samāśritāḥ 
SV_5,15.60cd–5,15.63cd	 anyaiḥ saṅgati abhāve api satyam tat syāt rasa ādi vat mithyātvam yat asaṅgatyā tad ajñāne prasajyate jñāyamānasya doṣaḥ tu na tu kaḥ cit asaṅgateḥ pramāṇa antara gamye arthe padam nityam prayujyate dharmaḥ ayam na ca sarveṣām padānām abhyupeyate asti eva saṅgatiḥ ca atra vṛkṣāḥ hi bahavaḥ vanam te pramāṇa antāt jñātāḥ saṃshyā ca eṣā anya vastuni 
SV_5,15.64ab–5,15.67ab	 na anekasya eka śabdyam ced eka śeṣavat iṣyatām tatra saṃkhyā vivṛddhiḥ ced astu tanmātra varjanam tasmāt sāmānya dṛṣṭena siddha eka tvasya saṅgatiḥ tena anyān avagamyā api saṃkhyā syāt sūrya yāna vat ke cit bahu tva sāmānyam āhuḥ vṛkṣa sthitam vanam tatra ca eka tvam asti eva vana tvam vā api vidyate vinā api eka āśraya tvena yathā eva avayavaḥ tathā 
SV_5,15.67cd–5,15.70cd	 asaṃyuktaiḥ abhivyaktiḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt na virotsyate anyatra api ca tad buddheḥ sāmānyam tat abhaviṣyati yathā ca bhramaṇa tva ādi bhaṅgiṣu avayaveṣu api vyaktam nānā āśrayatve api gṛhyate vanatā tathā yat vā eka kārya hetu tvāt eka go śabda vat vanam nityam ye vyasta vijñātā vṛkṣāḥ na iṣṭā hi te vanam yat vā lakṣaṇayā eka tvam deśa kāla kriyā ādibhiḥ 
SV_5,15.71ab–5,15.74ab	 dravya eka tvāt vinā api iṣṭam paṅkti yūtha vana ādiṣu vṛkṣāṇām samudāye ca vana dhīḥ jāyate yathā na evam go samudāye api go tva dhīḥ upajāyate yādṛśī vṛkṣadhīḥ tatra go tva dhīḥ api tādṛśī vana vat na apṛthak siddheḥ samudāya tva kalpanā na ca sāsnādi saṅghātaḥ tad buddhi ālambanam bhavet kṣīṇeṣu piṇḍa buddhyaiṣu tad sāmānye hi go tvadhīḥ 
SV_5,15.74cd–5,15.77cd	 tena avayavi abhāve api sāmānyam vyatiricyate pūrva uktāt eva tu nyāyāt sidhyet atra avayavi api tasya api atyanta bhinna tvam na syāt avayavaiḥ saha vyaktibhyaḥ jāti vat ca eṣa na niṣkṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate kaiḥ cit avyatirikta tvam kaiḥ cit ca vyatirikta tā dūṣitā sādhitāḥ vā api na ca tatra balābalam kadā cit niścitam kaiḥ cit tasmāt madhyastha tā varam 
SV_5,15.78ab–5,15.81ab	 tatas anyānanyate nasya staḥ na staḥ ca iti kīrttyate tasmāt citra vat eva asya mṛṣā syāt eka rūpa tā vastu aneka tva vādāt ca na sandindhā pramāṇa tā jñānam sandihyate yatra tatra na syāt pramāṇatā iha anaikāntikam vastu iti evam jñānam su niścitam niṣkṛṣya avayavān buddhyā yā avaī avya pratīta tā buddhi stha tvāt vināśasya saulūkyasya api yujyate 
SV_5,15.81cd–5,15.84cd	 vṛttiḥ ca avayaveṣu asya vyāsa jyā eva pratīyate tatas kārtsnya ādi sampraśnaḥ pratyākhyeyaḥ atra jāti vat sāsnādi guṇa hetuḥ ced na anyasmin go tva dhīḥ bhavet bhinnaḥ eva hi sāsnādiḥ piṇḍāt piṇḍa antareyataḥ na ca avayava sāmānyam pareṣām upapadyate tasmāt sa āsnāditaḥ anyena go tva dhīḥ upajanyate vana antar eṣa yā buddhiḥ vanam iti upajāyate 
SV_5,15.85ab–5,15.88ab	 tasyāḥ tat eva vṛkṣa tvam grāhyam bahu āśrayam viduḥ eka tve api ākṛteḥ yadvat bahu tvam vyakti apekṣayā bahu tve hi tathā vyakteḥ ekatvam jāti apekṣayā eka aneka abhidhāne ca śabdāḥ niyata śaktayaḥ ke cit vyaktim tu asaṃkhyākām gamayanti ambara ādiṣu ekaḥ vrīhiḥ su niṣpannaḥ iti jātim sva saṃkhyayā patnī sannahana ādau tu vyaktim ākṛti saṃkhyayā 
SV_5,15.88cd–5,15.91cd	 kapiñjala ādi jāteḥ tu pratītiḥ vyakti saṃkhyayā vyakti jātī vadanti anye dravya avayava saṃkhyayā asmān iti yathā ekasmin pāśānaditiḥ iti api tatra vrīhi ādi śabdānām saṃkhyā yogaḥ yathāruci vana dāra ādi śabdāḥ tu pravartante vyavasthayā jaṅgame sthāvare ca arthe yathā yūtha vana ādayaḥ tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dāra ādiḥ ced prayujyate 
SV_5,15.92ab–5,15.95ab	 vyakteḥ avayavānām ca saṃkhyām ādāya vartate vana śabdaḥ punar vyaktīḥ jāti saṃkhyā viśeṣitāḥ bahvīrāha atha vā jātim bahu vyakti samāśrayām evam paṅkti ādi śabdānām saṃyoga ādi viśeṣaṇam sarveṣām kiñ cit asti iti na nirālambana eka dhīḥ tulyam pratyakṣayā aakṛtyāḥ vane yat tat asat yadi vṛkṣāḥ tatra tayā tulyāḥ iti śūnya tva vādi tā 
SV_5,15.95cd–5,15.97cd	 pratyakṣa ābhāsa gamya tvāt vṛkṣebhyaḥ anyat tu tat vanam nā aakṛtyā saha tasya asti sparddhā pratyakṣa gamyayā athā aakṛtyāḥ vanam tulyam sadbhāvena prasajyate jāti pakṣa vimokena vana siddhānta dūṣaṇam iti nigaditam etat loka siddhaiḥ padārthaiḥ vyavahṛtiḥ iha śāstre na svatantra abhyupetaiḥ bhavati ca jana dṛṣṭyā jāti paṅkti ādi bhedaḥ yadi tu na ghaṭate asau na eva bādhaḥ asti kaḥ cit 
SV_5,16.1ab–5,16.4ab	 bhavetām nāma śabda arthau yau= etau= uditau tvayā yad arthaḥ tu prayāsaḥ ayam sa sambandhaḥ nirūpyatām pūrvam eva upadiṣṭaḥ san sambandhaḥ kin tu pṛcchyate svarūpa akathanāt ca etat uttaram na upapadyate kim auṣadham jvarasya iti pṛṣṭaḥ yadi vadet idam yena asau naśyati iti evam kim tena kathitam bhavet tatra ke cit vanti eva pūrvatra aparitoṣataḥ 
SV_5,16.4cd–5,16.7cd	 praśnaḥ punar upakrāntaḥ sambandha antaram icchatā yaḥ saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandhaḥ prati iti uttaraḥ yatas sā ca anya pūrvikā tasmāt na asya pratyāyana aṅga tā ajānānaḥ api saṃjñā tvam sambandha antara darśanāt buddhyate artham tatas paścāt kaḥ cit saṃjñā iti manyate tam eva anyaḥ avinābhāvam atra sambandham icchati na hi tasmāt vinā śabde jñāte syāt artha bodhanam 
SV_5,16.8ab–5,16.11ab	 tattva yuktam na bhāṣye asti tādṛś sambandha kīrtanam yadi hi etāvatā ucyeta kim na anuktaḥ pratīyate prayuktaḥ ca avinā abhāva saṃjñā lokāt tu gamyate saṃjñā iti agamyamāne api gamaka tvam pratīyate tasmāt saḥ eva śabda artha cintā vyavahitaḥ adhunā nitya anitya vicāra artham sambandhaḥ smāryate punar yat śabde jñātaḥ iti evam śaktiḥ eva atra kīrtyate 
SV_5,16.11cd–5,16.14cd	 kartṛ tvam karaṇa tvam vā yat tasya artha abhidhām prati svatas na eva asti śakta tvam vācya avācakayoḥ mithas pratītiḥ samayāt puṃsām bhavet akṣinikoca vat samayaḥ pratimartyam yā pratyuccāraṇam eva vā kriyate jagat ādau vā sakṛt ekena kena cit pratyekam vā api sambandhaḥ bhidyeta ekaḥ atha vā bhavet eka tve kṛtakaḥ na syāt bhinnaḥ ced bheda dhīḥ bhavet 
SV_5,16.15ab–5,16.18ab	 bhinna tve pratisambandham śaktiḥ kalpyā abhidhā prati ekasmin jñāta śaktau vā na anyena artha matiḥ bhavet atha yaḥ yasya puṃsaḥ syāt sa tena pratipadyate yasya anekena sambandhaḥ kṛtaḥ tasya katham bhavet eka arthānām vikalpaḥ ced na itara atyanta bādhanāt samuccayaḥ api na eteṣām vyavahāre avagamyate kiñ cit eva ekam ādāya vyavahāraḥ hi dṛśyate 
SV_5,16.18cd–5,16.21cd	 bahubhiḥ kṛta sambandhe na ca ekaḥ gamakaḥ bhavet śabda arthayoḥ abhede api pumba hutve api kartari na ayam vā iti matiḥ dṛṣṭā vikalpaḥ atas na yujyate go śabde sakṛt ukte ca bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu vikalpyamāne sambandhe kaḥ cit budhyeta na itare samuccayaḥ nṛ bhedāt ced na vaktra aikyāt asambhavāt vaktṛ śrotṛdhiyoḥ bhedāt vyavahāraḥ ca duṣyati 
SV_5,16.22ab–5,16.24cd	 vaktuḥ anyaḥ hi sambandhaḥ buddhau śrotuḥ tathā aparaḥ śrotuḥ kartum ca sambandham vaktā kam pratipadyatām pūrva dṛṣṭaḥ hi yaḥ tena śrotuḥ na eva karoti tam yam karoti navam saḥ api na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ sarvathā śrotṛ siddhiḥ ced asiddham na itaraḥ vadet ghaṭa ādau api tulyam ced na sāmānya prasiddhitaḥ 
SV_5,16.25ab–5,16.28ab	 yadi api jñāta sāmarthyā vyaktiḥ kartum na śkyate kriyate yā na tasyāḥ ca śaktiḥ kārye avadhāritā tathā api ākṛtitaḥ siddhā śaktiḥ utpādana ādiṣu tasyāḥ na ca ādi mattā asti sambandhaḥ tu ādimān tava yadi tatra api sāmānyam nityam abhyupagamyate tathā api asmad matam siddham na tu dvi ākāra sambhavaḥ śaktiḥ eva hi sambandhaḥ bhedaḥ ca asyāḥ na vidyate 
SV_5,16.28cd–5,16.31cd	 sā hi kārya anumeya tvāt tad bhedam anuvartate anyathā anupapattyā ca śakti sadbhāva kalpanam na ca ekayā eva siddhe arthe bahvīnām kalpanā iṣyate sambandha ākhyāna kāle ca go śabda ādau udīrite ke cit sambandha buddhyā artham buddhi ante na apare tathā tatra sambandhana astitve sarvaḥ artham na avadhārayet astitve sarva bodhaḥ ced na kaiḥ cit anupagrahāt 
SV_5,16.32ab–5,16.35ab	 jñāpaka tvāt dhi sambandhaḥ sva ātma jñānam apekṣate tena asau vidyamānaḥ api na agṛhītaḥ prakāśakaḥ vidyamānasya ca arthasya dṛṣṭam agrahaṇam kva cit na tu atyanta asataḥ astitvam kān cit pratyupapadyate viruddhau sat asat bhāvau na syātām eka vastuni nanu tulyam virodhi tvam jñāta ajñāta tvayoḥ api jñānam hi puruṣa ādhāram tad bhedāt na virotsyate 
SV_5,16.35cd–5,16.38cd	 puruṣa antara saṃstham ca na ajñānam tena bādhyate sambandha ādhāra tāyām ca virodhaḥ sat asat tvayoḥ pratyukta tvāt ca bhedasya tad vaśāt na avirodhitā andha anandha samīpa sthaḥ śuklaḥ andhaiḥ na avagamyate gamyate ca itaraiḥ tasya sat asat tvena tāvatā śakti aśaktyoḥ narāṇām tu bhedāt tatra avirodhitā na hi anyaḥ darśanasya asti sambandhāt dhetuḥ atra hi 
SV_5,16.39ab–5,16.42ab	 evam eva indriyaiḥ tulyam vyavahāra upalambhanam yeṣām syāt te avabhotsyante tatas artham na itare andhavat ādhāna vat sakṛḥ ca etat tantreṇa upakariṣyati smaraṇam bhetsyate ca asya vahni praṇayana ādi vat sarveṣām anabhijñānām pūrva pūrva prasiddhitaḥ siddhaḥ sambandhaḥ iti evam sambandha ādiḥ na vidyate pratyuccāraṇa nirvṛttiḥ bhāṣyaḥ eva nirākṛtāḥ 
SV_5,16.42cd–5,16.45ab	 sarga ādau ca kriyā na asti tādṛś kālaḥ hi na iṣyate yadi tu ādau jagat sṛṣṭvā dharma adharmau sa sādhanau yathā śabda artha sambandhān vedān kaḥ cit pravartayet jagat hitāya vedasya tathā kiñ cit na duṣyati sarvajña vat tu dussādham iti atra etat na saṃśritam yadā sarvam idam na āsīt kva avasthā tatra gamyatām 
SV_5,16.45cd–5,16.48cd	 prajāpateḥ kva vā sthānam kim rūpam ca pratīyatām jñātā ca kaḥ tadā tasya yaḥ janān bodhayiṣyati upalabdheḥ vinā ca etat katham adhyavasīyatām pravṛttiḥ katham ādyā ca jagataḥ sampratīyate śarīra ādeḥ vinā ca asya katham icchā api sarjane śarīra ādi atha tasya syāt tasya utpattiḥ na tad kṛtā tadvat anya prasaṅgaḥ api nityam yadi tat iṣyate 
SV_5,16.49ab–5,16.52ab	 pṛthivī ādau anutpanne kimmayam tat punar bhavet prāṇinām prāya duḥkhā ca sisṛkṣā asya na yujyate sādhanam ca asya dharma ādi tadā kiñ cat na vidyate na ca nissādhanaḥ kartā kaḥ cit sṛjati kiñ cana na ādhāreṇa vinā sṛṣṭi ḥ ūrṇanābheḥ api iṣyate prāṇinām bhakṣaṇāt ca api tasya lālā pravarttate abhāvāt ca anukampyānām na anukampā asya jāyate 
SV_5,16.52cd–5,16.55cd	 sṛjet ca śubham eva ekam anukampā prayojitaḥ atha aśubhāt vinā sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiḥ vā na upapadyate ātma adhīna abhyupāye hi bhavet kim nāma dṛṣkaram tathā ca apekṣamāṇasya svātantryam pratihanyate jagat ca asṛjataḥ tasya kim nāma iṣṭam na sidhyati prayojanam anuddiśya na mandaḥ api pravartate evam eva pravṛttiḥ ced caitanyena asya kim bhavet 
SV_5,16.56ab–5,16.59ab	 krīḍā arthāyām pravṛttau ca vihanyeta kṛtārtha tā bahu vyāpāra tāyām ca kleśaḥ bahutaraḥ bhavet saṃhāra icchā api ca etasya bhavet apratyayāt punar na cakais cit asau jñātum kādā cit api śakyate sva rūpeṇa upalabdhe api sraṣṭṛ tvam na avagamyate sṛṣṭi ādyāḥ praṇinaḥ ye ca budhyantām kim nu te tadā kutas vayam iha utpannāḥ iti tāvat na jānate 
SV_5,16.59cd–5,16.62cd	 prāc avasthām ca jagataḥ sraṣṭṛ tvam ca prajāpateḥ na ca tad vacanena eṣām pratipattiḥ su niścitāḥ asṛṣṭvā api hi asau brūyāt ātma aiśvarya prakāśanāt evam vedaḥ api tad pūrvaḥ tad sadbhāva ādi bodhane sa āśaṅkaḥ na pramāṇam syāt nityasya vyāpṛtiḥ kutas yadi prāk api asau tasmāt arthāt āsīt na tena saḥ sambaddhaḥ iti tasya anyaḥ tad arthaḥ anya prarocanā 
SV_5,16.63ab–5,16.66ab	 stuti vākya kṛtaḥ ca eṣa janānām mati vibhramaḥ paurvāparya aparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ anyām kurute matim upākhyāna ādi rūpeṇa vṛttiḥ veda vat eva naḥ dharma ādau bhārata ādīnām bhrāntiḥ tebhyaḥ api atas bhavet ākhyāna anupayogi tvāt teṣu sarveṣu vidyate stuti nindā āśrayaḥ kaḥ cit vedaḥ tat coditaḥ api vā vedasya ādi pravṛttau ca na akṛta tva matiḥ bhavet 
SV_5,16.66cd–5,16.69cd	 pralayeṣu sthitiḥ ca asya sa āśaṅkā syāt prajāpatau kartṛ sarga vināśānām atha anādi tva kalpanā sā evam yuktāyatha idānīm bhūtānām dṛśyate kramāt pralaye api pramāṇam naḥ sarva uccheda ātmake na hi na ca prayojanam tena syāt prajāpati karmaṇā na ca karmavatām yuktā sthitiḥ tad bhoga varjitāḥ karma antara niruddham hi phalam na syāt kriyā antarāt 
SV_5,16.70ab–5,16.73ab	 sarveṣām tu phala apetam na sthānam upapadyate na ca api anupabhogaḥ asau kasya cit karmaṇaḥ phalam aśeṣa karma nāśe vā punar sṛṣṭiḥ na yujyate karmāṇām vā api abhivyaktau kim nimittam tadā bhavet īśvara icchā yadīṣyeta sā eva syāt loka kāraṇam īśvara icchā vaśi tve hi niṣphalā karma kalpanā na ca animittayā yuktam utpattum hi īśvara icchayā 
SV_5,16.73cd–5,16.76cd	 yat vā tasyāḥ nimittam yat tat bhūtānām bhaviṣyati sanniveśa viśiṣṭānām utpattim yaḥ gṛha ādi vat sādhayet cetanā adhiṣṭhām dehānām tasya ca uttaram kasya cit dhetu mātra tvam yadi adhiṣṭhātṛtā iṣyate karmabhiḥ sarva jīvānām tad siddheḥ siddha sādhanam icchā pūrvaka pakṣe api tad pūrva tvena karmaṇām icchā anantara siddhiḥ tu dṛṣṭānte api na vidyate 
SV_5,16.77ab–5,16.80ab	 anekāntaḥ ca hetuḥ te tad śarīra ādinā bhavet utpattimān ca tad dehaḥ deha tvāt asmad ādi vat atha tasya api adhiṣṭhānam tena eva iti avipakṣatā aśarīraḥ hi adhiṣṭhātā na ātmā mukta ātma vat bhavet kumbhakāra ādi adhiṣṭhānam ghaṭa ādau yadi ca iṣyate na īśvara adhiṣṭhita tvam syāt asti ced sādhya hīna tā yathā siddhe ca dṛṣṭānte bhavet dhetoḥ viruddha tā 
SV_5,16.80cd–5,16.83cd	 anīśvara vināśi ādi kartṛmat tvam prasajyate kulāla vat ca na etasya vyāpāraḥ yadi kalpate acetanaḥ katham bhāvaḥ tad icchām anurudhyate tasmāt na paramāṇu ādeḥ ārambhaḥ syāt tad icchayā puruṣasya ca śuddhasya na aśuddhā vikṛtiḥ bhavet svādhīna tvāt ca dharma ādeḥ tena kleśaḥ na yujyate tad vaśena pravṛttau vā vyatirekaḥ prasajyate 
SV_5,16.84ab–5,16.87ab	 svayam ca śuddha rūpa tvāt asattvāt ca anya vastunaḥ svapna ādi vat avidyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ tasya kim kṛtā anyena upaplave abhīṣṭe dvaita vādaḥ prasajyate svābhāvikīm avidyām tu na ucchettum kaḥ cit arhati vilakṣaṇa upapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikī kva cit na tu eka ātmā abhyupāyānām hetuḥ asti vilakṣaṇaḥ pumān akartā yeṣām tu teṣām api guṇaiḥ kriyā 
SV_5,16.87cd–5,16.90cd	 katham ādau bhavet tatra karma tāvat na vidyate mithyājñānam na trāsti rāga dveṣa ādayaḥ api vā manaḥ vṛttiḥ hi sarveṣām na ca utpannam tadā manaḥ karmaṇām śakti avasthānām yaiḥ uktā bandha hetu tā sā na yuktāḥ na kāryam hi śakti sthāt kāraṇāt bhavet dadhi śaktiḥ na hi kṣīre dādhika ārambham arhati dadhi ārambhasya sā hetuḥ tatas anyā dādhikasya tu 
SV_5,16.91ab–5,16.93cd	 kāraṇāt śakti avasthāt ca yadi kāryam prajāyate bandhaḥ punar prasajyeta phale datte api karmaṇā śakti avastha tvam eva iṣṭam vināśe api hi karmaṇām prāk ca api śakti sadbhāvāt anuṣṭhānam vṛthā bhavet śakti avastham ca rāga ādi kim na iṣṭam bandha kāraṇam karma adatta phala tvāt ced na avyaktim api tat vrajet 
SV_5,16.94ab–5,16.97ab	 tad śakti aprayogi tvāt na jñānam mokṣa kāraṇam karma śaktyā na hi jñānam virodham upagacchati yadi api ajñāna janya tvam karmaṇām avagamyate rāga ādi vat tathā api eṣām na jñānena nirākriyā karma kṣayaḥ hi vijñānāt iti etat ca apramāṇa vat phalasya alpasya vā dānam rāja putra aparādha vat adya tve api hi śakti stham yadi syāt karma kāraṇam 
SV_5,16.97cd–5,16.100cd	 tatas pradhāna kāle api yujyate kāraṇa abhidhā manaḥ vṛttiḥ idānīm tu hetuḥ na asti ca sā tadā manasām saṅkarāt ca api tadā syāt karma saṅkaraḥ gasmāt na eṣaḥ adhikāra ākhyaḥ bandha hetuḥ prakalpate yogya tve api adhikāra ākhye viprayogaḥ na yujyate caitanyam yogya tā puṃsaḥ prakṛteḥ tad anātma tā bhoktṛ bhogya tvayoḥ te ca na tābhyām apagacchataḥ 
SV_5,16.101ab–5,16.104ab	 utpattau karmaṇām ca iṣṭam ajñānam kāraṇam yadi tad nāśāt syāt anutpattiḥ teṣām na phaloa varjanam jñānam mokṣa nimittam ca gamyate na indriya ādinā na ca sāṅkhya ādi vijñānāt mokṣaḥ vedena codyate ātmā jñātavyaḥ iti etat mokṣa artham na ca coditam karma pravṛtti hetu tvam ātma jñānasya lakṣyate vijñāte ca asya pārārthye yā api nāma phala śrutiḥ 
SV_5,16.104cd–5,16.107cd	 sārthavādaḥ bhavet eva na svarga ādeḥ phala antaram sukha upabhoga rūpaḥ ca yadi mokṣaḥ prakalpyate svargaḥ eva bhavet eṣa paryāyeṇa kṣayaḥ ca saḥ na hi kāraṇa vat kiñ cit akṣayitvena gamyate tasmāt karma kṣayāt eva hetu abhāve na mucyate na hi abhāva ātmakam muktvā mokṣa nitya tva kāraṇam na ca kriyāyāḥ kasyāḥ cit abhāvaḥ phalam iṣyate 
SV_5,16.108ab–5,16.111ab	 tatra jñāta ātma tattvānām bhogāt pūrva kriyā kṣaye uttara pracaya asattvāt dehaḥ na utpadyate punar karma janyā upabhoga artham śarīram na pravartate tad abhāve na kaḥ cit dhi hetuḥ tatra avatiṣṭhate mokṣa arthī na pravarteta tatra kāmya niṣiddhyoḥ nitya naimittike kuryāt pratyavāya jihāsayā prārthyamānam phalam jñātam na ca anicchoḥ bhaviṣyati 
SV_5,16.111cd–5,16.114cd	 ātma jñe ca etat asti iti tat jñānam uapi ujyate sarga pralaya vijñānam samasta jagat āśrayam sva śarīra vidām puṃsām na ādhikyena upayujyate tasmāt adya vat eva atra sarga pralaya kalpanā samasta kṣaya janmabhyām na sidhyati apramāṇikā sarvajña vat niṣedhyā ca sraṣṭuḥ sadbhāva kalpanā na ca dharmāt ṛte tasya bhavet lokāt viśiṣṭha tā 
SV_5,16.115ab–5,16.118ab	 na ca ananuṣṭhitaḥ dharmaḥ na anuṣṭhānam ṛte mateḥ na ca vedāt ṛte sā syāt vedaḥ na ca pada ādibhiḥ tasmāt prāk api sarve amī sraṣṭuḥ āsan pada ādayaḥ syāt tad pūrvaka tā ca asya caitanyāt asmad ādi vat evam ye yuktibhiḥ prāhuḥ teṣām durlabham uttaram aneṣyaḥ vyavahāraḥ ayam anādiḥ veda vādibhiḥ pratyakṣa ādau upakṣīṇe yaḥ anumānena ḍittha vat 
SV_5,16.118cd–5,16.121cd	 sambandhi tvāt niyoktāram gavā ādau api kalpayet gavā ādi śabda sambandham sarvaḥ anyasmāt prapadyate madvat tad vyavahāri tvāt tasya etat pratisādhanam devadatta ādi śabde api prasaktā evam anāditā sambandhasya balīyaḥ tvāt dṛṣṭa bādhāt nivartate tatra api śakti nitya tvam niyogasya tu anitya tā tad gatāt ca api anitya tvāt śaktau bhrāntiḥ pravartate 
SV_5,16.122ab–5,16.124cd	 gavā ādiṣu tu na bhrāntiḥ niyoga anāditāḥ yatas yaḥ yaḥ gṛhītaḥ sarvasmāt pūrvam sambandha darśanāt siddhaḥ sambandhaḥ iti evam sambandha ādiḥ na vidyate yadā ca āpta praṇīta tvāt śabdaḥ artham pratipādayet na sva śaktyā tad āpta tvam mitau na smaryate katham yathā bauddha ādayaḥ yāvat buddha ādi uktam na jānate 
SV_5,16.125ab–5,16.127cd	 na tāvat pratipadyante bodhe vākyena sati api samaye kathyamāne anyaiḥ asmarantaḥ api pāṇinim ādaicaḥ pratipadyante vṛddhim kartum smṛtiḥ vṛthā sūtra sthaḥ pāṇiniḥ tatra sva saṃjñām pratipādayet gauḥ sāsnādimatī iti evam vākyam tu atra na vidyate asambandhāt ca sarveṣām evam kartum asambhavaḥ 
SV_5,16.128ab–5,16.131ab	 tasmāt na pratipattiḥ syāt kathan cit kartṛ varjitā dṛṣārtha vyavahāra tvāt vṛddhi ādau sambhavet api dharmāya niyamaḥ atra api na vinā pāṇineḥ bhavet ākāra anugamaḥ yaḥ hi vṛddhyā syāt āśvalāyane na asau apāṇinīya tve sādhuḥ iti avagamyate dṛṣṭe bhavatu mā vā bhūt kartṛ sampratipanna tā vaididaḥ vyavahāraḥ tu na kartṛ smaraṇāt ṛte 
SV_5,16.131cd–5,16.134cd	 burgeṣu gavi go śabda prayogaḥ gamyate katham gatvā ced kena cit dṛṣṭaḥ sambanddhā kim na gacchati īśvara tvāt agatiḥ ca asya na kva cit pratibadhyate bahūnām kāryataḥ ca api saṅgānam kena vāryate ekatra kathitam ca api lokena anyatra nīyate vṛddhyāt iva atas vyākhyā dvitīyā eva atra śobhanā kān cit prasiddha sambandhān abhyupetya vadet yadi 
SV_5,16.135ab–5,16.138ab	 sambandha karaṇam tatra ke siddhāḥ iti durvadam na tāvat anyaḥ eva āsan śabdāḥ iti hi yuktimat viśeṣaḥ adyatanānām ca gavā ādīnām na dṛśyate śabda artha anāditām muktvā sambandhānādi kāraṇam na syāt anyat atas vede sambandha ādiḥ na vidyate upāya rahita tvena sambandha karaṇa anumā anākhyāna anumānam tu dṛṣṭena eva viruddhyate 
SV_5,16.138cd–5,16.141ef	 buddhānām dṛśyamānā ca pratipattiḥ punar punar upāyaḥ iti tad ha anirasiddha avagatim prati hasta saṃjñā ādi upāyaḥ hi siddhaḥ nādya kriyāsu naḥ na hi asau jñāta sāmarthyaḥ vinā anyaiḥ vyavahartṛbhiḥ śabda vṛddha abhidheyān ca pratyakṣeṇa atra paśyati śrotuḥ ca pratipanna tvam anumānena ceṣṭayā anyathā anupapattyā ca buddhyet śaktim dvaya āśritām arthāpattyā avabuddhi ante sambandham tri pramāṇakam 
SV_5,17.1ab–5,17.4ab	 citra ādi niṣphala tve api yat uktam sādhana dvayam tatra hetoḥ asiddha tvam ānantaryam hi acoditam ānantarya śrutiḥ ca atra sāma arthyāt api na iṣyate na aviśeṣā phala utpattiḥ karmaṇā na upapadyate karmaṇām ca api vaicitryāt deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇāt kasya cit ca arddha bhukta tvāt karma anyat pratibadhyate tena anantarya niṣpattiḥ phalasya iha apramāṇikāḥ 
SV_5,17.4cd–5,17.7cd	 pratyakṣa ādi visaṃvādaḥ na śabde doṣa māsajet ānantarya visaṃvādaḥ na aviśeṣa pravartinīm codanām bādhitum śaktaḥ sphuṭāt viṣaya bhedataḥ yā tu mardana sādharmyāt ānantaryā anumā kṛtā bādhyate anupalabdhyā asau samāna viṣayāḥ yatas dṛṣṭa arthasya api sevā ādeḥ āyātam api sat phalam utpadyate cireṇa eva pratibandhena kena cit 
SV_5,17.8ab–5,17.10cd	 upta mātre na hi vrīhau phalam utpadyate kva cit atha aṅkuraḥ api tatra syāt svargaḥ api asti iti gamyatām sthūlībhūtaḥ cireṇa eṣa bhogya tvam pratipadyate sarvasya utpadyamānasya kramaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sthitaḥ anantara phala tvam tu citra ādeḥ yadi sādhyate tatas syāt siddha sādhya tvam anyadā na phalam bhavet 
SV_5,17.11ab–5,17.14ab	 vyabhicārāt ca sevā ādeḥ paśu ādeḥ sādhana antaram kim api adṛṣṭam asti eva tatra anyat niṣpramāṇakam īśvara icśā adhikāra ādi śabda liṅga ādi varjanāt kṛtam kadā cit citra ādi śabdena tu avagamyate nirnimittā na ca utpattiḥ na hi sarva apramāṇa tā bodhayan na ca śabdaḥ atra prāmāṇyāt ativarttate yeṣām tu iha phalāni eva citra ādīni iti kalpanā 
SV_5,17.14cd–5,17.17cd	 nirnimittam phalam teṣām syāt iha akṛta karmaṇām citra ādīnām phalam tāvat kṣīṇam tatra eva janmani na ca svarga phalasya iha kaḥ cit aṃśaḥ anuvartate na eva hi anya phalam karma sādhayet naḥ phala antaram gautamīye api tad śeṣaḥ tasmāt citra ādi apekṣayā svābhāvika tve siddhe ca karma anantara bhāvi api phalam kriyā nimitta tvam na kathan cit prapadyate 
SV_5,17.18ab–5,17.21ab	 tatra mleccha ādi vat sarve karma akṛtvā api vaidikam palam labhante iti evam naṣṭā veda pramāṇa tā anantaram niyogena paśu ādi ca bhavet yadi pratyakṣa phala tā eva syāt trivṛt pāna vireka vat janma antara anubhūtam ca na smaryate iti īdṛśam na bhāṣyam na ca sūtram syāt aprāpte śāstram arthavat tasmāt kāla aviśeṣeṇa codanā arthaḥ yathā sthitaḥ 
SV_5,17.21cd–5,17.24ab	 sa tathā eva anugantavyaḥ na adhikaḥ niṣpramāṇakaḥ sarveṣām karma vaiguṇyāt phala abhāvam vadanti ye ānantaryam upetya eva te svābhāvika vādinaḥ svargasya amuṣmika tvam tu ṣaṣṭha ādye sthāpayiṣyate paśu ādeḥ niyama abhāvaḥ yoga siddhiḥ iti iha tu yadā kadā cit bhavat etat iṣyate phalam hi paśu ādi na sāmparāyikam 
SV_5,17.24cd–5,17.26cd	 tathā sthitasya eva hi tasya sādhanam vidhīyate yaḥ api bhṛśam tvarā anvitaḥ sādhāraṇam yat tu palam bahūnām svabhāvataḥ tādṛśam eva ca iṣṭam sarvasya vā aasat na tayā eva kāmyam vṛṣṭi ādi tat ca aihikam eva yuktam kamipadam aviśiṣṭam yadi api śrūyate vā bhavati phala viśeṣī na anyathā kāmyate hi phalati yadi ni sarva tat kadā cit tadā eva dhruvam aparam abhuktam karma śāstrī yamāḥ te 
SV_5,18.1ab–5,18.4ab	 sākṣāt yadi api sambandhaḥ na ātmanaḥ yajña sādhanaiḥ tathā api lakṣaṇa āvṛttyā śarīra dvārakaḥ bhavet pratyakṣa tvam ca deha stham bhāktam ātmani kalpitam ātmanaḥ svarga yānam vā śarīrasya upacaryyate nairātmyena atra ca ākṣiptāḥ sarvāḥ eva hi codanāḥ sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ tad uktaḥ na hi siddhyati tāḥ hi kartuḥ phalena āhuḥ sambandham kvāpi janmani 
SV_5,18.4cd–5,18.7cd	 na ca vijñāna mātra tve bhoktṛ kartṛ tva sambhavaḥ śarīra vinipātāt ca param na anyat yat eṣyate adatta phalaiṣṭi ādau tadā tat vacanam mṛṣā tasmāt veda pramāṇa artham ātmā atra pratipādyate yadi api prakṛtam vākyam vyākhyāyeta artha vādataḥ śarīra indriya buddhibhyaḥ vyatirikta tvm ātmanaḥ nitya tvam ca iṣyate śeṣam śarīra ādi vinaśyate 
SV_5,18.8ab–5,18.11ab	 nityaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve pratipannaḥ api san yadā na karma phala sambandham bhoga kāle avabudhyate mayā yat tu kṛtam karma tasya idam bhujyate phalam śubha aśubham mayā eva iti tadā kaḥ asya rasaḥ bhavet aprāmṛśyamāne hi sva karma pratyaye phale na viśeṣaḥ bhavet kaḥ cit sva para ātmā upabhogayoḥ kurvan api aśubham karma tena evam cintayet naraḥ 
SV_5,18.11cd–5,18.14cd	 na smariṣyāmi bhoge aham iti na etat vivarjayet tatra nitya tva pakṣe api kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau phalatas tulya rūpau ced vṛthā tad pratipādanam na eṣa doṣaḥ na bhoge hi smṛtiḥ naḥ upayujyate na pravṛtiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā bhoga kāle smṛteḥ bhavet tad aṅgam yaḥ parāmarśaḥ tat astitvam ca mṛgyate prāk pravṛtteḥ tu saḥ asti eva viduṣām śāstrataḥ sphuṭaḥ 
SV_5,18.15ab–5,18.18ab	 paścāt api ca śāstra jñāḥ vimṛśanti eva ke cana teṣām eva adhikāraḥ ca mā bhūt aviduṣām tu saḥ parāmarśaḥ ca sarvatra na asti sarva pramāṇakaḥ na ca anyena aparāmṛṣṭe syāt anyasya apramāṇa tā na avabudhyeta yaḥ tu evam mama asmāt karmaṇaḥ phalam bhaviṣyati iti avidvat tvāt daivāt eva atra na kriyā aparāmṛśyamāne api svāpa kāle sukha āśraye 
SV_5,18.18cd–5,18.21cd	 sambhoge mṛdu śayyā ādau prāc pravṛttiḥ ca dṛśyate bhoga kāle anusandadhyāt phalam yadi tu kaḥ cana ratha ādi karma vat yāge śāstram syāt aprakalpakam tava nitya vibhu tvābhyām ātmānaḥ niṣkriyāḥ yadi sukha duḥkha avikāryāḥ ca kīdṛśaḥ kartṛ bhoktṛ tā atha kartṛ tva velāyām duḥkha ādeḥ ca api janmani prāgrūpāt anyathātvam syāt nityatā asya virudhyate 
SV_5,18.22ab–5,18.25ab	 na anitya śabda vācya tvam ātmanaḥ vinivāryate vikriyā mātra vāci tve na hi ucchedaḥ asya tāvatā syātām atyanta nāśe asya kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau na tu avasthā antara prāptau loke bāla yuva ādi vat avasthā antara bhāvyetat phalam mama śubha aśubham iti jñātvā anutiṣṭhan ca vijahat ceṣṭate janaḥ anavasthā antara prāptiḥ dṛśyate na ca kasya cit 
SV_5,18.25cd–5,18.28cd	 anucchedāt tu na anya tvam bhoktuḥ lokaḥ avagacchati sukha duḥkha ādi avasthāḥ ca gacchan api naraḥ mama caitanya dravya satta ādi rūpam na eva vimuñcati duḥkhinaḥ sukhī avasthāyām naśyeyuḥ sarve eva te duḥkhi tvam ca anuvarteta vināśe vikriyā ātmake tasmāt ubhaya hānena vyāvṛtti anugama ātmakaḥ puruṣaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ kuṇḍala ādiṣu svarṇa tvat 
SV_5,18.29ab–5,18.32ab	 na ca kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve puṃsaḥ avasthāsam āśrite tena avasthāvataḥ tattvāt karttā eva āpnoti tad phalam na ca avasthā antara utpāde pūrva atyantam vinaśyati uttara anuguṇa tvāt tu sāmānya ātmani līyate sva rūpeṇa hi avasthānām anyonyasya virodhitā aviruddhaḥ tu sarvāsu sāmānya ātmā pravartate nairātmya vāda pakṣe tu pūrvam eva avabudhyate 
SV_5,18.32cd–5,18.35cd	 mad vināśāt phalam nasyāt mattaḥ anyasya atha vā bhavet iti na eva pravṛttiḥ syāt na ca veda pramāṇa tā janma anare abhyupete api jñāna mātra ātma vādinām jñānānām kṣaṇika tvāt dhi kartṛ bhoktranyatā bhavet niṣkriya tva avibhu tvābhyām na ca deha antara aśritiḥ kartā yaḥ eva santānaḥ nanu bhoktā saḥ eva naḥ vijñāna kṣaṇa bhedaḥ tu tvad avasthā antaraiḥ samaḥ 
SV_5,18.36ab–5,18.39ab	 kartṛ tvam eva duḥsādham dīrgha kāleṣu karmasu satsu jñāna sahastreṣu kula kalpa upamam hi tat vyatiriktaḥ hi santānaḥ yadi na abhyupagamyate santāninām anitya tvāt kartā kaḥ cit na labhyate bhoktuḥ atyanta bhedāt ca prasajyeta akṛta āgamaḥ kṛta nāśam tu na brūmaḥ kṛtam na eva hi kena cit santāna ananyatāyām tu vācā uyukti antareṇa te 
SV_5,18.39cd–5,18.42ab	 tatra ca uktam na ca avastu santānaḥ kartṛ tām vrajet santāna kṣaṇika tve ca tat eva akṣaṇikaḥ tu atha siddhānta hāniḥ evam ca saḥ api dravya antaram bhavet ekā ca avyatiriktā ca santānibhyaḥ atha santatiḥ bheda abhedau prasaṅktavyau grāhya grāhakayoḥ yathā tasmāt atyanta bhedaḥ vā kathan cit vā api bhinna tā 
SV_5,18.42cd–5,18.45cd	 santānasya iti ayam ca ātmā syāt vaiśeṣika sāṃkhyayoḥ santānaḥ ayam saḥ eva iti na tu abhedāt vinā bhavet vāyudopādi santāne vāyu tvā ādiḥ na bhidyate jñāna tvena api abhinna tvam śūnya vāde nirākṛtam tathā eva karmabhiḥ veṣṭā phala artham citta vāsanā na ca atra vāsanā kālam kiñ cit cittam avasthitam avastu tvāt ca santānaḥ karma bhinā eva vāsyate 
SV_5,18.46ab–5,18.49ab	 tad pāramparya jāte api bhuñjāne karmaṇaḥ phalam tādātmyena vinā spaṣṭau kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau santāna antara jebhyaḥ ca yaḥ hetu phala bhāvataḥ viśeṣaḥ saḥ api dussādhaḥ parihāraḥ na ca anayoḥ tasmin asati api brūyāḥ parihāram tvam anyathā samāna pṛthivī vāsa jñāna tva ādi aviśeṣatas samānaḥ iti na api etad ekatva anugamāt vinā 
SV_5,18.49cd–5,18.52cd	 tena yat citta jam tasya santānaḥ iti vaḥ mṛṣā na hi yat śabda tad śabdau vartete bhinna vastuni tena eka ātmaka taiṣṭavyā tad santāna ātma vādibhiḥ nanu anya tvam vidantaḥ api putra ādi phala siddhaye pravartante yathā tadvat jñāna santāninaḥ api nam anya tve ca samāne api yathā vaṃśa antara udbhavāḥ na labhante phalam tadvat santāna antara jāḥ kṣaṇāḥ 
SV_5,18.53ab–5,18.56ab	 na tāvat buddhiḥ atra evam api ca ātma phala icchayā putrāi bharaṇe vṛttiḥ syāt tat api atra na asti te phala antaram anuddiśya na ca putra ādi bibhrati vinaṣṭasya tu na ātmīya santāna bharaṇāt phalam yaḥ tu anena eva mārgeṇa phala antaram api icchati sva santāni antaraiḥ bhogyam tad santānāni upakārakam anavasthā īdṛśī tasya sva upabhogāt ṛte bhavet 
SV_5,18.56cd–5,18.59cd	 na eva hi anyaḥ api santānī kaḥ cit tasya ātma vat mataḥ yāvat yāvat ca dūra sthe santānini phalam bhavet tāvat tāvat ca tat naśyet sutarām viprakarṣataḥ bharaṇam yat apatyānām tiryak ādiṣu dṛśyate ajñānam śaraṇam tatra prājñānām tu na yujyate deha antare ca buddhīnām sañcāraḥ na upapadyate pūrva dehāt bahis bhāvaḥ na ca tāsām pratīyate 
SV_5,18.60ab–5,18.63ab	 vāyunā preryamāṇam hi jvālā ādi anyatra sañcaret buddheḥ kāraṇa deśāt tu preraṇam na asti kena cit amūrta tvāt svayam na asau= utplutyāḥ anyatra gacchati jīvat dehe api tena asyāḥ gamanam na upapadyate antarā abhava dehaḥ tu niṣiddhaḥ vindhya vāsinā tad astitve pramāṇam hi na kiñ cit avagamyate sahasā jāyate tat ca sahasā eva vinaśyati 
SV_5,18.63cd–5,18.66cd	 sūkṣma rūpa ādi yuktam ca iti utprekṣā mātram eva tat sati api jñāna sañcāraḥ tatra syāt niṣpramāṇakaḥ tena ca anya śarīreṣu punar nikṣepa kalpanā kalala ādiṣu vijñānam asti iti etat ca sāhasam asan jāta indriya tvāt dhi na tatra arthaḥ avagamyate na ca artha avagateḥ anyat rūpam jñānasya yujyate mūrcchā ādau api tena asya sadbhāvaḥ na upapadyate 
SV_5,18.67ab–5,18.70ab	 na ca api śakti rūpeṇa tadā dhīḥ avatiṣṭhate nirāśraya tvāt śaktīnām sthitiḥ na hi avakalpate yadi bhūta indriya ādhārā jñānaśaktiḥ bhavet tatas tat caitanyam prasajyeta na ca janma antaram bhavet pariṇāma viveka ādyaiḥ śakti abhivyakti anugrahāt tebhyaḥ eva bhavet buddhiḥ na buddhi antara pūrvikā tathā eva uttara kāle api pūrva buddheḥ yat ucyate 
SV_5,18.70cd–5,18.73cd	 buddhi antara prasūta tvam dṛṣṭāntaḥ atra na vidyate atha ādhāra vinirmuktā śaktiḥ syāt kalala ādiṣu paścāt vijñāna siddhi artham ātmā śakti abhidhaḥ bhavet śakti ādhāra prakptau vā na ātmanaḥ anyaḥ prakalpyate jvālā budbuda vat vṛttiḥ na ca ādhārāt dhiyām jñāna śakti svabhāvaḥ atas nityaḥ sarva gataḥ pumān deha antara kṣamaḥ kalpyaḥ saḥ agacchan eva yokṣyate 
SV_5,18.74ab–5,18.77ab	 yajamāna tvam api ātmā sa kriya tvāt prapadyate na parispandaḥ eva ekaḥ kriyāḥ naḥ kaṇa bhoji vat na ca sva samavetā eva kartṛbhiḥ kriyate kriyā kriyā dhātu artha mātram syāt anya ādhāre api kartṛ tā sattā jñāna ādi rūpāṇām kartā tāvat svayam pumān yaḥ api bhūta parispandaḥ tatra adhiṣṭānataḥ bhavet tad uddeśa pravṛtteḥ ca yā yā deha indriyaiḥ kriyā 
SV_5,18.77cd–5,18.80cd	 kriyate puruṣeṇa eva sā sā sarvā kṛta ucyate na eva hi eṣām pravṛttiḥ syāt puruṣeṇa aparigrahe asvātantryāt atas na eṣām parispande api kartṛ tā tad karma upārjitaiḥ cetaiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu karmasu kartṛ tā yajamānānām ṛtvij paraśukarma vat yathā parikrayāmnānāt ṛtvij dvārā kriyā iṣyate gamana ādi vidheḥ tadvat bhūta dvāra tvam āśritam 
SV_5,18.81ab–5,18.84ab	 krayaḥ yathā ātmanaḥ na asti gamana ādi tathā eva hi vidhīyate ca tena atra para dvāra asya kartṛ tā yathā vā devadattasya cchedane kāṣṭha saṃśrite kartṛ tvam evam puṃsaḥ syāt śarīra gamana ādiṣu vyāpāra antarataḥ tatra kartṛ tvam ced iha api naḥ saṅkalpa sattva vat tvābhyām pumān iṣṭaḥ prayojakaḥ sādhāraṇyena kartṛ tvam sattvavat tvena karmasu 
SV_5,18.84cd–5,18.87cd	 saṅkalpanaiḥ punar bhedāt pratikarmā asya kartṛ tā na ca sarvatra tulya tvam syāt prayojaka karmaṇām calanena hi asim yoddhā prayuṅkte cchedanam prati senāpatiḥ tu vāciava bhṛtyānām viniyojakaḥ rājā sannidhi mātreṇa viniyuṅkte kadā canaḥ tasmāt acalataḥ api syāt calane kartṛtā ātmanaḥ yathā eva abhidyamānasya devadattasya bhettṛ tā 
SV_5,18.88ab–5,18.91ab	 karma antaraiḥ yadā dānam sva vyāpāraḥ saḥ eva vā bhūta kriyāsu puṃsaḥ syāt tāni bhūta antaraiḥ punar tāni bhūta antarebhyaḥ ca iti evamādiḥ na vidyate karma kṣayāt tu anātmīyaiḥ kṛtam karma na limpati anvārambhaṇa mānādau= audumbarī ādi varttini svarūpa asambhavāt yaṣṭuḥ śarīreṇa eva kartṛ tā tasmāt yathā kṛtau śāstram pravṛttam vyaktim āśrayet 
SV_5,18.91cd–5,18.95ab	 tathā puṃsi pravṛttasya bhūta indriya samāśrayaḥ paraiḥ abhigatān pūrvam ātma hetun nirasyati na iti etāvat avacchedyam vidharmāṇaḥ ime yatas atha avasthā antaram tatra tathā mṛtyuḥ api iṣyatām etāvan iha bhedaḥ syāt śarīre dṛḍhaḥ eva yā prāṇa ādi apagatiḥ tatra nimittam na pratīyate guṇaḥ dravya vināśāt vā vināśam upagacchati 
SV_5,18.95cd–5,18.98cd	 guṇa antara upapātāt vā tasmāt utkṛtya nāśyate na tāvat tat dvayam mṛtyau sarvasya eva upalabhyate avinaṣṭa śarīrasya prāṇa ādiḥ ca apagacchati tasmāt na deha dharma tvam prāṇa ādeḥ iti gamyate tasmin dṛṣṭe api asadbhāvāt sraj vilepana gandha vat bahis vṛtti tvam api asti prāṇa ādeḥ iti gamyate para indriyaiḥ sukha ādiḥ tu na antara tvāt pratīyate 
SV_5,18.99ab–5,18.102ab	 prahṛṣṭa vadana tva ādi liṅga gamyam sadā eva hi antar sthiteḥ na dṛṣṭiḥ ced pāṭite api anupagrahāt antar śarīre rūpa ādi pāṭitasya upalabhyate na sukha ādiḥ agaḥ asya asau na manaḥ buddhi vat guṇaḥ guṇa tvāt āśrita tvam hi sukha ādeḥ syāt rasa ādi vat yaḥ āśritaḥ saḥ ātmā iti bruvāṇasya etat uttaram puṇānām paratantra tvāt guṇavān anumīyate 
SV_5,18.102cd–5,18.105cd	 siddhe guṇa tve tat tu asmān pratyasiddham sukha ādiṣu bhedena kim upanyastā tulya nyāya icchayā smṛtiḥ ubhayam na hi adṛṣṭe arthe vāsanātas ca siddhyati upalabdhim anāśritya smṛtyā eva icchā upajāyate upalabdhi samānaḥ asyāḥ kartā na ekāntataḥ bhavet upalabdhi anusāreṇa smṛtyātmā punar iṣyate samānaḥ tena kartā asti tad artham punar ucyate 
SV_5,18.106ab–5,18.109ab	 tatra api tu samānāyām santatau vāsanā yatas tasmāt sati api bhinna tve smaraṇam vyavatiṣṭate hetuṣu evam para ukteṣu pratiṣiddheṣu samprati aham pratyaya vijñeyaḥ svayam ātma upapādyate aham yāmi iti ahaṃśabdaḥ śarīra arthaḥ prayujyate gantṛ tvāt tasya na hi ātmā gamanam pratipadyate smaraṇa pratyabhijñāne bhavetām vāsanā vaśāt 
SV_5,18.109cd–5,18.112cd	 anya artha viṣaye jñātuḥ pratyabhijñā tu durlabhā aham vedmi iti aham buddhiḥ jñātāram adhigacchati tatra syāt jñātṛ vijñānam tad ādhāraḥ atha vā pumān kṛtam bhūta indriyāṇām ca caitanya pratiṣedhanam samasta vyasta saṅghāta viveka pariṇāminām sāṅkhya ādibhiḥ aśuddha tvāt saṅghātāt sanniveśataḥ mṛta vat ca śarīra tvāt bhūta tvāt bāhya bhūta vat 
SV_5,18.113ab–5,18.115cd	 cetana tve hi sarveṣām na sambandhaḥ parasparam sama tvāt ekacaitanye anyasya aṅga tvam virudhyate saṅghāta sanniveśau ca na staḥ pārārthya varjitau bhoktā ca cetanaḥ kaḥ cit asti iti atra aviruddha tā yadi syāt jñāna mātram ca kṣaṇikam jñātṛ tatra vaḥ na bhavet pratyabhijñānam pūrva jñātari samprati 
SV_5,18.116ab–5,18.119ab	 jñātavān aham eva idam purā idānīm ca vedmi aham tasya jñāna kṣaṇaḥ kaḥ nu viṣayaḥ parikalpyatām pūrva vṛtte hi viṣaye jñātavān iti sambhavet jānāmi iti na satyam syāt na idānīm vetti asau tatas yadi idānīntanaḥ grāhyaḥ jānāmi iti upapadyate jñātavān iti adaḥ asatyam na eva ajñāsīt ayam yatas ubhaya grāhyatām tu dvayam api anṛtam bhavet 
SV_5,18.119cd–5,18.122cd	 na hi etau jñātavantau vā jānītaḥ vā adhunā punar santānaḥ na ca tat grāhyaḥ dvairūpyasya asambhavāt jñātavān na hi asau pūrvam avastu tvāt na vā adhunā sāmānyam na ca kiñ cit te jñātṛ pūrva aparakṣaṇe sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñā ced na syāt asadṛśeṣu sā gām aham jñātavān pūrvam aśvam jānāmi aham punar atha jñātṛ tva sāmānyam tat syāt deha antareṣu api 
SV_5,18.123ab–5,18.126ab	 tatra sarveṇa vijñāte bhavet aham iti smṛtiḥ eka santāna je ca api saḥ iti syāt kṣaṇe matiḥ yathā deha antara jñāne ghaṭa ādau vā bahis sthite jñātari pratyabhijñām ca vāsanā kartum arhati na ātasmin saḥ iti jñānam na hi asau bhrānti kāraṇam na ca aham pratyayaḥ bhrāntiḥ iṣṭaḥ bādhaka varjanāt jñātuḥ anyaḥ ca viṣayaḥ tasya na syāt svabhāvataḥ 
SV_5,18.126cd–5,18.129cd	 aham pratyaya vijñeyaḥ jñātāḥ naḥ sarvadā eva hi guruḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśaḥ vā aham iti dehe api yā matiḥ bhrāntiḥ sā bheda rūpam hi guru me tat iti iṣyate idam mama īdṛśam cakṣuḥ manaḥ me bhrāntam iti api indriyeṣu api bhedena vyavahāraḥ ca dṛśyate ajñātṛ tvasya siddha tvāt virodhāt bhedavatī api pratyāsatti nimittaḥ tu syāt abheda matiḥ bhramaḥ 
SV_5,18.130ab–5,18.133ab	 mama ātmā iti mati bheda vyapadeśena yātmanaḥ tatra avasthā ātmanā bhedam jñānasya āśritya kalpanā mamaa iti etasya mukhya arthaḥ na ātmanaḥ anyaḥ pratīyate tena asau bheda hetuḥ syāt bhedaḥ ca jñāna hetukaḥ ye ca iha ājñāta nānātvāḥ teṣām deheṣu aham matiḥ tatra api ātma abhimānena iti ahambuddhiḥ dhruva ātmani ye tu vijñāta nānātvāḥ te deheṣu anahaṃkṛtāḥ 
SV_5,18.133cd–5,18.136cd	 jānāmi aham iti idam tu jñānam na eva nivarttate tad nivṛttau na teṣām syāt dhyānam śiṣya upadeśane pravṛttiḥ dṛśyate sā ca tena ātmā taiḥ pratīyate śāstrāt avardha vijñāte yadi aham jñātavān iti na avagacchet tatas sarvaḥ pravarteta āditas punar tena asmāt pratyabhijñānāt sarva loka avadhāritāt nairātmya vāda bādhaḥ syāt ete ca pratihetavaḥ 
SV_5,18.137ab–5,18.140ab	 hyastana āhamm atigrāhyaḥ jñātādya api anuvarttate ahaṃpratyaya gamya tvāt id ānīnta ba uddhṛ vat eṣa vā hyas bhavet jñātā jñātṛ tvāt tat eva vā hyastana jñātṛ vat teṣām pratyayānām ca sādhya tā eka santāna sambandhi jñātra hampratyaya tvataḥ hyastanāt yatanāḥ save tulya arthaḥ ca eka buddhi vat vedāt eva ātmanā astitvam yaḥ nāma pratipadyate 
SV_5,18.140cd–5,18.143cd	 virodham vā ātmanā brūyāt tam prati brāhmaṇa abhidhā anyathā anupapatteḥ ca vidhinā ātmani apekṣite astitvat yotanāt etaiḥ artha ākṣipta samarthanam śāntāyām vācya śaktāyām ātmā kena prakāśyate ātmanā eva prakāśyaḥ ayam ātmā jyotiḥ iti īritam agrāhya iti sāmānyāt sarveṇa iti pratīyate ātma jyotiṣṭvavacanāt paraiḥ iti avatiṣṭhate 
SV_5,18.144ab–5,18.148cd	 arthāt eva artha buddhiḥ yā sā śuddhā eva upamā ucyate sādṛśya bodhanam śabdaiḥ upamāna āgamau punar ātma jñāna āvinābhūta dṛṣṭa ceṣṭā nirūpaṇāt pareṣām ātma vijñānam anumānāt udāhṛtam sadasat nāśya nāśa ātma parikīrtanam ūḍhayā coditaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ ayam iti siddhāntam abravīt avināśī svarūpeṇa puruṣaḥ yā tu nāśitā mātrāṇām sā adhikārāṇām bhūta ādīnām asaṃjñitāḥ iti āha na asti kya nirākariṣṇuḥ ātma astitām bhāṣya kṛt atra yuktyā dṛḍha tvam etat viṣayaḥ ca bodhaḥ prayāti vedānta niṣevaṇena 
SV_6.1ab–6.4ab	 yadi anitya tva pakṣe api śabdāt arthaḥ avagamyate anādiḥ vyavahāraḥ ca nitya tvam kim nu sādhyate satyam icchanti te api evam nyāyaḥ tatra parīkṣyate na para abhyupagatya eva prāmāṇyam avatiṣṭhate yadā hi kṣaṇikaḥ śabdaḥ na śaktaḥ artha avadhāraṇe yuktyā avadhāryate tatra nirmalā veda dhīḥ bhavet nirmūlaiḥ api vijñānaiḥ dṛṣṭa artheṣu bhavet gatiḥ 
SV_6.4cd–6.7cd	 śruti mātra āśraya tvāt tu dharmaḥ dauḥsthityam āśritaḥ anādi vyavahāra tvam ādimat vastu saṃśrayam pratyākhyeyam ghaṭa tva ādi jātau vyakti bhramaḥ hi saḥ sthite kūṭastha nitya tve vyavahārasya nitya tā kūṭasthena vinā etena na tasya ālambanam bhavet prasiddha tvāt ṛte sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ hi na iṣyate tasmāt veda pramāṇa artham nitya tvam iha sādhyate 
SV_6.8ab–6.11ab	 paraspara āvinā abhāvāt anitya kṛtaka tvayoḥ kāraṇam dvaya siddhi artham kiñ cit kasya cit ucyate nānā deśau= agamya tvāt yugapad tulya buddhibhiḥ asmābhiḥ kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ bhavet akṣara lekhya vat yaugapadya upalambhāt vā bhedaḥ bhedāt ca kārya tā avibhu tve hi yugapanna ekaḥ nānā avagamyate kārtyena ca avagamya tvāt eka deśe ghaṭa ādi vat 
SV_6.11cd–6.14cd	 śabdasya avibhūtāḥ tasmāt anya tā asya mukha antare ekaḥ san eka deśa sthaḥ yadā ekena prayujyate tadā vaktṛ antare na syāt eka vaktṛ mukha ādi vat kāryatve syāt kriyā bhedāt phala bhedaḥ pratikriyam tena eka buddhiḥ sādṛśyāt sphuṭe anya tve avakalpate nitya tve tu ekabuddheḥ syāt na kiñ cit bhrānti kāraṇam kāmam deśāḥ iti nyāyāt tat ca eka tvam viruddhyate 
SV_6.15ab–6.18ab	 na ca vyañjaka bhedena deśa bheda upalambhanam pradīpaiḥ bhinna deśa sthaiḥ na bhinnaḥ vyajyate ghaṭaḥ vyomān avayavam ca eṣām dhvanīnām āśrayaḥ matam sa vyaṅgyānām atas sarvaiḥ vyaktiḥ ekatra te bhavet vastu antara vikārya tvāt smṛti sādṛśya sādhitāt ikāra ādeḥ anitya tvam dadhi kṣīra guḍa ādi vat hetu vṛddhi anusāri tvāt kārya tā asya ghaṭa ādi vat 
SV_6.18cd–6.21cd	 na hi dīpa sahasre api vyañjake varddhate ghaṭaḥ anaikāntika tā tāvat hetūnām iha kathyate prayatna anantarā dṛṣṭiḥ nitye api na viruddhyate tasmāt tatra eva dṛṣṭa tvāt anyatra adṛṣṭa kalpanā prāk ūrdhva anupalabdhaḥ ced dhetu tvena vivakṣite jāti aulūkyasya sāṃkhyasya caitanyena ātma vartinā śākyasya api tu anaikāntaḥ kṣaṇika vyatirekibhiḥ 
SV_6.22ab–6.25ab	 pratisaṃkhyā pratisaṃkhyā nirodhavyom abhiḥ tribhiḥ buddhi pūrvam vināśe hi pratisaṃkhyā nirodha dhīḥ abuddhi pūrvakaḥ teṣām nirodhaḥ apratisaṃkhyayā tau ca dvau api anāśi tvāt iṣṭa avakṛtakau api āhuḥ svabhāva siddham hi te vināśam ahetukam hetuḥ yasya vināśaḥ api tasya dṛṣṭaḥ aṅkura ādi vat vināśasya vināśaḥ tu na asti tasmāt akṛtrimaḥ 
SV_6.25cd–6.28cd	 bhavati hi agni sambandhāt kāṣṭāt aṅgāra santatiḥ mudgara ādi hatāt ca api kapālam jāyatte ghaṭāt svābhāvikaḥ vināśaḥ tu jāta mātra pratiṣṭitaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sadṛśa santāna dṛtteḥ anupalakṣitaḥ yadā vilakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ patet sadṛśa santatau vilakṣaṇena kāryeṇa sthūlaḥ abhivyajyate tadā tena asadṛśa santānaḥ hetoḥ san jāyate yatas 
SV_6.29ab–6.32ab	 tena eva akriyamāṇaḥ api nāśaḥ abhivyajyate sphūṭaḥ sa mudgara prahāra ādi prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ yasmāt akṛtakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hetuḥ syāt vyabhicāryataḥ ākāśam api nityam sat yadā bhūmi jala āvṛtam vyajyate tad apohena sva nana utsecana ādibhiḥ prayatna anantaram jñānam tadā tatra api dṛśyate tena anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ yat uktam tatra darśanāt 
SV_6.32cd–6.35cd	 atha sthagitam api etat asti eva iti anumīyate tirohita anabhivyakteḥ śabda buddhi prabandha vat śabdasya eva anavasthānāt iti hetum vadet yadi asthānāt iti ayam hetuḥ tadā anaikāntikaḥ bhavet ākāśa dhī prabandhaḥ hi tadā tasmin na tiṣṭati tirohita anabhivyakteḥ śabda buddhi prabandha vat śabdasya eva anavasthanāt iti hetum vadet yadi 
SV_6.36ab–6.39ab	 asiddhaḥ eva vaktavyaḥ tatas abhivyakti vādinā tad vyāpāra kṛta tve api vyaṅgyaiḥ mūla udaka ādibhiḥ kutaka tve apii teṣām hi na utpattiḥ khanana ādinā na ca āt cāraṇataḥ anyā asti śabdasya utpādikā kriyā nibandharyasatī iti evam viśiṣṭe api tathā eva naḥ abandhāḥ syuḥ yat iteṣām abodhaḥ hetu abhāvataḥ vyañjaka abhāvataḥ śabde api abodhaḥ badhira ādi vat 
SV_6.39cd–6.42cd	 tasya eva vā nibandhṛ tve bhavet dhetoḥ asiddha tā atha pūrva apara asattvam hituḥ tatra api asiddha tā san eva sādhāna abhāvāt śabdaḥ na eva upalabhyate kṣaṇikam sādhanam ca asya buddhiḥ api anuvartate megha andhakāra śarvaryā vidyut janita dṛṣṭi vat yathā ghaṭa ādeḥ dīpa ādiḥ abhivyañjakaḥ iṣyate cakṣuṣaḥ anugrahāt evam dhvaniḥ syāt śrītra saṃskṛteḥ 
SV_6.43ab–6.46ab	 na ca paryanuyogaḥ atra kena ākāreṇa saṃskṛtiḥ utpattau api tulya tvāt śaktiḥ tatra api atīndriyāḥ nityam kārya anumeyā ca śaktiḥ kim anuyujyate tad bhāva bhāvitā mātram pramāṇam tatra gamyate atas atīndriyayā evete śaktyā śaktim atīndriyām indriyasya ādadhānāḥ syuḥ śabda abhivyakti hetavaḥ vyañjakaḥ na anya jātiḥ ced śrotram śabdsya te katham 
SV_6.46cd–6.49cd	 pārthivānām ghaṭa ādīnām pradopādiḥ ca taijasaḥ ātma ādi samprayoge ca kāryaiḥ syāt tulya jātitā jātiḥ yā kā cit iṣṭā ced sā naḥ atra api bhaviṣyati upalabdhi nimittāt ca na anyat vyañjakam ucyate tasmāt yathā upalabdha tvāt sa jāti vyañjakaḥ bhavet tathā tad avinā abhāvāt vijātīyaḥ bhaviṣyati vāyavīya anabhijña tvāt tālu ādi stha abhimānataḥ 
SV_6.50ab–6.53ab	 anabhivyañjaka tva artham āha uparatayoḥ api vāyavīradhiyā eva uktam na nūnam iti ca uttaram abhighāta vacaḥ taḥ prāk evam gūḍha dhiyau= ubhau yadi śabdam iti iha api tredhā abhivyakti sambhavaḥ sā hi syāt śabda saṃskārāt indriyasya ubhayasya vā tatra sarvaiḥ pratīyeta śabdaḥ saṃskriyate yadi nirbhāgasya vibhoḥ na syāt eka deśe hi saṃskriyāḥ 
SV_6.53cd–6.56cd	 na ca asya ādhāra bhedena saṃskāra niyamaḥ bhavet yatas śabdaḥ nirādhāraḥ vyoma ātma ādi vat eva ca atha api ākāśam ādhāraḥ tatra anavayave asati na syāt pradeśa saṃskāraḥ kṛtsna śabda mateḥ api na hi sāmastya rūpeṇa yāvat vyoma vyavasthitaḥ śaktyate sakalaḥ boddhum eka deśena saṃskṛtaḥ ākāśa śrotra pakṣe ca vibhu tvāt prāpti tulya tā 
SV_6.57ab–6.60ab	 dūra bhāve api śabdānām iti jñānam prasajyate śrotrasya ca evam eka tvam sarva prāṇabhṛtām bhavet tena eka śruti velāyām śṛṇuyuḥ sarve eva te tasya anavayava tvāt ca na dharma adharma saṃskṛtaḥ nabhaḥ deśaḥ bhavet śrotram vyavasthā dvaya siddhayate vaiśeṣika ādi siddhānteṣu evam tāvat prasajyate kāpile api vibhu tvena śrotra ādeḥ iyam eva diś 
SV_6.60cd–6.63cd	 sakṛt ca saṃskṛtam śrotram sarva śabdān prabodhayet ghaṭāya unmīlitam cakṣuḥ paṭam na hi na budhyate etat eva prasaṅktavyam viṣayasya api saṃskṛtau samāna deśa varti tvāt saṃskāraḥ api aviśeṣatas sthira vāyu apanītyā ca saṃskāraḥ asya bhavan bhavet dṛṣṭam vā āvaraṇa apāye tad deśa anya upalambhanam saṃskṛta asaṃskṛta tve ca śabda eka tve na siddhi atas 
SV_6.64ab–6.67ab	 eka avasthā abhyupetaḥ vā sarvaiḥ jñāyeta vā na vā pratyeka abhihitāḥ doṣāḥ syuḥ dvayoḥ api saṃskṛtau tena prādeśikam jñānam na kṛta tvāt vinā bhavet uttaram śrotra saṃskārāt bhāṣya kāreṇa varṇitam tad bhedāt śruti bhedaḥ ca pratiśrotṛ vyavasthitaḥ na avaśyam śrotram ākāśam asmābhiḥ ca abhyupeyate na ca anavayavam vyoma jaina sāṃkhya niṣedhataḥ 
SV_6.67cd–6.70ab	 tena ākāśa eka deśaḥ vā yat vā vastu antaram bhavet kārya arthāpatti gamyam na ḥ śrotram pratinaram sthiram yadi api vyāpi ca ekam ca tathā api dhvani saṃskṛtiḥ adhiṣṭhāneṣu sā yasya tat śabdam pratipatsyate atha api indriya saṃskāraḥ saḥ api adhiṣṭhāna deśataḥ śabdam na śroṣyati śrotram tena asaṃskṛta śaṣkuli 
SV_6.70cd–6.73cd	 aprāpta karṇa deśa tvāt dhvaneḥ na śrotra saṃskriyāḥ atas adhiṣṭhāna bhedena saṃskāra niyama sthitiḥ nanu ekasmin adhiṣṭhāne labdha saṃskāram indriyam bodhakam sarva deheṣu syāt eka indriya vādinaḥ puṃsā deha pradeśeṣu vijñāna utpattiḥ iṣyate tena pradhāna vaideśyāt viguṇā sā tu saṃskṛtiḥ niṣpradeśaḥ api ca ātmā naḥ kārtsnyena ca vidan api 
SV_6.74ab–6.77ab	 śarīraḥ eva gṛhṇāti iti evam ukte na dṛṣyati eka tve api yathā ākāśam dravyaiḥ sa avayavaiḥ pṛthak saṃsarga bhedam labhate saṃskāra asaṃskṛtaḥ tathā vyomnaḥ anavayava vyāpti sadbhāve api bhuviṣthitān dvi āśraya tvam na saṃsargaḥ ghaṭa ādīn anurudhyate bādhirya ādi vyavasthānam anena eva ca hetunā tat eva abhogyam anyasya dharma adharma vaśīkṛtam 
SV_6.77cd–6.80cd	 yathā tatra vasan eva svāmi tvāt avaropitaḥ na bhogam labhate tadvat badhiraḥ anyatra śṛṇvati śrotra śabda āśrayāṇām ca na nāma avayavāḥ svayam na ca eka deśa vṛtti tvam tathā api etat na duṣyati vyañjakānām hi vāyūnām bhinna avayava deśa tā jāti bhedaḥ ca tena eva saṃskāraḥ vyavatiṣṭhate anya artham preritaḥ vāyuḥ yathā anyam na karotivaḥ
